
-----title
南京（江宁）
-----detail

class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42730?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和王明府见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（960年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42730")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42730_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42730'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42730'>时情世难消吾道，薄宦流年厄此身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42730'>莫叹京华同寂寞，曾经兵革共漂沦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42730'>对山开户唯求静，贳酒留宾不道贫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42730'>善政空多尚淹屈，不知谁是解忧民。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42730_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42730'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42730_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>春，在江宁府为太子右谕德，复知制诰。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>春，在江宁府为知制诰，有诗与人唱和。作品：再领制诰和王明府见贺。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_42694' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42694' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42694'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42694'>蹇步还依列宿边，拱辰重认旧云天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42694'>自嗟多难飘零困，不似当年胆气全。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42694'>鸡树晚花疏向日，龙池轻浪细含烟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42694'>从来不解为身计，一叶悠悠任大川。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42694'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42694_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>本年，在江宁府为知制诰，迁中书舍人，通署中书省事。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7d3bea825303408c91df22ba6bc11fb0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7d3bea825303408c91df22ba6bc11fb0");'><span id='7d3bea825303408c91df22ba6bc11fb0_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=960&endYear=960')">960年</a>　约于本年，在江宁府为中书舍人，有诗送高越使南汉。作品：送高舍人使岭南。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_42947' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42947' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42947?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送高舍人使岭南</a><span class='authorDate'>（960年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42947")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_42947_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_42947'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3542, "poem_allusion_42947")'>终童</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_42947_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42947'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42947'>西掖官曹近，南溟道路遥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42947'>使星将渡汉，仙棹乍乘潮。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42947'>柳映<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作䀹）</span>灵和折，梅依大庾飘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42947'>江帆风淅淅，山馆雨萧萧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42947'>陆贾真迂阔，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3542, "poem_sentence_4_42947")'>终童</span>久寂寥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_42947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_42947'>送君何限意，把酒一长谣。<div id='poem_sentence_5_42947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_42947'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_42947_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='0d72201dae9244f3a41615d0ad62caf0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0d72201dae9244f3a41615d0ad62caf0");'><span id='0d72201dae9244f3a41615d0ad62caf0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年</a>，46岁</div><div id='0d72201dae9244f3a41615d0ad62caf0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年7月</a>　七月，在江宁府为中书舍人，李煜嗣位，迁礼部侍郎，仍为中书舍人，通署中书省事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年7月</a>　七月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，作严续迁官制。作品：右揆严续除司空兼门下侍郎平章事制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_1145793' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145793' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145793?labeling=true' target='_blank'>右揆严续除司空兼门下侍郎平章事制</a><span class='authorDate'>（961年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145793")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145793_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145793'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145793'>门下：天作司牧，必生丞弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145793_comment'></div>非君臣同体，道则不明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145793_comment'></div>非律吕交感，功则不济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145793_comment'></div>粤予眇质，负荷景灵，不有时贤，岂戡多难？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145793_comment'></div>敬若先意，畴兹旧臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145793_comment'></div>某纯粹炳灵，惠和成性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145793_comment'></div>袭台鼎之庆，连肺腑之亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145793_comment'></div>历奉累朝，亟更庶尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145793_comment'></div>忧国家之事，知无不为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145793_comment'></div>经夷险之间，中立不倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145793_comment'></div>言必由于忠信，行必自于诚明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145793_comment'></div>劳而弗矜，谦以自牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145793_comment'></div>先朝鉴其诚志，任以腹心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145793_comment'></div>顷当巡守之初，俾贰主留之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145793_comment'></div>尽规竭虑，夜思昼行，京辅以宁，时乃之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145793_comment'></div>及奉扬末命，以佑冲人，送往事居，礼无违者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145793_comment'></div>忠勋茂绩，人无间然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145793_comment'></div>今二后在天，万物思理，予方乃眷，民亦具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145793_comment'></div>是用命作司空，倚为左相，兼国史枢机之任，进升阶食赋之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145793_comment'></div>岂曰宠章，是同忧责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145793_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145793_comment'></div>受遗作弼，厥惟艰哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145793_comment'></div>尔其崇远大之谟，布简宽之政，询箴谏之士，塞便佞之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145793_comment'></div>满假自贤，则其智益蔽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145793_comment'></div>虚怀接物，则其猷益光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145793_comment'></div>念兹在兹，以底于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145793_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1145793_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年7月</a>　七月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，代百官上表奏请行圣尊后册礼。作品：百官奏请行圣尊后册礼表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二〇。）</span><div id='poem_1145873' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145873' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145873?labeling=true' target='_blank'>百官奏请行圣尊后册礼表</a><span class='authorDate'>（961年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145873")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145873_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145873'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145873'>文武百官臣某等言：伏奉制旨，以圣尊后册礼奉令旨俟百日后上进者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145873_comment'></div>仰承严命，固合遵行，但以事有未安，理须陈奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145873_comment'></div>伏以历代已来，嗣极之主，礼之大者，尊奉上宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145873_comment'></div>傥或止仪未行，庶事莫敢先举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145873_comment'></div>所以陛下裁膺册礼，即下制书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145873_comment'></div>长乐归尊，已先孝理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145873_comment'></div>百司承式，将撰吉辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145873_comment'></div>及金辂言还，六宫即叙，惟忧典礼，已属稽迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145873_comment'></div>遽睹丝言，备听慈旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145873_comment'></div>在苴麻之次，诚极感伤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145873_comment'></div>然凶吉之仪，本无妨碍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145873_comment'></div>历观前载，遍考儒臣，法度具存，事体至大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145873_comment'></div>况涣汗之泽，普及诸侯，简册之行，便当相次，未修大礼，交慊群情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145873_comment'></div>伏乞陛下再禀严慈，俯回听允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145873_comment'></div>臣等幸尘有位，庶免旷官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145873_comment'></div>冒渎冕旒，无任云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1145873_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年10月</a>　十月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，为徐景运别墅园林作碑记。作品：毗陵郡公南原亭馆记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_1145947' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145947' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145947?labeling=true' target='_blank'>毗陵郡公南原亭馆记</a><span class='authorDate'>（961年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145947")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145947_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145947'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145947'>人生而静，性之适也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145947_comment'></div>若乃庙堂之贵，轩冕之盛，君子所以劳心济物，屈己存教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145947_comment'></div>功成事遂，复归于静，用能周旋于道，常久而不已者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145947_comment'></div>有唐再造，俗厚政和，人多暇豫，物亦茂遂，名园胜概，隐辚相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145947_comment'></div>至于东田之馆，西州之墅，娄湖张侯之宅，东山谢公之游，青溪赋诗之曲，白杨饮酒之路，风流人物，高视昔贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145947_comment'></div>京城坤隅，爰有别馆，百亩之地，芳华一新，旧相毗陵公习静之所也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145947_comment'></div>其地却据峻岭，俯瞰长江，北弥临沧之观，南摭新林之戍，足以穷幽极览，忘形放怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145947_comment'></div>于是建高望之亭，肆游目之观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145947_comment'></div>睨多鸟于云外，认归帆于天末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145947_comment'></div>四山隐见而屏列，重城逦迤而霞舒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145947_comment'></div>纷徒步而右回，辟精庐于中岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145947_comment'></div>倚层崖而筑室，就积石以为阶，土事不文，木工不斲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145947_comment'></div>虚牖夕映，密户冬燠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145947_comment'></div>素屏麈尾，榧几黎床，谈玄之侣，此焉游息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145947_comment'></div>设射堂于其左，湛方塘于其下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145947_comment'></div>虚楹显敞，清风爽气袭其间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145947_comment'></div>椅岸萦回，红蕖翠荇藻其涘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145947_comment'></div>至于芳草嘉禾，修竹茂林，纷敷翳蔚，不可殚记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145947_comment'></div>凡厩库之室，厨廪之区，宾燕所资，不戒而具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145947_comment'></div>每良辰美景，欣然命驾，众从子弟，结驷相追，角巾藜杖，优游笑咏，观之者不知其为公相也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145947_comment'></div>古人有言：朝廷之士，入而不能出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145947_comment'></div>况于轻钟鼎之贵，徇山林之心，将相之权不能累其真，肺腑之亲不能系其遁，道风素范，岂不美欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145947_comment'></div>又以铉无事事之情，有善善之志，见徵拙笔，用勒贞珉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145947_comment'></div>是时岁次辛酉冬十月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1145947_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年11月</a>　十一月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，奉命出使南汉。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d3eb0dbc9c3e45aaa5f9a67ce1a0197b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d3eb0dbc9c3e45aaa5f9a67ce1a0197b");'><span id='d3eb0dbc9c3e45aaa5f9a67ce1a0197b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年</a>，46岁</div><div id='d3eb0dbc9c3e45aaa5f9a67ce1a0197b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年</a>　约于本年，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，与殷崇义有诗歌唱和。作品：和门下殷侍郎新茶二十韵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_42970' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42970' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42970?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和门下殷侍郎新茶二十韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（961年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42970")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_42970_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42970'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42970'>暖吹入春园，新芽竞粲然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42970'>才教鹰觜拆，未放<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_42970", 42970, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>雪花</span>妍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42970'>荷杖青林下，携筐旭景前<span class='inlineComment2'>（采茶须在日未出前）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42970'>孕灵资雨露，钟秀自山川。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42970'>碾后香弥远，烹来色更鲜。<div id='poem_sentence_4_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_42970'>名随土地贵，味逐水泉迁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_42970'>力藉流黄暖，形模紫笋圆<span class='inlineComment2'>（茶之美者有圆捲紫笋）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_42970'>正当钻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_42970", 42970, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>柳火</span>，遥想涌金泉<span class='inlineComment2'>（阳羡茶山有金涉泉，修贡时出）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_42970'>任道时新物，须依古法煎。<div id='poem_sentence_8_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_42970'>轻瓯浮绿乳，孤灶散馀烟。<div id='poem_sentence_9_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_42970'>甘荠非予匹，宫槐让我先<span class='inlineComment2'>（槐芽亦可为茶）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_42970'>竹孤空冉冉，荷弱谩田田。<div id='poem_sentence_11_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_42970'>解渴消残酒，清神感夜眠。<div id='poem_sentence_12_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_42970'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_42970", 42970, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>十浆</span>何足馈，百榼尽堪捐。<div id='poem_sentence_13_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_42970'>采撷唯忧晚，营求不计钱。<div id='poem_sentence_14_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_42970'>任公因焙显，陆氏有经传。<div id='poem_sentence_15_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_42970'>爱甚真成癖，尝多合得仙。<div id='poem_sentence_16_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_42970'>亭台虚静处，风月艳阳天。<div id='poem_sentence_17_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_42970'>自可临泉石，何妨杂管弦。<div id='poem_sentence_18_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_42970'>东山似蒙顶，愿得从诸贤。<div id='poem_sentence_19_42970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_42970'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_42970_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d53be462a0b641808b514abc375e4bff_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d53be462a0b641808b514abc375e4bff");'><span id='d53be462a0b641808b514abc375e4bff_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=963&endYear=975')">963-975年</a>，48-60岁</div><div id='d53be462a0b641808b514abc375e4bff' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=963&endYear=963')">963年</a>　本年，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，评大周后所作《霓裳羽衣曲》声太急。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=963&endYear=963')">963年</a>　约于本年秋，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，有诗与陈德成唱和。作品：和歙州陈使君见寄。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_42941' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42941' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42941?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和歙州陈使君见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（963年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42941")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_42941_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42941'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42941'>新安风景好，时令肃辕门。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42941'>身贵心弥下，功多口不言。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42941'>韬钤家法在，儒雅素风存。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42941'>簪履陪游盛，乡闾俗化敦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42941'>临窗山色秀，绕郭水声喧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_42941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_42941'>纤络文章丽，矜严道义尊。<div id='poem_sentence_5_42941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_42941'>楼台秋月静，京庾晚云屯。<div id='poem_sentence_6_42941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_42941'>晓吹传衙鼓，晴阳展信幡。<div id='poem_sentence_7_42941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_42941'>一篇贻友好，千里倍心论。<div id='poem_sentence_8_42941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_42941'>未见归骖动，空能役梦魂。<div id='poem_sentence_9_42941_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_42941'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_42941_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=964&endYear=964')">964年3月</a>　三月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，奉命覆试进士舒雅、冯僎等五人，雅等不就。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=964&endYear=964')">964年10月</a>　十月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，奉诏为李仲宣作墓志。作品：岐王墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一七。）</span><div id='poem_1146002' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146002' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146002?labeling=true' target='_blank'>岐王墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（964年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146002")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146002_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146002'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146002'>天地之灵气，发为贤人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146002_comment'></div>邦家之积庆，钟于公族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146002_comment'></div>其或富老成之智，促殇子之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146002_comment'></div>感群情者自出于天资，垂英声者非由于事业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146002_comment'></div>是以苍舒轸悼于魏祖，表行曰哀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146002_comment'></div>夏王钟爱于明皇，锡名为一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146002_comment'></div>中兴在运，代有人杰，见于岐王矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146002_comment'></div>王讳仲宣，今上之第二子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146002_comment'></div>文武储庆，日月输祥，实太姒之子，如鲁桓之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146002_comment'></div>天质秀发，神机内融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146002_comment'></div>亦既免怀，未遑就傅，问安长乐，视膳寝门，承欢爱于瑶斋，极友悌于朱邸，成人之量，宛由生知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146002_comment'></div>三岁受封为宣城郡公，假大司马之秩，维城之望，日以光矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146002_comment'></div>不幸遘疾，甲子岁冬十月二日，薨于阁内，年四岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146002_comment'></div>主上痛幼敏之异，极天慈之怀，诏辍朝七日，册赠司徒，追封岐王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146002_comment'></div>既而，感上圣之忘情，遵先王之从俭，节哀简礼，以厚古风，即以其月十有八日备卤簿鼓吹，葬于江宁府某县某里之原，有司谥曰怀献，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146002_comment'></div>惟王以襁褓之年，蕴金玉之度，异迹昭灼，可得而言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146002_comment'></div>至如禁中娱侍，常在左右，或异宫一日，则思恋通宵，翌旦未明，必亲至御幄，须奉颜色，然后即安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146002_comment'></div>其孝也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146002_comment'></div>上每罢朝稍晏，庄色未回，王则俨然侍立，不妄言笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146002_comment'></div>须天颜悦怿，则趋就膝下，怡怡稚戏，不失其仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146002_comment'></div>中宫以上之钟爱，恐渐于骄，故抚字之方，威克于爱，每加教诲，过于严厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146002_comment'></div>而王凛然祗畏，初不坏容，退或见上，乃啼以自悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146002_comment'></div>其敬也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146002_comment'></div>始二岁，上亲授以《孝经》、《杂言》，虽未尽识其字，而每至发端止句之处，皆默记不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146002_comment'></div>至于寝疾，近数千言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146002_comment'></div>时听奏乐，必振袂击节，咸中律度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146002_comment'></div>工人试中变其曲，王辍止之，曰：「非前曲也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146002_comment'></div>虽周郎之顾，何以加焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146002_comment'></div>其惠也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146002_comment'></div>受封之日，见于内殿，音词宣朗，容止闲习，观之者咸叹重焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146002_comment'></div>其敏也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1146002_comment'></div>凡玩好之物，意有欲者，瞬目赏誉，未尝求索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1146002_comment'></div>或识其意，持以与之，必再三推却，不肯即受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1146002_comment'></div>其毅也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1146002_comment'></div>上曰：「昔人谓王绩为神仙童子，今此儿近是乎」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1146002_comment'></div>及其薨也，悼念之甚，曰：「吾见他人贤子弟犹惜之，岂惟父子之性乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1146002_comment'></div>中宫哀恸，至于加疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1146002_comment'></div>自非英姿感动，孰能臻此哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1146002_comment'></div>议者以为列宿沦精，高真降迹，表瑞王室，今复还矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1146002_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1146002_comment'></div>凡我臣庶，暨乎藩戚，瞻飞盖之何期，慨神理之难测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1146002_comment'></div>宁尽美于称赞，庶腾芳于简册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1146002_comment'></div>词臣奉诏，谨勒贞石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1146002_comment'></div>其铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1146002'>粤我仙源，流光庆延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1146002_comment'></div>公族之异，惟王生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1146002_comment'></div>礼诗仁孝，斯之谓贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1146002_comment'></div>夙习非学，生知自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1146002_comment'></div>既与之智，胡夺之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1146002_comment'></div>瞻庭兰刈，顾掌珠捐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1146002_comment'></div>孟冬寒气，京兆新阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1146002_comment'></div>鼓吹箫箫，旌旐翩翩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1146002_comment'></div>踠逸躅于稚齿，閟藩房于夜泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1146002_comment'></div>已焉哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1146002_comment'></div>庶彭殇之一梦，岂没世之无传？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1146002_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_1146002'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1146002_comment'></div>庭兰伊何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1146002_comment'></div>方春而○。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1146002_comment'></div>掌珠伊何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1146002_comment'></div>在玩而倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1146002_comment'></div>珠沉媚泽，兰陨芳馨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1146002_comment'></div>人犹沮恨，我若为情！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1146002_comment'></div>萧萧极野，寂寂重扃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1146002_comment'></div>与子长诀，挥涕吞声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1146002_comment'></div>噫嘻哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1146002_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_64_1146002'>又铭一首，至尊所作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1146002_comment'></div>上省「庭兰」、「掌珠」之句，谓得比兴之实，遂广其意，发为斯文，亲迂宸翰，批于纸尾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1146002_comment'></div>足以厚君亲之义，行孝慈之风，是用勒石，永光泉户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1146002_comment'></div>谨记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_67_1146002_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=964&endYear=964')">964年11月</a>　十一月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，大周后殂，上谥号曰“昭惠”作品：昭惠后谥议。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1145880' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145880' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145880?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭惠后谥议</a><span class='authorDate'>（964年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145880")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145880_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145880'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145880'>臣闻广莫极于坤元，则含容光大，拟议著焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145880_comment'></div>尊莫隆于王后，则窈窕思贤，咏歌发焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145880_comment'></div>是以上德无名，而称谓流于百代；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145880_comment'></div>至道无象，而仪形表于万方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145880_comment'></div>此固天理，出于自然，圣人所以无避者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145880_comment'></div>矧惟节惠之礼，百王盛典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145880_comment'></div>述德之议，史臣至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145880_comment'></div>诞昭耿光，敢扬懿德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145880_comment'></div>伏惟大行国后，生商遗烈，安刘积庆，淑质奇相，惠问英才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145880_comment'></div>光映台华，作俪公族，绍隆藩阃，载辑储闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145880_comment'></div>世子专寝门之礼，孝心不匮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145880_comment'></div>大君以家人之庆，天覆有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145880_comment'></div>诚由肃雍之德，叶此睦姻之盛，言内则者以为美谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145880_comment'></div>及属运飞天，尊归配地，严恭匪懈，禀母仪于上宫，慈惠积中，率妇道于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145880_comment'></div>浣濯是服，而六衣有炜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145880_comment'></div>环佩中节，而九御有伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145880_comment'></div>思脱簪之诫，以成忧勤之政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145880_comment'></div>躬大练之饰，以辅纯俭之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145880_comment'></div>阴教既孚，王化茂远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145880_comment'></div>方舆告变，椒风永閟，恸结长乐，哀缠紫宸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145880_comment'></div>龟筮叶从，攒涂将启，旌德之号，彤管斯存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145880_comment'></div>若乃山河表德，而文之以礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145880_comment'></div>金玉其相，而守之以恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145880_comment'></div>垂训以慈，进贤以哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145880_comment'></div>至于诵经习诗之敏，审音知乐之明，超然远识，夐绝终古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145880_comment'></div>勤行孝养，下自从化，故宽裕怀于六宫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145880_comment'></div>天资明惠，学无不通，故遗爱钟于宸眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145880_comment'></div>载稽具美，实光前烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145880_comment'></div>谨案《谥法》，「德礼不愆」、「容仪恭美」皆曰「昭」，「慈哲远识」、「宽裕遗爱」皆曰「惠」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145880_comment'></div>仰惟实录，足表鸿猷，谥曰昭惠后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145880_comment'></div>谨议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1145880_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=964&endYear=964')">964年</a>　约于本年，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，为重修徐孺亭作碑记。作品：重修徐孺亭记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_1145945' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145945' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145945?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重修徐孺亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（964年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145945")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145945_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145945'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145945'>至矣哉，天之爱民甚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145945_comment'></div>虽数有治乱，而常生圣贤，故得其位则功加于时，舛其运则教垂于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145945_comment'></div>虽销声灭迹，全身远害，不德而德普，逃名而名扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145945_comment'></div>拥彗筑宫，礼重于列国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145945_comment'></div>式闾表墓，道光于无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145945_comment'></div>举善而教，政之大者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145945_comment'></div>恭惟我祖，炳灵南国，旧宅界乎仙馆，高台峙乎澄陂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145945_comment'></div>孺亭之称，海内瞻仰，名公良牧，代加崇饰，千载之下，犹旦暮焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145945_comment'></div>顷属邦君非才，败我王度，剪焉层构，鞠为茂草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145945_comment'></div>噫，百世之祀，谁能废之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145945_comment'></div>庚申岁始建王都，辛酉岁遂迂清跸，肆觐群后，畴咨先贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145945_comment'></div>馀基未倾，伟人将至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145945_comment'></div>既而鼎湖在御，桐圭锡壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145945_comment'></div>丞相司空邓王以茂亲之重，膺分陕之权，思老成之典型，仰高山之景行，罔言而信，不肃而严，乃命经营，将从缔构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145945_comment'></div>九成方起，百堵未周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145945_comment'></div>甲子岁，入秉国钧，以武昌连帅、侍中济南公代司宫籥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145945_comment'></div>公致用以武，从政以文，祗奉萧规，率由周礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145945_comment'></div>再赓成制，详考旧基，夷坎窞而就平，裨崖岸而增固，乃崇堂奥，乃加藻缋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145945_comment'></div>右严樽坫之序，左设庖膳之区，前临康庄，旁眺城阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145945_comment'></div>平湖千亩，凝碧于其下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145945_comment'></div>西山万叠，倒影于其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145945_comment'></div>依然悬榻之场，想见致刍之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145945_comment'></div>与夫洪崖之馆，绚彩于烟霞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145945_comment'></div>滕王之阁，骞飞于雉堞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145945_comment'></div>南州之物象备矣，前哲之光灵萃焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145945_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145945_comment'></div>君子兴一役，建一事，于时必可颂，于后必可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145945_comment'></div>兹亭之作也，都人朋悦，过宾瞩目，纪于方国之史，播于《乐职》之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145945_comment'></div>铉也幸成燕翼之谋，获参翰墨之任，俾垂不朽，敢惮芜音！</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1145945_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=964&endYear=964')">964年</a>　约于本年九月二十七日，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，作赠序送人。作品：送刘生序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1145894' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145894' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145894?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送刘生序</a><span class='authorDate'>（964年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145894")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145894_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145894'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145894'>彭城刘生为南畿令，天官侍郎昌黎公作序以送，盛称故历阳宰杨员外光儒之为政以勖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145894_comment'></div>铉与杨君有姻，深知其内行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145894_comment'></div>君清简仁爱，心无适莫，自妻子仆妾及家族吏民，接之无亲疏之隔，求之于形骸之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145894_comment'></div>盖真纯之气充，而感召之应远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145894_comment'></div>民之好竞者皆相与言曰：「众若嚚讼，必挠吾员外矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145894_comment'></div>呜呼，其古人乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145894_comment'></div>今刘生才俊于杨，学优于杨，观其政绩等，然生犹有耿介不平之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145894_comment'></div>观吏部之勖子，与予之赠言，盖为是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145894_comment'></div>子其平心藏用，㳷然与道合，在古人上矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145894_comment'></div>矧西山神仙之宅也，旌阳其远乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145894_comment'></div>仆固倦谈，生停骖已久，故扬榷以论之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145894_comment'></div>九月二十七日，中书舍人徐铉序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1145894_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=965&endYear=965')">965年9月</a>　九月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，李煜母钟氏殂，为作谥册。作品：光穆后谥册。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1145862' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145862' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145862?labeling=true' target='_blank'>光穆后谥册</a><span class='authorDate'>（965年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145862")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145862_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145862'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145862'>维年月日，嗣国主臣某再拜稽首言：臣闻体厚德而母万物，存乎尊位；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145862_comment'></div>腾耿光而蕃百世，系乎鸿名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145862_comment'></div>继统广业，莫斯为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145862_comment'></div>顾惟小子，惧忝贻谋，对越祖宗，敢扬公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145862_comment'></div>伏惟大行圣尊后，姜、任显族，皇、英茂德，作合元圣，长发祥符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145862_comment'></div>秉妇礼于储闱，正嫔则于四海，孝心天赋，惠问川流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145862_comment'></div>祚启重熙，尊归理内，率循阴教，钦若皇猷，顺承利坤元之贞，辅佐流《周南》之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145862_comment'></div>慈抚公族，仁怀六宫，清净广于真风，戒慎刑于外戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145862_comment'></div>用能永锡繁祉，弘济多难，保佑冲人，克荷丕构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145862_comment'></div>仰繄慈训，方恢景福，灵台告祲，永乐长违，罔极之怀，触绪荒殒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145862_comment'></div>恭惟尊名节惠之典，载考儒臣礼官之称，咸以为光大孝悌之懿，肃雍贤德之盛，昭映前烈，垂示无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145862_comment'></div>列辟承式，弗敢失坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145862_comment'></div>谨奉玉册琮宝，上尊谥曰光穆皇后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145862_comment'></div>伏惟威灵如在，鉴兹缛礼，延九庙之积庆，与二仪而长存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145862_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145862_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1145862_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=965&endYear=965')">965年</a>　冬，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，有诗挽光穆皇后。作品：光穆皇后挽歌三首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_42691' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42691' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42691?labeling=true' target='_blank'>光穆皇后挽歌三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（965年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42691")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42691_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42691'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42691'>仙驭期难改，坤仪道自光。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42691'>閟宫新表德，沙麓旧膺祥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42691'>素帟尧门掩，凝笳毕陌长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42691'>东风惨陵树，无复见亲桑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42691'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42691_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_42692' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42692' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42692?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（965年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42692_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42692'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42692'>永乐留虚位，长陵启夕扉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42692'>返虞严吉仗，复土掩空衣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42692'>功业投三母，光灵极四妃。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42692'>唯应彤史在，不与露花晞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42692'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42692_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_42693' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42693' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42693?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（965年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42693_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42693'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42693'>隐隐阊门路，烟云晓更愁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42693'>空瞻金辂出，非是濯龙游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42693'>德感人伦正，风行内职修。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42693'>还随偶物化，同此畏轩丘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42693'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42693_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=965&endYear=965')">965年</a>　约于本年，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，有诗咏严续宅牡丹。作品：严相公宅牡丹。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_42703' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42703' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42703?labeling=true' target='_blank'>严相公宅牡丹</a><span class='authorDate'>（965年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42703")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42703_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42703'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42703'>但是豪家重牡丹，争如丞相阁前看。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42703'>凤楼日暖开偏早，鸡树阴浓谢更难。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42703'>数朵已应迷国艳，一枝何幸上尘冠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42703'>不知更许凭栏否，烂熳春光未肯残。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42703'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42703_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=966&endYear=966')">966年1月</a>　正月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，为方讷作墓志。作品：唐故河南方公墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一五。）</span><div id='poem_1145990' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145990' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145990?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故金紫光禄大夫检校司徒行少府监河南方公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（966年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145990")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145990_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145990'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145990'>公讳讷，字希仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145990_comment'></div>其先河南人也，后世从官，徙籍新安，支派繁衍，遂为郡之著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145990_comment'></div>迨公数世，皆以儒雅退让，播为门风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145990_comment'></div>曾祖颙，登州文登县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145990_comment'></div>祖亮，左武卫兵曹参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145990_comment'></div>考縠，荣王府司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145990_comment'></div>母聂氏，追封河南县太君，问政先生师道之长女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145990_comment'></div>公承积善之庆，负夙成之智，砥节励行，好学能文，时然后言，非礼勿动，乡曲之党，翕然称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145990_comment'></div>太师陶公，来守新安，抚纳人士，署为郡吏，委以典签，恪恭详敏，甚称所职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145990_comment'></div>历事累政，其志如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145990_comment'></div>烈祖肇基王业，元宗实综军政，管记之任，勤择其人，闻公之名，召致幕府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145990_comment'></div>王国初建，署宁国军节度馆驿巡官，掌都统表奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145990_comment'></div>皇室再造，庆赏遂行，擢拜虞部员外郎，掌元帅表奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145990_comment'></div>数岁，以皇孙就傅，命公侍读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145990_comment'></div>讲道赞德，励裨益之诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145990_comment'></div>端己直躬，尽表微之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145990_comment'></div>俄迁水部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145990_comment'></div>明年，皇孙封南昌王、东都留守，以公为留守判官，迁主客郎中，参赞政务，事无违者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145990_comment'></div>改司农少卿，依前充职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145990_comment'></div>明年，王移任宣、润二州大都督，复以公为浙西营田副使，通判军府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145990_comment'></div>六载匪懈，庶职交修，懋官之赏，诏命叠委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145990_comment'></div>累迁至金紫光禄大夫、检校司徒，封河南县男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145990_comment'></div>俄拜泰州刺史，充本州屯田监院使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145990_comment'></div>正身而令，悉心为理，公无遗利，民自从风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145990_comment'></div>属强敌深侵，东京失守，而州兵尽出，人心大摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145990_comment'></div>于是士庶老幼，尽室南渡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145990_comment'></div>公自归阙下，坐是除名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145990_comment'></div>数年，除歙州团练判官，上曰：「战争之际，吾岂以武勇责书生哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145990_comment'></div>军法不得不尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145990_comment'></div>即召拜太子右谕德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145990_comment'></div>今上嗣位，迁少府监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1145990_comment'></div>丙寅岁正月十六日，卒于京师美仁坊官舍，享年七十七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1145990_comment'></div>上为之废朝一日，赐谥曰定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1145990_comment'></div>以其年某月日葬于某所，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1145990_comment'></div>前夫人谢氏早亡，继室施氏封沛县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1145990_comment'></div>长子前，宣州宁国县主簿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1145990_comment'></div>次子志，饶州文学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1145990_comment'></div>公以名教为乐，以矩矱自任，行必中立，居无惰容，搢绅之间，推为纯行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1145990_comment'></div>公之外祖，得道之士，故公颇以朝礼修养为务，鸡鸣而起，孜孜不倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1145990_comment'></div>年俯悼耄，体常康强，及属纩之晨，无伏枕之疾，斯亦力行之报也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1145990_comment'></div>铉也不佞，早辱交契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1145990_comment'></div>昔先君从事黟、歙，公适仕本部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1145990_comment'></div>及公策名郎署，铉亦忝官联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1145990_comment'></div>既熟其素履，愿垂于不朽，附于史氏，以永令猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1145990_comment'></div>其铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1145990'>圣人四教：文行忠信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1145990_comment'></div>惟公似之，光有令问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1145990_comment'></div>秉笔赞画，登朝典郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1145990_comment'></div>宠至若惊，道丧无闷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1145990_comment'></div>年俯中寿，官参列卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1145990_comment'></div>归全委顺，终吉永贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1145990_comment'></div>宰树长在，高台自倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1145990_comment'></div>用刊圆石，閟此佳城。</div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1145990_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=966&endYear=966')">966年6月</a>　六月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，为刘鄗作墓志。作品：唐故常州团练判官检校尚书左仆射刘君墓志。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一六。）</span><div id='poem_1145999' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145999' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145999?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故常州团练判官检校尚书左仆射刘君墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（966年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145999")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145999_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145999'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145999'>夫资忠全孝，含贞履洁，君子所以没身而守之，圣人所以屈己而申之，其道可传，其风可仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145999_comment'></div>呜呼，刘君其殆庶乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145999_comment'></div>君讳鄗，字巨源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145999_comment'></div>其先彭城人，徙居广陵重世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145999_comment'></div>曾祖永，澧州司户参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145999_comment'></div>祖审，不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145999_comment'></div>考瑰，检校户部尚书，赠右仆射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145999_comment'></div>君生而岐嶷，有异常童。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145999_comment'></div>五岁而孤，即禀至性；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145999_comment'></div>年在幼学，卓然老成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145999_comment'></div>初，先君事吴，实干近职，而太夫人王氏与贞穆皇后复有姻旧，故宣帝命君使事丹阳公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145999_comment'></div>府公龙飞，以君为殿前承旨，便蕃左右，靖恭夙夜，动必称职，人无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145999_comment'></div>二十年间，累迁检校礼部尚书，充崇贤殿使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145999_comment'></div>及转俯代谢，众或将迎，君侃然正色，有死无二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145999_comment'></div>游说之词不能入，权利之势不能动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145999_comment'></div>于是阉竖希旨，以飞语中之，坐除名流池阳郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145999_comment'></div>明年，有唐受禅，烈祖嘉君尽忠，亟召之还，除常州长史，悉还其官阶田宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145999_comment'></div>未几，又改和州长史，听归广陵旧居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145999_comment'></div>初，元宗方在胶庠，吴帝使君召拜郎中，赐以章绶，自尔至于为相，每朝谒必先见君而后入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145999_comment'></div>及元宗即位，召至京师，复命太夫人入禁中，如贞穆之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145999_comment'></div>谓曰：「吾受吴朝恩礼，不敢忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145999_comment'></div>今犹数梦让皇帝，执臣子之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145999_comment'></div>吾观当时近臣，唯夫人长为长者，帝意亲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145999_comment'></div>今复得在吾左右，良足慰也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145999_comment'></div>君闻之，遂称足疾，不任趋拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145999_comment'></div>上仍赐第以居之，岁时锡赉甚厚，时使亲近谕旨，竟不能移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145999_comment'></div>上乃加太夫人封邑，召君受命于朝，固辞以疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145999_comment'></div>上叹息曰：「此子至孝，今以其母故，召之不来，是必然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145999_comment'></div>此亦古人所难，吾何为夺其节耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145999_comment'></div>久之，以君为常州团练判官，不使之任，优其禄而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145999_comment'></div>今上嗣位，加检校右仆射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1145999_comment'></div>君家承钟鼎之富，少居绮纨之职，时逢革故，年甫壮室，而遂闭门却扫，高谢人间，孜孜色养，怡怡自得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1145999_comment'></div>姻族以之肃穆，士友以之景仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1145999_comment'></div>名节终始，清风邈然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1145999_comment'></div>丙寅岁夏六月某日，终于建安某坊之私第，春秋五十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1145999_comment'></div>初，君葬太夫人于茅山良常洞之西，因自卜茔地，即以其年月日葬焉，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1145999_comment'></div>前夫人张氏早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1145999_comment'></div>今夫人吴氏，实有莱妻之贤，能从伯鸾之操，天资玉映，令问薰兰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1145999_comment'></div>子昭嗣、女某等，善庆所钟，家声不陨，爱敬哀戚，在礼无违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1145999_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1145999_comment'></div>令人其必有后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1145999_comment'></div>铉家世通旧，复连懿亲，常以君抗节遗世，既近代之孤标，而元宗推诚耸善，又列辟之难事，足以激扬薄俗，垂示将来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1145999_comment'></div>乃为铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_1145999'>忠于事君，孝于养亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1145999_comment'></div>逢时有道，以义卫身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1145999_comment'></div>隐不绝俗，居能保真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1145999_comment'></div>我永终吉，谁为古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1145999_comment'></div>地胏之原，小茅之麓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1145999_comment'></div>左盼松冈，前瞻柳谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1145999_comment'></div>栾棘新吹，松楸再卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1145999_comment'></div>令问昭显，流光似续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1145999_comment'></div>刻此苕华，永芳兰菊。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1145999_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=966&endYear=966')">966年</a>　本年，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，与江直木日会饮酒，相与赋诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=966&endYear=966')">966年</a>　约于本年，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，知贡举，取吴淑，以女妻之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=967&endYear=967')">967年10月</a>　十月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，为周廷构作墓志。作品：唐故筠州刺史周君墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一五。）</span><div id='poem_1145991' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145991' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145991?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故客省使寿昌殿承宣金紫光禄大夫检校太保使持节筠州诸军事筠州刺史本州团练使汝南县开国男周君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（967年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145991")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145991_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145991'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145991'>君讳廷构，字正材，洛阳人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145991_comment'></div>岐山至德，绵瓜瓞者万邦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145991_comment'></div>洛宅旧都，守枌榆者百世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145991_comment'></div>簪组相继，谱谍存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145991_comment'></div>曾祖侃，太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145991_comment'></div>祖潜，深州乐寿县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145991_comment'></div>避乱南徙，因家广陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145991_comment'></div>考延禧，明经擢第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145991_comment'></div>有吴之霸，受辟为淮南巡官，累官至户部郎中，与殷文公、游贞公同掌文翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145991_comment'></div>无禄早世，故大位不跻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145991_comment'></div>君即户部第四子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145991_comment'></div>幼而岐嶷，长而笃厚，躬行孝悌，馀力学文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145991_comment'></div>以荫释褐，补弘文馆校书，试吏为池州司户参军，改宣州宁国县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145991_comment'></div>烈祖在藩，乃眷旧族，闻君修谨，复有吏能，因表为黄州长史，宠以朱绂，置之府朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145991_comment'></div>及受禅，迁通事舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145991_comment'></div>鸿业肇兴，王泽遐布，赞导之任，实寄司聪，护戎修聘，观风按狱，受命而出，动罔不臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145991_comment'></div>历事两朝，任遇弥厚，赏赐既数，阶勋屡迁，而通事之任如故，盖惜其能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145991_comment'></div>保大七年，转将作少监，判四方馆事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145991_comment'></div>浩穰之地，尹正为难，复以本官判江宁府事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145991_comment'></div>其间监诸侯之典者十，通四方之命者三，摄州府之政者六，按枉挠之狱者四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145991_comment'></div>或敷惠于新附之俗，或投身于危乱之地，本于忠而后动，忘其生而后存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145991_comment'></div>元宗嘉之，以为客省使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145991_comment'></div>今上嗣位，深惟旧劳，特加金紫光禄大夫、台州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145991_comment'></div>常御寿昌殿视事，中外之人，咸得引见，又以君为寿昌殿承宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145991_comment'></div>出为忠义军监军、泉南等州宣谕使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145991_comment'></div>还，迁筠州刺史、本州团练，仍使充客省使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145991_comment'></div>君以备尝艰危，复逼迟暮，恳辞繁剧，恩旨不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145991_comment'></div>丙寅岁十月二十二日，终于京师某里之官舍，春秋六十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145991_comment'></div>诏废朝一日，赐谥曰某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145991_comment'></div>明年正月日葬于某所，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145991_comment'></div>夫人天水县君姜氏，辅佐之勤，率由妇礼，训诲诸子，备有义方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1145991_comment'></div>子大理评事崇俭，太常寺奉礼郎崇素，及崇顺、崇信等，皆儒谨，且不坠其先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1145991_comment'></div>铉家世通旧，尝接姻娅，淡成之分，终始不渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1145991_comment'></div>何以寘怀，是用刊德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1145991_comment'></div>其铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1145991'>猗嗟周君，世济其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1145991_comment'></div>展如之人，克嗣厥声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1145991_comment'></div>受任干蛊，临难忘身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1145991_comment'></div>居中处约，全和保真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1145991_comment'></div>与物皆化，万古同尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1145991_comment'></div>松楸勿伐，兰菊惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1145991_comment'></div>刊石表墓，于嗟善人！</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1145991_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=967&endYear=967')">967年</a>　本年，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，不奉佛，然绝好鬼神之说。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=968&endYear=968')">968年8月</a>　八月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，为亡妻王畹作墓志。作品：唐故文水县君王氏夫人墓铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一七。）</span><div id='poem_1146008' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146008' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146008?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故文水县君王氏夫人墓铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（968年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146008")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146008_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146008'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146008'>夫人讳畹，字国香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146008_comment'></div>其先太原人，今为庐江人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146008_comment'></div>祖潜，左司郎中，赠太府卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146008_comment'></div>考坦，礼部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146008_comment'></div>皆以贞干纯懿，见称于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146008_comment'></div>夫人丽窈窕之容，秉明慧之性，幼失所恃，事继亲以孝闻，在家不违于姆师，移天不失于妇顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146008_comment'></div>初，先姑之治家也，严而有惠，通而得礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146008_comment'></div>夫人观形禀教，莫不率循，故三十馀年，门风家法，凛然如旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146008_comment'></div>性尚静退，不乐世喧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146008_comment'></div>始愚之在要职也，夫人忧形于色；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146008_comment'></div>及其居贬所，反欣然忘贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146008_comment'></div>此其所以为异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146008_comment'></div>虽门族素盛，而世涂多故，禄赐所入，赒给无遗，丰约同之，亲疏如一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146008_comment'></div>至于浣濯之俭，组紃之勤，蘩藻尽敬，儒玄励操，环佩中节，始终不渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146008_comment'></div>少善秦声，长亦舍弃，每晨兴，诵《五千言》而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146008_comment'></div>享年五十，戊辰岁八月一日终于京师舜泽里之官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146008_comment'></div>其年十月二十三日，归窆于西山洪崖乡鸾冈里，从先姑大茔，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146008_comment'></div>有子曰夷直，女曰神华、林华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146008_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146008_comment'></div>愚常以体道委命为怀，而情之所钟，不知其恸，衔涕秉笔，庶不泯其声尘焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146008_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1146008'>缑岭之灵，生此淑人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146008_comment'></div>洪崖之滨，寄此新坟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146008_comment'></div>生与道俱，没与仙邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146008_comment'></div>悠悠精爽，岂或为尘！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146008_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146008_comment'></div>吾信积善之必尔，故摅恨于斯文。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1146008_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=968&endYear=968')">968年11月</a>　十一月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，奉诏参定李煜纳小周后婚礼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=968&endYear=968')">968年11月</a>　十一月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，于李煜纳小周后婚宴上赋诗。作品：纳后夕侍宴。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42939' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42939' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42939?labeling=true' target='_blank'>纳后夕侍宴</a><span class='authorDate'>（968年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42939")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_42939_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42939'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42939'>天上轩星正，云间湛露垂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42939'>礼容过渭水，宴喜胜瑶池。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42939'>彩雾笼花烛，升龙肃羽仪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42939'>君臣欢乐日，文物盛明时。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42939'>帘捲银河转，香凝玉漏迟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_42939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_42939'>华封倾祝意，觞酒与声诗。<div id='poem_sentence_5_42939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_42939'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_42939_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=968&endYear=968')">968年11月</a>　十一月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，有诗讽李煜纳小周后。作品：又三绝。<span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=968&endYear=968')">968年</a>　本年，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，为义兴县兴道观北极殿碑记篆额。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=968&endYear=968')">968年</a>　约于本年，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，与殷崇义有诗歌唱和。作品：奉和右省仆射西亭高卧作。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42942' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_0_42942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42942'>蝉声当槛急，虹影向檐垂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=969&endYear=969')">969年2月</a>　二月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，侍李煜游北苑，分题赋诗。作品：北苑侍宴杂咏诗五首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42577' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42576_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42576'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42576'>昨朝才解冻，今日又开花。<div id='poem_title_42579_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42579'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42579'>细丽披金彩，氛氲散远馨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42579'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_42579_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=969&endYear=969')">969年2月</a>　二月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，侍李煜游北苑，应制作诗。作品：柳枝词十首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42611' class='_poem'><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42614'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42614'>绿水成文柳带摇，东风初到不鸣条。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42614_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42618'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42618'>新春花柳竞芳姿，偏爱垂杨拂地枝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42619'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42619'>凝碧池头蘸翠涟，凤凰楼畔簇晴烟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42619'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_42619_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_42620' class='authorDate'>（969年2月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_42620_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42620'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42620'>侍从甘泉与未央，移舟偏要近垂杨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42620'>樱桃未绽梅花老，折得柔条百尺长。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42620_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42620'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_42620_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=969&endYear=969')">969年2月</a>　二月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，侍李煜游北苑，奉诏为侍宴诗集作序。作品：北苑侍宴诗序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1145903' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145903' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145903?labeling=true' target='_blank'>北苑侍宴诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（969年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145903")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145903_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145903'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145903'>臣闻通物情而顺时令者，帝王之能事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145903_comment'></div>感惠泽而发颂声者，臣子之自然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145903_comment'></div>况乎上国春归，华林雨霁，宸游载穆，圣藻先飞，雷动风行，君唱臣和，故可告于太史，播在薰弦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145903_comment'></div>帝典皇坟，莫不由斯者已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145903_comment'></div>岁躔己巳，月属仲春，主上御龙舟，游北苑，亲王旧相，至于近臣，并俨华缨，同参曲宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145903_comment'></div>时也风清景淑，物茂人和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145903_comment'></div>望蒋峤之嵚崟，祝为圣寿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145903_comment'></div>汎潮沟之清浅，流作天波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145903_comment'></div>丝篁与击壤齐声，盏斝共君恩并醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145903_comment'></div>乃命即席分题赋诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145903_comment'></div>睿思云飘，天词绮缛，文明所感，蹈咏皆同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145903_comment'></div>既击钵以争先，亦分题而较胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145903_comment'></div>长景未暮，百篇已成，自扬《大雅》之风，岂在遒人之职？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145903_comment'></div>奉诏作序，冠于首篇，授以集书，藏之金匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145903_comment'></div>谨上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1145903_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=969&endYear=969')">969年3月</a>　三月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，有诗和殷崇义。作品：奉和宫傅相公怀旧见寄四十韵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42977' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42977' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42977?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和宫傅相公怀旧见寄四十韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（969年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42977")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_42977_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42977'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42977'>谢傅功成德望全，鸾台初下正萧然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42977'>抟风乍息三千里，感旧重怀四十年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42977'>西掖新官同贾马，南朝兴运似开天。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42977'>文辞职业分工拙，流辈班资让后先。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42977'>每愧陋容劳刻画，长惭顽石费彫镌。<div id='poem_sentence_4_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_42977'>晨趋纶掖吟春永，夕会精庐待月圆。<div id='poem_sentence_5_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_42977'>立马有时同草诏，联镳几处共成篇。<div id='poem_sentence_6_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_42977'>闲歌柳叶翻新曲，醉咏桃花促绮筵。<div id='poem_sentence_7_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_42977'>少壮况逢时世好，经过宁虑岁华迁。<div id='poem_sentence_8_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_42977'>云龙得路须腾跃，社栎非材合弃捐。<div id='poem_sentence_9_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_42977'>再谒湘江犹是幸，两还宣室竟何缘。<div id='poem_sentence_10_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_42977'>已知瑕玷劳磨莹，又得官司重接连。<div id='poem_sentence_11_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_42977'>听漏分宵趋建礼，从游同召赴甘泉。<div id='poem_sentence_12_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_42977'>云开阊阖分台殿，风过华林度管弦。<div id='poem_sentence_13_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_42977'>行止不离<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_42977", 42977, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>宫仗</span>影，衣裾尝惹御炉烟。<div id='poem_sentence_14_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_42977'>师资稷契论<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_42977", 42977, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>中礼</span>，依止山公典小铨。<div id='poem_sentence_15_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_42977'>多谢天波垂赤管，敢教晨景过华塼。<div id='poem_sentence_16_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_42977'>翾飞附骥方经远，巨楫垂风遂济川。<div id='poem_sentence_17_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_42977'>玉烛调时钧轴正，台阶平处德星悬。<div id='poem_sentence_18_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_42977'>岩廊礼绝威容肃，布素情深友好偏。<div id='poem_sentence_19_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_42977'>长拟营巢安大厦，忽惊操钺领中权。<div id='poem_sentence_20_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_42977'>吴门日丽龙衔节，京口沙晴鹢画船。<div id='poem_sentence_21_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_42977'>盖代名高方赫赫，恋恩心切更乾乾。<div id='poem_sentence_22_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_42977'>袁安辞气忠仍恳，吴汉精诚直且专。<div id='poem_sentence_23_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_42977'>却许丘明师纪传，更容疏广奉周旋。<div id='poem_sentence_24_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_42977'>朱门自得施行马，厚禄何妨食万钱。<div id='poem_sentence_25_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_42977'>密疏尚应劳献替，清谈唯见论空玄。<div id='poem_sentence_26_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_42977'>东山妓乐供闲步，北牖风凉足晏眠。<div id='poem_sentence_27_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_42977'>玄武湖边林隐见，五城桥下棹洄沿。<div id='poem_sentence_28_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_42977'>曾移苑树开红药，新凿家池种白莲。<div id='poem_sentence_29_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_42977'>不遣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_42977", 42977, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>前驺</span>妨野逸，别寻逋客互招延。<div id='poem_sentence_30_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_42977'>棋枰寂静陈虚阁，诗笔沉吟劈彩笺。<div id='poem_sentence_31_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_42977'>往事偶来春梦里，闲愁因动落花前。<div id='poem_sentence_32_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_42977'>青云旧侣嗟谁在，白首亲情倍见怜。<div id='poem_sentence_33_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_42977'>尽日凝思殊怅望，一章追叙信精研。<div id='poem_sentence_34_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_42977'>韶颜莫与年争竞，世虑须凭道节宣。<div id='poem_sentence_35_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_42977'>幸喜书生为将相，定由阴德致神仙。<div id='poem_sentence_36_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_42977'>羊公剩有登临兴，尚子都无嫁娶牵。<div id='poem_sentence_37_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_42977'>退象天山镇浮竞，起为霖雨润原田。<div id='poem_sentence_38_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_42977'>从容自保君臣契，何必扁舟始是贤。<div id='poem_sentence_39_42977_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_42977'></div><div id='poem_sentence_40_42977_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=969&endYear=969')">969年3月</a>　三月，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，又有诗和殷崇义。作品：相公垂览和诗复贻长句辄次来韵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42688' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42688' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42688?labeling=true' target='_blank'>右省仆射<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>相公垂览和诗复贻长句辄次来韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（969年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript:
