class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_42688_0'>① 四字原缺，据《全唐诗》补</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42688'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42688'>西院春归<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_42688", 42688, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>道思</span>深，披衣闲听暝猿吟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42688'>铺陈政事留黄阁，偃息神机在素琴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42688'>玉柄暂时疏末座，瑶华频复惠清音。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42688'>开晴便作东山约，共赏烟霞放旷心。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42688'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42688_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=969&endYear=969')">969年</a>　春，在江宁府为礼部侍郎，徙尚书左丞，逾月而罢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=969&endYear=969')">969年</a>　本年，在江宁府为尚书左丞，拜兵部侍郎、知制诰、翰林学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=970&endYear=970')">970年2月15日</a>　二月十五日，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，为常州义兴县重建长桥作碑记。作品：常州义兴县重建长桥记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一三。）</span><div id='poem_1145944' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145944' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145944?labeling=true' target='_blank'>常州义兴县重建长桥记</a><span class='authorDate'>（970年2月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145944")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145944_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145944'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145944'>圣人作川梁以济不通，舟车所及，纚连棋布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145944_comment'></div>若乃形胜杰大，名闻天下者，亦无几何，阳羡长桥其一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145944_comment'></div>夫英贤之所躔次，邑居之所瞻望，山川之精粹宅焉，里城之神灵凭焉，废而兴之，圮而葺之，岂惟备政，足以徼福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145944_comment'></div>是桥也，徵诸图谍，则后汉邑令袁君创造，国朝永泰中令丘君新之，其他无闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145944_comment'></div>中兴之初，邑有义夫曰吴濛、吴浈，率以私帑，备加营构，人赖其利，踰三十载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145944_comment'></div>丙辰岁，国步中梗，百越寇边，邑人败之，烧营而遁，飞焰旁及，宏梁半摧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145944_comment'></div>甲寅岁，著作佐郎刘君来为邑长，视其制度，知非民力之所能济，乃状其事，白于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145944_comment'></div>上闻嘉之，诏赐钱八十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145944_comment'></div>君信而好古，宽而得众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145944_comment'></div>尉卢茜鼎甲馀庆，俊造策名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145944_comment'></div>政是以和，事无不举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145944_comment'></div>乃相与敷王泽，因民心，备物致用，程功揆日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145944_comment'></div>器利工善，材良事时，戊辰岁冬而裁，明年暮春而毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145944_comment'></div>长五十步，广七步，对县楼而直出，跨荆溪而横绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145944_comment'></div>丹雘其饰，宛偃蹇而虹舒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145944_comment'></div>崇高其势，邈苕亭而山立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145944_comment'></div>朱轮方轨，驷马连骑，营营市井，憧憧往来，有衽席之安，无揭厉之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145944_comment'></div>昔者，乘车济涉，圣人谓之无教；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145944_comment'></div>桥梁弗修，贤相知其弗能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145944_comment'></div>以今方古，胜负分矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145944_comment'></div>夫《书》云考绩，《传》载称伐，庸庸善善，其可废乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145944_comment'></div>刻之贞珉，以示来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145944_comment'></div>庚午岁春二月十五日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1145944_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=970&endYear=970')">970年5月5日</a>　端午，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，宿直，作赋抒怀。作品：新月赋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此赋见《徐公文集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1145778' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145778' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145778?labeling=true' target='_blank'>新月赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（庚午岁宿直作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（970年5月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145778")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145778_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145778'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145778'>五月五日，繁阴乍晴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145778_comment'></div>倬彼新月，丽于太清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145778_comment'></div>映玉绳而绚彩，掩银汉以腾精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145778_comment'></div>对鳷鹊西南之影，步明光东北之楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145778_comment'></div>历历迟漏，悠悠我情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145778_comment'></div>虽万古之不易，感一年而始生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145778_comment'></div>乃有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1145778", 1145778, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>騃女痴男</span>，朱颜稚齿，欣春物之骀荡，登春台之靡迤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145778_comment'></div>杂佩璀错，轻裾飒纚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145778_comment'></div>纷乎拜祝，怡然宴喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145778_comment'></div>人岁岁以潜换，景年年而若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145778_comment'></div>昔我当年，胡云不然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145778_comment'></div>世路多故，流光暗迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145778_comment'></div>易壮心于大观，变玄发于华颠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145778_comment'></div>顾一毛之无济，愧两绶之徒悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145778_comment'></div>况乎万象虚明，九门奥秘，对宣室以方罢，阅通宵而不寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145778_comment'></div>忧心似醉，既慷慨于君恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145778_comment'></div>急景如驰，更凄凉于往事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145778_comment'></div>想愬月以长歌，遂抽毫而见意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1145778_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=970&endYear=970')">970年8月</a>　八月，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，奉诏作诗送李从益出镇宣州。作品：御筵送邓王。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42914' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42914' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42914?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御筵送邓王</a><span class='authorDate'>（970年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42914")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42914_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42914'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42914'>禁里秋<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作花）</span>光似水清，林烟池影共离情。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42914'>暂移黄阁只三载，却望紫垣都数程。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42914'>满座清风天子送，随车甘雨郡人迎。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42914'>绮霞阁上诗题在，从此还应有颂声。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42914'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42914_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=970&endYear=970')">970年8月</a>　八月，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，奉诏作诗序送李从益出镇宣州。作品：和送邓王二十六弟牧宣城诗序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷八八二。）</span><div id='poem_1145918' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145918' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145918?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和送邓王二十六弟牧宣城诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（970年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145918")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145918_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145918'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145918'>夫政成调鼎，寄重于蕃，盖欲圣主之恩均于远迩，贤人之业浃于中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145918_comment'></div>故所以命丞相邓王从镒，佩相印，被公衮，拥双旌，统千骑，扬帆江宁之浦，弭节敬亭之区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145918_comment'></div>若乃割友悌之怀，辍股肱之侍，所以示天下之至公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145918_comment'></div>夙驾已严，前驺将引，既辞复召，重赐饯筵，所以极大君之恩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145918_comment'></div>敦睦之义，于斯有光，申诏侍臣，述叙赋诗云尔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1145918_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=970&endYear=970')">970年9月7日</a>　九月七日，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，作文祭韩熙载。作品：祭韩侍郎文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二〇。）</span><div id='poem_1146042' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146042' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146042?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭韩侍郎文</a><span class='authorDate'>（970年9月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146042")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146042_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146042'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146042'>维开宝三年太岁庚午，九月己亥朔七日乙巳，东海徐铉，谨以清酌庶羞之奠，昭祭于故中书侍郎、赠相国昌黎公之灵：天祐下民，必生贤人，数有治乱，道或亨屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146042_comment'></div>君子处之，全名保真，穷不易节，达不私身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146042_comment'></div>呜呼明公，与道为邻，其本也忠，其动也仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146042_comment'></div>折而不挠，屈则能伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146042_comment'></div>懋此成绩，扬于王庭，名闻天下，道合明君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146042_comment'></div>宜若张公，上应台星；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146042_comment'></div>宜如卫武，享兹百龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146042_comment'></div>如何不淑，与世同尘！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146042_comment'></div>城郢遗忠，感深紫宸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146042_comment'></div>黔娄之衾，赐从御府；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146042_comment'></div>季子之印，佩入泉扃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146042_comment'></div>知与不知，孰无悲辛？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146042_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146042_comment'></div>某惟不佞，早奉光容，倾盖之交，缱绻相从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146042_comment'></div>公之知我，如我知公，何义不协，何言不同？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146042_comment'></div>宁惧触鳞之忤，岂防羸角之凶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146042_comment'></div>先号后笑，无初有终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146042_comment'></div>霰雪既消，阳光乃融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146042_comment'></div>海郡山城，几怜煦沫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146042_comment'></div>南宫西掖，近见抟风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146042_comment'></div>岂主恩之可报，幸吾道之非穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146042_comment'></div>今也岁月<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1146042", 1146042, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>遒迈</span>，悲欢一空，平生气宇，夙昔心胸，极视听而无所，与造化而冥蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146042_comment'></div>露泫门柳，霜凋井桐，物感于外，悲来自中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146042_comment'></div>生刍表德，絮酒申恭，愿<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1146042", 1146042, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>贞魂</span>之降鉴，庶丹恳以斯通。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1146042_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=970&endYear=970')">970年9月</a>　九月，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，为韩熙载作墓志。作品：唐故中书侍郎光政殿学士承旨昌黎韩公墓铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一六。）</span><div id='poem_1145994' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145994' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145994?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故中书侍郎光政殿学士承旨昌黎韩公墓铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（970年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145994")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145994_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145994'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145994'>公讳熙载，字叔言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145994_comment'></div>其先南阳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145994_comment'></div>《传》称武王之穆，《诗》美韩侯受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145994_comment'></div>晋以六卿升降，汉以三杰重轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145994_comment'></div>至东晋末，征西从事延之以忠义之节，践艰屯之运，避乱远徙，遂家昌黎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145994_comment'></div>馀庆流光，最为繁衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145994_comment'></div>曾祖钧，太仆卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145994_comment'></div>祖殷，侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145994_comment'></div>考光嗣，秘书少监、淄青观察支使，故又为齐人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145994_comment'></div>公秉夙成之智，负不羁之才，文高学深，角立杰出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145994_comment'></div>年始弱冠，游于洛阳，声名蔼然，一举擢第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145994_comment'></div>同光之乱，藩郡崩离，公以国难方兴，家艰仍构，瞻乌择木，杖策渡江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145994_comment'></div>烈祖孝高皇帝纳麓在辰，侧席时彦，得公甚喜，宾礼有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145994_comment'></div>于时有吴肇基，庶事草创，公以俊迈之气，高视名流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145994_comment'></div>既绛、灌之徒弗容，亦季、孟之间不处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145994_comment'></div>以校书郎释褐，出为滁、和、常三州从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145994_comment'></div>公亦怡然，不以屑意，咏风月，游山水而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145994_comment'></div>中兴受命，上嗣抚军，以公有七子之才，膺四友之拜，徵为秘书郎，掌东宫文翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145994_comment'></div>元宗深器之，及践位，以为虞部员外郎、史馆修撰，赐绯，又以大礼繁叠，加太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145994_comment'></div>时有司议孝高庙宜称宗，司门郎中萧君俨上疏论之，公与给事中江君文蔚协同其议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145994_comment'></div>凡书疏论难，皆成于公手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145994_comment'></div>由是庙号尊谥，定于一言，君子以为真博士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145994_comment'></div>顷之，以本官权知制诰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145994_comment'></div>初，公但以文章际会，未尝与政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145994_comment'></div>及其当惟新之运，感知己之恩，未及听政，章疏相属，或驳正失礼，或指摘时病，由是大为权要所嫉，竟罢其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145994_comment'></div>丞相宋公，朝之元老，势逼地高，公又廷奏党与，词旨深切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145994_comment'></div>天子优容之，而用事者滋怒，旋贬和州司士参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145994_comment'></div>数年，移宣州节度推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145994_comment'></div>徵还，复为虞部员外郎，迁郎中、史馆修撰，赐紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145994_comment'></div>俄拜中书舍人，从时望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145994_comment'></div>公虽才识优赡，而质性疏散，凡在位者，道复不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1145994_comment'></div>于是深居移病，罕与朝谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1145994_comment'></div>时兵兴之后，国用不充，公援古酌今，请以钱为币。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1145994_comment'></div>时献封者甚众，元宗独以公议为长，即拜户部侍郎，充铸钱使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1145994_comment'></div>今上践位，改吏部侍郎，兼修国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1145994_comment'></div>初，铸钱之作也，自宰执而下，相与沮之，故百司不供，久未能就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1145994_comment'></div>上为之晓譬事理，亲加督责，而公犹不胜其忿，尝因对见，声色俱厉，因徙为秘书监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1145994_comment'></div>不逾年，复拜吏部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1145994_comment'></div>新钱既行，大济经费，诏赐钱二百万，拜兵部尚书，充勤政殿学士承旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1145994_comment'></div>公少而放旷，不拘小节，及年位俱高，弥自纵逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1145994_comment'></div>拥妓女，奏清商，士无贤愚，皆得接待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1145994_comment'></div>职务既简，称疾不朝，家人之节，颇成宽易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1145994_comment'></div>虽名重于世，人亦讶其太过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1145994_comment'></div>上不得已，左迁太子右庶子，分司南都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1145994_comment'></div>于是谢遣妓乐，单车首路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1145994_comment'></div>留之未几，复为兵部尚书、学士如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1145994_comment'></div>是时岁比旱歉，主上忧勤，公复论刑政之源，明防救之术，又上《格言》五篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1145994_comment'></div>手诏嘉纳，即拜中书侍郎，充光政殿学士承旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1145994_comment'></div>初，上选近侍数臣直宿禁中，常御光政殿召对，夜分乃罢，故命公此职，以宠异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1145994_comment'></div>霖雨之望方深，钟漏之期遽逼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1145994_comment'></div>春秋六十有九，庚午岁秋七月二十七日没于京凤台里之官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1145994_comment'></div>上省奏震悼，为之涕流，有司奏当辍朝三日，</div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1145994_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=970&endYear=970')">970年</a>　约于本年，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，为李煜《杂说》作序。作品：御制杂说序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1145902' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145902' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145902?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御制杂说序</a><span class='authorDate'>（970年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145902")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145902_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145902'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145902'>臣闻轩后之神也，畏爱止乎三百；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145902_comment'></div>唐尧之圣也，倦勤及乎耄期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145902_comment'></div>文王之明夷也，爻象周于六虚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145902_comment'></div>宣父之感麟也，褒贬流于百代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145902_comment'></div>乃知功利之及物者，与形器而有限；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145902_comment'></div>道德之垂宪者，将造化而常新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145902_comment'></div>是故体仁者必恳恳于立言，务远者必勤勤于弘道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145902_comment'></div>然则封泰山，告成功，七十二家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145902_comment'></div>正礼乐，删《诗》、《书》，一人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145902_comment'></div>大矣哉，立教之难也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145902_comment'></div>有唐基命，长发祥符，旧物重甄，斯文不坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145902_comment'></div>皇上高明博厚，浚哲文思，既承累圣之资，仍就甘盘之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145902_comment'></div>鸿才绮缛，理绝名言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145902_comment'></div>默识泉深，事符影响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145902_comment'></div>自祗膺眷命，钦若重熙，广大孝以厚时风，励惟精而勤庶政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145902_comment'></div>宥万方而罪己，体百姓以为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145902_comment'></div>俗富刑清，时安岁稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145902_comment'></div>其或万机暇豫，禁籞宴居，接对侍臣，宵分乃罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145902_comment'></div>讨论坟典，昧旦而兴，口无择言，手不释卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145902_comment'></div>尝从容谓近臣曰：「卿辈从公之暇，莫若为学为文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145902_comment'></div>为学为文，莫若讨论六籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145902_comment'></div>游先王之道义不成，不失为古儒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145902_comment'></div>今之为学，所宗者小说，所尚者刀笔，故发言奋藻，则在古人之下风，以是故也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145902_comment'></div>其高识远量又如此焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145902_comment'></div>昔魏武帝有言「老而勤学」，而所著止于兵书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145902_comment'></div>吴大帝亦云「学问自益」，而无闻述作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145902_comment'></div>风化之旨，彼其恧欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145902_comment'></div>属者国步中艰，兵锋始戢，惜民力而屈己，畏天命而侧身，静虑凝神，和光戢耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145902_comment'></div>而或深惟遂古，遐考万殊，惧时运之难并，鉴谟猷之可久，于是属思天人之际，游心今古之间，触绪研几，因文见意，纵横毫翰，炳焕缣缃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145902_comment'></div>以为百王之季，六乐道丧，移风易俗之用，荡而无止，慆心堙耳之声，流而不反，故演《乐记》焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145902_comment'></div>尧舜既往，魏晋已还，授受非公，争夺萌起，故论享国延促焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1145902_comment'></div>三正不修，法弊无救，甘心于季世之伪，绝意于还淳之理，故论古今淳薄焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1145902_comment'></div>战国之后，右武贱儒，以狙诈为智能，以经艺为迂阔，此风不革，世难未已，故论儒术焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1145902_comment'></div>父子恭爱之情，君臣去就之分，则褒申生，明荀彧，俾死生大义皎然明白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1145902_comment'></div>推是而往，无弗臻善，皆天地之深心，圣贤之密意，礼乐之极致，教化之本源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1145902_comment'></div>六籍之微辞，群疑之互见，莫不近如指掌，焕若发蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1145902_comment'></div>万物之动不能逃其形，百王之变不能异其趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1145902_comment'></div>洋洋乎，大人之谟训也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1145902_comment'></div>夫天工不能独运，元后不能独理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1145902_comment'></div>故有道无时，孟子所以咨嗟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1145902_comment'></div>有君无臣，郑公所以叹恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1145902_comment'></div>庶乎斯民有幸，大道将行，举而错之域中，则三五之功，何远乎尔？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1145902_comment'></div>臣又闻将顺致美，铺陈耿光，布尧言于万邦，称汉德于殊俗，盖词臣之职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1145902_comment'></div>若乃向明而理，负扆而朝，庆赏威刑，豫游言动，则有太史氏存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1145902_comment'></div>又若雅颂文赋，凡三十卷，鸿笔丽藻，玉振金相，则有中书舍人、集贤殿学士徐锴所撰《御集序》详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1145902_comment'></div>今立言之作，未即宣行，理冠皇坟，谦称《杂说》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1145902_comment'></div>臣铉以密侍禁掖，首获观瞻，有诏冠篇，勒成三卷，而三卷之中文义既广，又分上下焉，凡一百篇，要道备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1145902_comment'></div>将《五千》而并久，与二曜以同明，昭示孙谟，永光册府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1145902_comment'></div>谨上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1145902_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=970&endYear=970')">970年</a>　约于本年，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，有诗献殷崇义。作品：史馆庭梅见其毫末历载三十今已半枯尝僚诸公唯相公与铉在耳睹物兴感率成短篇谨书献上伏惟垂览。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42687' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42687' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42687?labeling=true' target='_blank'>史馆庭梅见其毫末历载三十今已半枯尝<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>僚诸公唯相公与铉在耳睹物兴感率成短篇谨书献上伏惟垂览</a><span class='authorDate'>（970年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42687")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42687_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_42687_0'>① 四库本、备要本、徐本、《全唐诗》作尝</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42687'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42687'>东观婆娑树，曾怜甲坼时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42687'>繁英共攀折，芳岁几推移。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42687'>往事皆陈迹，清香亦暗衰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42687'>相看宜自喜，双鬓合垂丝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42687_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42687'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42687_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=970&endYear=970')">970年</a>　约于本年，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，有诗和殷崇义。作品：太傅相公深感庭梅再成绝唱曲垂借示倍认知怜谨用旧韵攀和。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42675' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42675' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42675?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太傅相公深感庭梅再成绝唱曲垂借示倍认知怜谨用旧韵攀和</a><span class='authorDate'>（970年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42675")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42675_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42675'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42675'>禁省繁华地，含芳自一时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42675'>雪英开复落，红药植还移<span class='inlineComment2'>（谓尝为翰林，又为史馆）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42675'>静想分今昔，频吟叹盛衰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42675'>多情共如此，争免鬓成丝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42675'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42675_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=970&endYear=970')">970年</a>　约于本年，命弟徐锴作诗和殷崇义。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=971&endYear=971')">971年11月</a>　十一月，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，代乔匡舜作李景达赠太弟哀册文。作品：齐王赠太弟哀册文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1145872' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145872' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145872?labeling=true' target='_blank'>齐王赠太弟哀册文<span class='inlineComment2'>（代乔侍郎）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（971年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145872")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145872_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145872'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145872'>维年月日，天策上将军、太师、尚书令、临川牧齐王薨于临川府之正寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145872_comment'></div>主上追先皇托付之意，表叔父逊让之风，乃下明诏，册赠太弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145872_comment'></div>即以其年十一月日葬于江州某县某乡庐山之原，从理命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145872_comment'></div>绡幕夕陈，虞歌晓引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145872_comment'></div>改兔园之宾馆，设龙楼之陛楯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145872_comment'></div>阒灵仪以愈远，穷哀端而靡尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145872_comment'></div>怆永恨于宸襟，俾诞扬于令问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145872_comment'></div>其词曰：皇天眷祐，锡唐良辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145872_comment'></div>时惟宗英，裔自文祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145872_comment'></div>孝悌敦悫，机神颖悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145872_comment'></div>昔在中兴，爰当就傅，申画宛水，锡兹茅土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145872_comment'></div>德望日跻，邦家是毗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145872_comment'></div>钩陈宿卫，官籥攸司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145872_comment'></div>于惟淮甸，实始皇基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145872_comment'></div>导之以礼，董之以威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145872_comment'></div>俗赋《甘棠》之颂，人歌《乐职》之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145872_comment'></div>运属继明，业隆二圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145872_comment'></div>首辑瑞玉，来参大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145872_comment'></div>乃为左相，其班上台；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145872_comment'></div>乃封夏口，其赋千乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145872_comment'></div>赫矣元后，蒸哉古风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145872_comment'></div>不私其子，天下为公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145872_comment'></div>并命叔仲，奋兹显庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145872_comment'></div>或践我旧藩，或陟尔青宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145872_comment'></div>辞不获命，处之益恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145872_comment'></div>晋郑之勋，推而更融；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145872_comment'></div>臧札之操，久而弥崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145872_comment'></div>若太伯之让，异周公之东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145872_comment'></div>京江汝水，旄节从容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145872_comment'></div>皇统既正，灵符允答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145872_comment'></div>国步清谧，群生欣洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1145872_comment'></div>复大道于三古，永文昭于万乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1145872_comment'></div>越我嗣君，尊尊亲亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1145872_comment'></div>极以吕望之高位，崇以贞观之旧称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1145872_comment'></div>赐书不诏，赞礼不名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1145872_comment'></div>曰予小子，实繄叔父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1145872_comment'></div>维藩维翰，宗社之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1145872_comment'></div>永锡难老，日新王度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1145872_comment'></div>谓天盖高，命亦靡常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1145872_comment'></div>台阶殒宿，河月沉光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1145872_comment'></div>恸东堂之哀临，辍南国之舂相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1145872_comment'></div>与圣贤而共叹，独天地之何长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1145872_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1145872_comment'></div>知生若寄，临凶奢于蜃炭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1145872_comment'></div>举士庶而均哀，颂声猷于无间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1145872_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1145872_comment'></div>归虎节于王府，靡鸾旌于雉门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1145872_comment'></div>闲西园之风月，惨缑岭之烟云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1145872_comment'></div>象辂回兮遵涂远，归帷整兮浙水奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1145872_comment'></div>宾友散兮霰雪积，巾箱故兮经籍残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1145872_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1145872_comment'></div>身殁壤存，道悠运促。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1145872_comment'></div>赠今日之典册，閟当时之宝玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1145872_comment'></div>全大义以经国，激清风而被俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1145872_comment'></div>昭遗烈于千龄，寄玄堂于陵谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1145872_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1145872_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_1145872'>李校云：「临凶以下有脱讹，诸本皆同」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1145872_comment'></div>《全唐文》「临凶」下有「阙」字。</div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1145872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1145872'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_55_1145872_0'>⑴ 《徐公文集》卷九。又见《全唐文》卷八八七。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1145872_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=971&endYear=971')">971年</a>　约于本年四月，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，有诗和李从善。作品：依韵和令公大王蔷薇诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_42940' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42940' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42940?labeling=true' target='_blank'>依韵和令公大王蔷薇诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（971年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42940")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_42940_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42940'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42940'>绿树成阴后，群芳稍歇时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42940'>谁将新濯锦，挂向最长枝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42940'>卷箔香先入，凭栏影任移。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42940'>赏频嫌酒渴，吟苦怕霜髭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42940'>架迥笼云幄，庭虚展绣帷。<div id='poem_sentence_4_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_42940'>有情萦舞袖，无力罥游丝。<div id='poem_sentence_5_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_42940'>嫩蕊莺偷采，柔条柳伴垂。<div id='poem_sentence_6_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_42940'>荀池波自照，梁苑客尝窥。<div id='poem_sentence_7_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_42940'>玉李寻皆谢，金桃亦暗衰。<div id='poem_sentence_8_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_42940'>花中应独贵，庭下故开迟。<div id='poem_sentence_9_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_42940'>委艳妆苔砌，分华借槿篱。<div id='poem_sentence_10_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_42940'>低昂匀灼烁，浓淡叠参差。<div id='poem_sentence_11_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_42940'>幸植王宫里，仍逢宰府知。<div id='poem_sentence_12_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_42940'>芳心向谁许，醉态不能支。<div id='poem_sentence_13_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_42940'>芍药天教避，玫瑰众共嗤。<div id='poem_sentence_14_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_42940'>光明烘昼景，润腻裛轻𩅰。<div id='poem_sentence_15_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_42940'>丽似期神女，珍如重卫姬。<div id='poem_sentence_16_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_42940'>君王偏属咏，七子尽搜奇。<div id='poem_sentence_17_42940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_42940'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_42940_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=971&endYear=971')">971年</a>　约于本年秋，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，奉李煜之命作诗。作品：茱萸诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42802' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42802' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42802?labeling=true' target='_blank'>茱萸诗<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（971年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42802")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42802_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_42802_0'>① 一本作《奉御札赋茱萸诗》。《御札》云：“新酒初熟，偶与郑王诸公开尝于清宴堂庑之间，既览秋物，复瞩霜笺，因赋茱萸一题，以遣此时之兴。卿鸿才敏思，不可独醒，宜应急徵，同赋前旨。”铉因进诗云：</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42802'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42802'>万物庆西成，茱萸独擅名。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42802_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42802'>房排红结小，香透夹衣轻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42802_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42802'>宿露沾犹重，朝阳照更明。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42802_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42802'>长和菊花酒，高宴奉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_42802", 42802, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>西清</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42802_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42802'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42802_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=971&endYear=971')">971年</a>　约于本年秋，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，有诗和李煜。作品：奉和御制茱萸。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42778' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42778' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42778?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制茱萸</a><span class='authorDate'>（971年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42778")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42778_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42778'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42778'>台畔西风御果新，芳香精彩丽萧辰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42778'>柔条细叶<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_42778", 42778, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>妆治</span>好，紫蒂红芳点缀匀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42778'>几朵得陪天上宴，千株长作洞中春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42778'>今朝圣藻偏流咏，黄菊无由更敢邻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42778'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42778_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=971&endYear=971')">971年</a>　约于本年秋，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，得李煜赐酒，进诗以谢。作品：蒙恩赐酒奉旨令醉进诗以谢。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42925' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42925' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42925?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蒙恩赐酒奉旨令醉进诗以谢</a><span class='authorDate'>（971年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42925")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42925_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42925'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42925'>明光殿里夜迢迢，多病逢秋自寂寥<span class='inlineComment2'>（臣以病戒酒多时）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42925'>蜡炬乍传丹凤诏，御题初认白云谣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42925'>今宵幸识衢尊味，明日知停入閤朝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42925'>为感君恩判一醉，不烦辛苦解金貂。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42925'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42925_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=971&endYear=971')">971年</a>　约于本年秋，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，作诗送陈致雍致仕。作品：送陈秘监归泉州。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42834' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42834' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42834?labeling=true' "poem_title_42834")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42834_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42834'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42834'>风满潮沟木叶飞，水边行客驻骖騑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42834'>三朝恩泽冯唐老，万里乡关贺监归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42834'>世路穷通前事远，半生谈笑此心违。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42834'>离歌不识高堂庆，特地令人泪满衣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42834'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42834_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=971&endYear=971')">971年</a>　约于本年秋，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，再作诗送陈致雍致仕。作品：又听霓裳羽衣曲送陈君。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42572' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42572' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42572?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又听霓裳羽衣曲送陈君</a><span class='authorDate'>（971年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42572")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_42572_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42572'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42572'>清商一曲远人行，桃叶津头月正明。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42572'>此是开元太平曲，莫教偏作别离声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42572'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_42572_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_42572'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(42572)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=971&endYear=971')">971年</a>　约于本年秋，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，又作诗送陈致雍致仕。作品：又题白鹭洲江鸥送陈君。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42953' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42953' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42953?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又题白鹭洲江鸥送陈君</a><span class='authorDate'>（971年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42953")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_42953_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42953'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42953'>白鹭洲边江路斜，轻鸥接翼满平沙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42953_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42953'>吾徒来送远行客，停舟为尔长叹息。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42953_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42953'>酒旗鱼艇两无猜，月影芦花镇相得。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42953_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42953'>离筵一曲怨复清，满座销魂鸟不惊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42953_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42953'>人生不及水禽乐，安用虚名上麟阁。<div id='poem_sentence_4_42953_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_42953'>同心携手今如此，金鼎丹砂何寂寞。<div id='poem_sentence_5_42953_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_42953'>天涯后会眇难期，从此又应添白髭。<div id='poem_sentence_6_42953_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_42953'>愿君不忘分飞处，长保翩翩洁白姿。<div id='poem_sentence_7_42953_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_42953'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_42953_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年</a>　春，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，有诗送孟宾于。作品：送孟宾于员外还新淦。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42840?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送孟宾于员外还新淦</a><span class='authorDate'>（972年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42840")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42840'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42840'>暂来城阙不从容，却佩银鱼隐玉峰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42840'>双涧水边欹醉石，九仙台下听风松。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42840'>题诗翠壁称逋客，采药春畦狎老农。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42840'>野鹤乘轩云出岫，不知何日再相逢。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42840'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42840_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年9月</a>　九月，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，遵陈德成遗嘱，为之作墓志。作品：唐故建州观察处置等使陈公墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一六。）</span><div id='poem_1145996' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145996' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145996?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故左右静江军都军使忠义军节度建州观察处置等使留后光禄大夫检校太尉右威卫大将军临颍县开国子食邑五百户陈公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（972年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145996")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145996_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145996'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145996'>公讳德成，字仲德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145996_comment'></div>其先颍川人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145996_comment'></div>帝妫馀烈，侯满崇封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145996_comment'></div>盛德之祀绵邈于百世，光远之庆蕃衍于万国，故我洪胄，代雄建安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145996_comment'></div>王室中微，闽方角立，网罗英异，弘济艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145996_comment'></div>我曾祖茂新、祖滔，皆以雄才勇略，奋扬忠力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145996_comment'></div>将领之任，生表其策勋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145996_comment'></div>督护之名，没垂于饰壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145996_comment'></div>父诲，检校太尉、兼侍中、建州刺史、忠义军节度使，谥忠烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145996_comment'></div>殊勋大节，有信史丰碑存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145996_comment'></div>公即忠烈公之长子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145996_comment'></div>钟粹和之气，秉冲淡之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145996_comment'></div>通习孙吴，固其家法；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145996_comment'></div>酷好坟典，乃自天资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145996_comment'></div>就傅之年，已著名誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145996_comment'></div>先公剖符剑、浦，威信洽闻，诤子之助，实有其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145996_comment'></div>弱冠，为本郡裨将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145996_comment'></div>先公以身守边郡，心存本朝，累表遣公入宿卫，即擢拜右千牛卫将军，充殿直指挥使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145996_comment'></div>恭命畏法，修身择交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145996_comment'></div>先公每言边事，常密疏于纸，遣公上启，默识强记，敷奏閒习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145996_comment'></div>元宗甚嘉之，累迁右静江指挥使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145996_comment'></div>值淮上兵起，王师不振，公屡上书自奋，诏隶西北面行营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145996_comment'></div>以舟师趣济难，破其屯戍，遂入海陵，与诸军会，励兵固守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145996_comment'></div>强敌日益，公连战破之，虏获千计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145996_comment'></div>围兵既遁，乃涉长淮，指下蔡，别率战舰，分击浮桥，三中流矢，神色自若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145996_comment'></div>自秋徂冬，且战且前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145996_comment'></div>凡五进军垒，皆以众寡不敌之势，当轻悍卒至之师，临难忘身，每战必捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145996_comment'></div>而元戎逗挠，逆臣携叛，群帅失道，公全军而还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145996_comment'></div>迁右宣威军厢虞候，制曰：「独此一军之众，堪为百战之师」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145996_comment'></div>其见称如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145996_comment'></div>数月，为和州刺史，又为左天威将军厢虞候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1145996_comment'></div>明年，改池州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1145996_comment'></div>是时疆埸俯定，闾井未完，公奉法循理，正身率下，庭无滞讼，吏不生奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1145996_comment'></div>铁轴牙樯，无忘水犀之备；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1145996_comment'></div>轻裘缓带，常为岘首之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1145996_comment'></div>赋诗纪颂，粲然可述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1145996_comment'></div>元宗南狩，从至石牌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1145996_comment'></div>上每登临置酒，必命公陪侍，访山川之形势，问风俗之美恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1145996_comment'></div>应对详敏，咸有条贯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1145996_comment'></div>捧觞上寿，进退由仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1145996_comment'></div>求解印扈跸，优旨不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1145996_comment'></div>今上嗣服，屡表乞还，徵为右天德军都虞候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1145996_comment'></div>旧制常以舟师为下军，至是，诏旨以南国之用，尚于舟楫，今而后知非是，乃简练精锐，置龙翔军以隶亲卫，命公为龙翔都虞候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1145996_comment'></div>舟师之重，自兹始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1145996_comment'></div>会先君来朝，卧疾邸第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1145996_comment'></div>公亲侍医药，躬执烦辱，容貌瘠损，衣不解带，客至问疾者，不知其已贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1145996_comment'></div>及丁忧制，哀毁过礼，扶护灵柩，归于建安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1145996_comment'></div>诏起为歙州刺史、本州团练使，视事三载，其理如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1145996_comment'></div>秩满，复为右龙翔诸军都虞候，迁都指挥使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1145996_comment'></div>每仲秋讲武训兵，仲冬而毕，进退号令，由公指顾，威容严整，睹者肃然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1145996_comment'></div>顷之，又为虔州巡检使、知州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1145996_comment'></div>五岭之际，地广民悍，内据溪洞，外接蛮夷，告讦敚𭤑，习以为俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1145996_comment'></div>于是申以刑政，示以严明，广视听，审情伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1145996_comment'></div>吏以微文出入者，皆面诘其状，莫不惕息而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1145996_comment'></div>弊为之革，人以之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1145996_comment'></div>于是浚沟隍，严壁垒，出私帑以助费，因农隙而僝功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1145996_comment'></div>凡书劳考绩，此其昭昭者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1145996_comment'></div>寻拜池州观察使，以其秩居虔州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1145996_comment'></div>上以建安之地，人思旧德，且欲以昼锦之盛，显公之能，乃除忠义军节度、建州观察处置等使留后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1145996_comment'></div>公以违奉岁久，无以私为，抗表来朝，固辞不拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1145996_comment'></div>改右威卫大将军，充左右静江都军使，又转光禄大夫、检校太尉，奉以建州之禄，岁计千万，甲第厩马，赐与优渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1145996_comment'></div>俄而被疾，自识终期，申告理命，备有规度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1145996_comment'></div>中使问疾，但曰：「世受主恩，未有以报，惟此为恨耳」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1145996_comment'></div>又亲问门吏，草遗奏既成，自益两句曰：「茍游岱之有知，必结草以为报」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1145996_comment'></div>上省表震悼，手诏答之，公犹捧诏向阙，稽首流涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1145996_comment'></div>壬申岁秋七月十有二日，卒于建业滨江里之官舍，春秋四十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1145996_comment'></div>上痛惜之，至再不视朝，赠安南大都护，遣中使监护葬事，皆从官给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1145996_comment'></div>有司考行，易名曰烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1145996_comment'></div>即以其年九月日葬于某所，从理命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1145996_comment'></div>夫人信都郡君刁氏，故昭武军节度使能之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1145996_comment'></div>容德之美，闺房之秀，宜家睦族，光此门风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1145996_comment'></div>子倩，孝友聪慧，修词好学，以荫起家，授著作佐郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1145996_comment'></div>必大之庆，其在于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1145996_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1145996_comment'></div>公生于戎马之际，长承钟鼎之业，修文习武，全孝资忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1145996_comment'></div>风格端庄，襟怀夷直，嫉恶奖善，如恐不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1145996_comment'></div>睦亲念旧，无有所遗，先人之费，公私毕给，出入数载，家为之贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1145996_comment'></div>在公之馀，手不释卷，篇咏词笔，皆传于时，近代儒学将，唯公而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1145996_comment'></div>凡四典藩郡，皆有借留去思之美，民到于今称之，由是恩顾特隆，委遇无间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1145996_comment'></div>修涂方骋，大年不登，知与不知，皆为悲叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1145996_comment'></div>铉与公非故，特以道义相期，虽复出处不齐，班序致隔，金兰之分，终始不渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1145996_comment'></div>寝门流恸，痛生死之永已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1145996_comment'></div>圆石表墓，患陵谷之靡常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1145996_comment'></div>亦公之遗言，以此见托，岂非慷慨之气，思振发于知己哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1145996_comment'></div>故为铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_84_1145996'>龙泉之灵，武夷之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1145996_comment'></div>生我儒将，垂兹令名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1145996_comment'></div>临戎有勇，察俗有声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1145996_comment'></div>为臣之节，与世作程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1145996_comment'></div>位逼建牙，秩参掌武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1145996_comment'></div>才实膺时，忠惟得主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1145996_comment'></div>郁此雄图，溘然中露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1145996_comment'></div>谓天盖高，不可以愬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1145996_comment'></div>悲哉俊气，永已荒丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1145996_comment'></div>凤台遗馆，梅岭穷秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1145996_comment'></div>树惟挂剑，地即眠牛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1145996_comment'></div>馀芳不泯，淮水长流。</div><div id='poem_sentence_95_1145996_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年10月</a>　十月，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，与弟徐锴各作一诗以哭乔匡舜。作品：哭刑部侍郎乔公诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《全唐诗》卷七五六。）</span><div id='poem_493757' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493757' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493757?labeling=true' target='_blank'>哭刑部侍郎乔公诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（972年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493757")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_493757_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493757'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493757'>举世重文雅，夫君更质真。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493757'>曾嗟混鸡鹤，终日异缁磷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493757'>词赋离骚客，封章谏诤臣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493757'>襟怀道家侣，标格古时人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493757'>逸老诚云福，遗形未免贫。<div id='poem_sentence_4_493757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_493757'>求文空得草，埋玉遂为尘。<div id='poem_sentence_5_493757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_493757'>静想忘年契，冥思接武晨。<div id='poem_sentence_6_493757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_493757'>连宵洽杯酒，分日掌丝纶。<div id='poem_sentence_7_493757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_493757'>蠹简书陈事，遗孤托世亲。<div id='poem_sentence_8_493757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_493757'>前贤同此叹，非我独沾巾<span class='inlineComment2'>（《徐公文集》卷一六）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_493757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_493757'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_493757_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年10月</a>　十月，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，为乔匡舜作墓志。作品：唐故守尚书刑部侍郎乔公墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一六。）</span><div id='poem_1145995' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145995' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145995?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故朝请大夫守尚书刑部侍郎柱国赐紫金鱼袋乔公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（972年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145995")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145995_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145995'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145995'>士有放怀夷旷，介然中立，外物无累于心，没齿不违于道，吾友乔公尝从事于斯矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145995_comment'></div>公讳匡舜，字亚元，广陵高邮人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145995_comment'></div>曾祖谭、祖泰，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145995_comment'></div>考鸿渐，本县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145995_comment'></div>家世清操，州闾称之，故其子孙必有兴者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145995_comment'></div>公少好学，善属文，弱冠游京都，词藻典丽，容止都雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145995_comment'></div>烈祖辅政，见而器之，补秘书省正字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145995_comment'></div>丞相宋楚公，初获进用，位望日崇，闻公之名，辟置门下，每为文赋诗咏，辄加称赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145995_comment'></div>由是名誉日洽，而卿士大夫皆前席待之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145995_comment'></div>累迁大理评事、司直、监察御史、屯田员外郎，从宋公出藩，为江西、浙西掌书记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145995_comment'></div>府公告老归九华山，公乃升朝，为驾部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145995_comment'></div>未几，守本官知制诰，就迁祠部郎中、中书舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145995_comment'></div>典掌枢机，周慎静默，凡十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145995_comment'></div>值边境俶扰，师出无功，诏旨亲征，中外忧惧，公上疏极谏，坐沮挠军势，黜居临川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145995_comment'></div>顷之，宋公获谴，又以故吏为累，由是累年沉废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145995_comment'></div>今上即位，徵为水部员外郎，改司农少卿，判太常寺，转殿中监，修国史，拜给事中，权知贡举，又兼献纳使，迁刑部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145995_comment'></div>公自徵还，数年间联历清望，盖旧齿直道，上简圣心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145995_comment'></div>至是，以老病不堪朝谒闻，上知其家贫，诏以二卿之秩养疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145995_comment'></div>壬申岁九月二十有三日，卒于京师滨江里官舍，享年七十有五，遗命以《周易》、《孝经》置棺中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145995_comment'></div>太常考行，易名曰贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145995_comment'></div>即以其年冬十月二十有三日，葬于江宁县某所，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145995_comment'></div>夫人太原县君郭氏，代公玄孙、晋陵令喻之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145995_comment'></div>馀庆所备，门风甚高，妇德母仪，闻于宗族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145995_comment'></div>一子僧孺，秘书省正字，早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145995_comment'></div>孙谞，亦为正字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145995_comment'></div>公之为人，宽简真率，常以诗酒自适，不以势利萦心，毁誉谗慝之词闻之晏如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145995_comment'></div>从事楚公府殆二十年，凡为府公见知者皆诡谲倾侧，公独淡然无营，守正不谄，故但以文义知赏，末尝任用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145995_comment'></div>烈祖下诏公卿，举可以亲民者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145995_comment'></div>楚公所荐非其人，烈祖甚不悦，谓给事中常公梦锡曰：「吾望其荐匡舜也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145995_comment'></div>常公及中书侍郎韩公熙载，嫉楚公如雠，而与公善，尝相谓曰：「宋公误识亚元，正可怪也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145995_comment'></div>公之历任，奉法循理，似不能言者，及其临危击节，抗词忤旨，侃侃然有古人之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1145995_comment'></div>黜官夺禄，甘贫守约，凡五年不形于言色，恂恂然道家之流也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1145995_comment'></div>故能享老寿，保康宁，归全委顺，斯可贵矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1145995_comment'></div>公临终数日，舍弟往候之，怡然言曰：「吾往矣，君兄弟可各为一诗哭我」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1145995_comment'></div>翌日，复告门生曰：「吾已得徐君兄弟许我诗，馀无事矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1145995_comment'></div>其忘怀死生也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1145995_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1145995_comment'></div>絮酒之礼，已隔平生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1145995_comment'></div>挂剑之信，永畀穹壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1145995_comment'></div>故以二章为志，閟于九原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1145995_comment'></div>所撰集七十馀卷，编纪之任，属于门人，此不备书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1145995_comment'></div>其诗云：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1145995'>举世重文雅，夫君更质真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1145995_comment'></div>曾嗟混鸡鹤，终自异淄磷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1145995_comment'></div>词赋离骚客，封章谏诤臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1145995_comment'></div>襟怀道家侣，标格古时人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1145995_comment'></div>逸老诚云福，遗形未免贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1145995_comment'></div>求文空得草，埋玉遂为尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1145995_comment'></div>静想忘年契，冥思接武晨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1145995_comment'></div>连宵洽杯酒，分日掌丝纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1145995_comment'></div>蠹简书陈事，遗孤托世亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1145995_comment'></div>前贤同此叹，非我独沾巾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1145995_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1145995'>锴诗云：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1145995'>诸公长者郑当时，事事无心性坦夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1145995_comment'></div>但是登临皆有作，未尝相见不伸眉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1145995_comment'></div>生前适意无过酒，身后遗言只要诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1145995_comment'></div>三日笑谈成理命，一篇投吊尚应知。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1145995_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年</a>　本年，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，有诗寄孟宾于。作品：忆新淦觞池寄孟宾于员外。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42676' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42676' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42676?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忆新淦觞池寄孟宾于员外</a><span class='authorDate'>（972年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42676")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42676_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42676'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42676'>往年淦水驻行轩，引得清流似月圆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42676'>自有溪光还<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_42676", 42676, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>碧甃</span>，不劳人力递金船。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42676'>润滋苔藓欺茵席，声入杉松当管弦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42676'>珍重诗人频管领，莫教尘土咽潺潺。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42676'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42676_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年</a>　约于本年，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，与乔匡舜、高远、潘佑撰成《吴录》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=972&endYear=972')">972年</a>　约于本年，在江宁府为兵部侍郎，拜御史大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=973&endYear=973')">973年1月15日</a>　正月十五日，在江宁府为御史大夫，为道士童处明作张灵官碑记。作品：庐山九天使者庙张灵官记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《全唐文》卷八八三。）</span><div id='poem_1145959' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145959' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145959?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庐山九天使者庙张灵官记</a><span class='authorDate'>（973年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145959")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145959_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145959'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145959'>开元中，尊崇至道，伸严祀典，诏置九天使者庙于匡庐之山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145959_comment'></div>真灵咸秩，率由科教，应门左右，图五百灵官之像焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145959_comment'></div>天祐初，江西连帅南平王钟公遣道士沈太虚设醮于庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145959_comment'></div>太虚醮罢，恍然若梦，见图像一人前揖太虚，曰：「我张怀武也，尝为军将，有微功及物，帝命为灵官」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145959_comment'></div>既寤，访怀武之名，无能知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145959_comment'></div>归以语进士沈彬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145959_comment'></div>彬后二十年游醴陵，邑令陆生客之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145959_comment'></div>方食，有军吏许某后至，话及张怀武，彬因问之，许曰：「怀武者蔡之裨将，某之长吏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145959_comment'></div>顷甲辰岁，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1145959", 1145959, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>大饥</span>，闻豫章独稔，即与一他将各率其属奔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145959_comment'></div>既即路，两军稍不相见，进至武昌，衅隙大构，剋日将决战，禁之不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145959_comment'></div>怀武乃携剑上戍楼，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1145959", 1145959, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>去梯</span>，谓其徒曰：『吾与汝今日之行，非有他图，直救性命耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145959_comment'></div>奈何不忍小忿，而相攻战哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145959_comment'></div>夫战，必强者伤而弱者亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145959_comment'></div>如是，何为去父母之国而死于道路耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145959_comment'></div>凡两军所以致战者，以有怀武故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145959_comment'></div>今我为汝等死，两军为一，无构难矣』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145959_comment'></div>遂自刭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145959_comment'></div>于是士众皆恸哭，乃与和亲，比及豫章，无逃亡者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145959_comment'></div>许某但怀其旧恩，不知灵官之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145959_comment'></div>沈君好道者也，常以此语人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145959_comment'></div>铉始在胶庠，预闻斯论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145959_comment'></div>辛酉岁扈从南幸，获谒祠宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145959_comment'></div>道士童处明出沈君所述传，求润色之，以刊贞石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145959_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145959_comment'></div>古之君子，体至公，综万殊，虚心存诚，事至而应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145959_comment'></div>道茍行矣，何必在己；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145959_comment'></div>物既济焉，何必享利！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145959_comment'></div>故有归全以为孝，杀身以成仁，此两者同出而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1145959", 1145959, "Clauses/86/Comments/0")'>异名</span>，同谓之玄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145959_comment'></div>非清贞之气，不能卫其义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145959_comment'></div>非灵仙之位，不足宁其神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145959_comment'></div>昭报动乎上，肸蚃应乎下，然则天之爱民甚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1145959_comment'></div>咨尔百代，高山仰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1145959_comment'></div>于是岁次癸酉上元日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1145959_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=973&endYear=973')">973年</a>　本年，在江宁府为御史大夫，有诗寄孟宾于。作品：送察院李侍御使庐陵因寄孟员外。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_42642' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42642' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42642?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送察院李侍御使庐陵因寄孟员外</a><span class='authorDate'>（973年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42642")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_42642_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42642'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42642'>绣衣乘驿急如星，山水何妨寄野情。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42642'>肯向九仙台下歇，闲听孟叟醉吟声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42642_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42642'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_42642_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=973&endYear=973')">973年</a>　约于本年，在江宁府为御史大夫，与张洎合力排挤潘佑。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=974&endYear=974')">974年9月24日</a>　九月二十四日，在江宁府为御史大夫，为道士罗自正作重修筠州祈仙观碑记。作品：重修筠州祈仙观记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一〇。）</span><div id='poem_1145936' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145936' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145936?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重修筠州祈仙观记</a><span class='authorDate'>（974年9月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145936")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145936_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145936'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145936'>筠州祈仙观者，东晋黄真君上升之地，因为道馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145936_comment'></div>绵历代祀，互有增修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145936_comment'></div>国朝保大中，元宗皇帝奉为吴让皇再加营构，金石具刻，此不备书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145936_comment'></div>夫言意假象，故立朝修之所；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145936_comment'></div>形器有坏，故资缮完之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145936_comment'></div>此观当荆楚之要津，实邮传之便道，过宾税驾，游子解装，憧憧往来，罕或虚月，必葺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145936_comment'></div>后二纪有馀，闬闳垣墉，颓落且半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145936_comment'></div>道士罗自正，总摄真侣，启焕玄风，以为道由人弘，德以勤继，下饰不美，人其谓何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145936_comment'></div>于是心谋躬行，节用畜力，授其徒之可任者，会其士之好道者，月省岁计，经之营之，即旧谋新，兴废补阙，十有馀岁，其绩大成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145936_comment'></div>凡建圣祖殿、黄真君殿各一区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145936_comment'></div>峙瑶坛，范洪钟，造横桥于通津，植茂树而蔽野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145936_comment'></div>其修旧整坏者，层楼重廊二十馀间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145936_comment'></div>其取材也时，其择匠也良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145936_comment'></div>程之以壮，督之以固，瓴甋碝磩尚其密，藻绘丹雘尚其丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145936_comment'></div>帑廪不费，工庸不劳，焕然新宫，峙此灵境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145936_comment'></div>君子是以知其能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145936_comment'></div>夫神仙之事，史臣不论，岂不以度越常均，非拟议所及故邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145936_comment'></div>仲尼书日食星陨，皆略其微而著其显，虑学者之致惑也，又况于希夷恍惚之际乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145936_comment'></div>然而载籍之间，微旨可得，《书》云「三后在天」，《诗》云「万寿无疆」，斯皆轻举长生之明效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145936_comment'></div>及周、汉而降，则事迹彰灼，耳目不诬，天人交感，民信之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145936_comment'></div>于是通儒洪笔，始著于篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145936_comment'></div>至如许君、黄君，通幽洞冥，穷神极妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145936_comment'></div>逮尔姻族，与夫家人，乘景上隮，超然绝俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145936_comment'></div>故墟旧井，真气裴回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145936_comment'></div>至其乡而思其人，仰其道而践其迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145936_comment'></div>斯观之盛，岂徒然哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145936_comment'></div>铉顷岁扈从南巡，有事于游帷之观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145936_comment'></div>二宫相距，两舍而遥，使指有程，瞻望弗及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145936_comment'></div>逮今一纪，无日忘之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145936_comment'></div>会罗君状其功绩，图其形胜，见托纪述，欣然而书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145936_comment'></div>开宝七年九月二十四日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1145936_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=974&endYear=974')">974年12月12日</a>　十二月十二日，在江宁府为御史大夫，为道士吴宗元作筠州清江县重修三清观碑记。作品：筠州清江县重修三清观记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一〇。）</span><div id='poem_1145937' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145937' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145937?labeling=true' target='_blank'>筠州清江县重修三清观记</a><span class='authorDate'>（974年12月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145937")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145937_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145937'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145937'>元气既判，天地乃位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145937_comment'></div>气之清明灵粹者，钟乎洞天福地、名山大川之间，真圣之所戾也，景福之所兴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145937_comment'></div>然则游居走望，乃建道馆焉，通都大邑，往往而在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145937_comment'></div>豫章之地，寔曰奥区，带豫章之通川，据西山之雄镇，郁映磅礴，神异所栖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145937_comment'></div>高真十二，震耀方夏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145937_comment'></div>万灵轨辙，靡迤蝉联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145937_comment'></div>保大庚戌岁，诏复高安县为筠州，析其北鄙为清江县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145937_comment'></div>而三清观负新邑之左，瞰长江之滨，形胜高奇，坛宇严净。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145937_comment'></div>闻诸故老云：昔吴、许二君尝游兹地，夜观青气上属于天，相与叹曰：「此非凡地，当为神仙之宅」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145937_comment'></div>及二君登晨之后，邑人追感前言，共构茅茨，岁时荐献，众目为草堂道院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145937_comment'></div>函关紫气，事往名存；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145937_comment'></div>盩屋草楼，人非郭是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145937_comment'></div>年世弥远，增修益崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145937_comment'></div>开成中始诏赐号三清之观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145937_comment'></div>自时厥后，又踰十纪，运逢治乱，道有污隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145937_comment'></div>中兴已还，百度咸复，官得其守，人尽其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145937_comment'></div>道士吴宗元，允迪玄风，克堪道任，以为朝礼之域，飙歘所临，不饰不美，众将安仰？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145937_comment'></div>于是月考岁计，庀工饬材，补废扶倾，无所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145937_comment'></div>建三清之殿，造虚皇之台，设待宾之区，敞饭贤之室，范华钟之铿訇，构层楼之苕亭，回廊复道，重深奥秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145937_comment'></div>于是饰仪卫，备器用，肃然必洽，焕焉可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145937_comment'></div>夫其诚至者，其礼修；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145937_comment'></div>其守固者，其事举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145937_comment'></div>道不远矣，人焉廋哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145937_comment'></div>宗元又以云境昭回，祥符肸蚃，思刻贞石，以贻后人，不远千里，见访论撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145937_comment'></div>嘉尚其志，故为直书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145937_comment'></div>时甲戌开宝七年十二月十二日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1145937_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=974&endYear=974')">974年</a>　本年，在江宁府为御史大夫，奉命修《元宗实录》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=974&endYear=974')">974年</a>　约于本年，在江宁府为御史大夫，改吏部尚书、知制诰、修文馆学士承旨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=975&endYear=975')">975年9月</a>　九月，在江宁府为吏部尚书，自请使宋。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b448ed16efc2425fa7b9ee53d4e63a47_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b448ed16efc2425fa7b9ee53d4e63a47");'><span id='b448ed16efc2425fa7b9ee53d4e63a47_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=975&endYear=975')">975年</a>，60岁</div><div id='b448ed16efc2425fa7b9ee53d4e63a47' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>十月，以使宋不副命，辞右仆射，转官左内史侍郎，同参左右内史事。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>十月，在江宁府为左内史侍郎，弟徐锴忧惧而卒。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ea9efd5d86a34038b5a629c0b4b19f75_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ea9efd5d86a34038b5a629c0b4b19f75");'><span id='ea9efd5d86a34038b5a629c0b4b19f75_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=975&endYear=975')">975年</a>，60岁</div><div id='ea9efd5d86a34038b5a629c0b4b19f75' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=975&endYear=975')">975年11月27日</a>　十一月二十七日，在江宁府为左内史侍郎，金陵城破，随李煜出降。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南昌（新建）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fefd15f0b0de41de9ed698d283d5d701_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fefd15f0b0de41de9ed698d283d5d701");'><span id='fefd15f0b0de41de9ed698d283d5d701_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=960&endYear=960')">960年</a>，45岁</div><div id='fefd15f0b0de41de9ed698d283d5d701' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=960&endYear=960')">960年</a>　本年，将父徐延休灵柩迁葬于洪州西山之鸾冈。<br /></div>
