-----title
贵池
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='164a6959e94a450699aff253046ac3eb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("164a6959e94a450699aff253046ac3eb");'><span id='164a6959e94a450699aff253046ac3eb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年</a>，46岁</div><div id='164a6959e94a450699aff253046ac3eb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年2月</a>　二月，扈驾往南昌，途经池州，应陈德成之请作重建池州紫极宫碑记。作品：池州重建紫极宫碑铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一二。）</span><div id='poem_1145983' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145983' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145983?labeling=true' target='_blank'>池州重建紫极宫碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（961年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145983")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145983_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145983'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145983'>域中之大曰道，百行之先曰孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145983_comment'></div>故孝心充乎内，必道气应乎外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145983_comment'></div>于是有聿修之德，追远之怀，扬名显亲之善，集灵徼福之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145983_comment'></div>用于邦国则臣节著，施于家庭则子道光，以之为政则民从乂，以之荐信则神降福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145983_comment'></div>然则坛馆之作，焉得已乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145983_comment'></div>池州紫极宫者，本东晋之普明观也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145983_comment'></div>浸之以秋浦，镇之以齐山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145983_comment'></div>北望陵阳，窦真人飞升之所；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145983_comment'></div>南瞻九子，费徵君栖隐之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145983_comment'></div>玄风徘徊，精气交感，代有奇士，居为殊庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145983_comment'></div>既奉玄元之御，因崇紫极之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145983_comment'></div>治乱迭运，隆替不常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145983_comment'></div>戊午岁，太守陈公始临此郡，历垝垣而叹息，岁遗址而顾瞻，役不徒兴，义将有属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145983_comment'></div>公妫水洪派，太丘旧族，重世避地，徙居建安，祖德门风，冠映图牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145983_comment'></div>王师拓境，闽方即叙，抚纳归附，旌访贤能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145983_comment'></div>惟我严君，首奋奇节，芟夷逋秽，弘济艰难，偏师所指，无往弗克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145983_comment'></div>故十年之间，由裨将历郡守，登上公，建齐坛，功名之盛，近古无匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145983_comment'></div>及王室多故，边城不宁，复遣公督舟师，率诸将万里赴援，三年转战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145983_comment'></div>算无遗策，兵不顿锋，威行军中，勋在王府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145983_comment'></div>舍爵再命，聿来是邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145983_comment'></div>于是解甲释兵，颁条布政，事从中兴，民用接和，会文赋诗，彬彬然有儒者之风矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145983_comment'></div>俄而王妣国太夫人凶问至，公孺慕出次，烝烝永怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145983_comment'></div>以为柔仪慈训，实大吾族；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145983_comment'></div>鞠育仁爱，兼倍诸孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145983_comment'></div>尝药弗亲，执绋且违，欲报之恩，王事靡盬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145983_comment'></div>思所以荐祉于冥莫，求神于希夷，非龟山之宫，必易迁之馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145983_comment'></div>然则琳房金阙，瑶坛桧井，迎列真之御，资阆风之游，仙经不诬，胜事可作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145983_comment'></div>于是瞻星揆日，饬用庀徒，散庑下之金，出荆门之绢，人百其力，工荐其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145983_comment'></div>易其倾颓，化以壮丽，成于心匠，不愆素期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145983_comment'></div>自某年月鸠工，至某年月讫事，凡出钱若干万，筑室若干间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145983_comment'></div>正殿当阳，三尊负扆，享列宿之位于东序，设三官之堂于西厢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1145983_comment'></div>严馈奠之室于艮维，所以尽时思之礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1145983_comment'></div>敞闲宴之亭于乾位，所以极坐忘之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1145983_comment'></div>矢棘雉飞，霞驳云蔚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1145983_comment'></div>琁题行月，焕城邑之晶光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1145983_comment'></div>飞甍白日，壮江山之气色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1145983_comment'></div>如是则飙歘之驾，不得不临；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1145983_comment'></div>肸蚃之福，不得不集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1145983_comment'></div>想见武夷之会，足申令伯之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1145983_comment'></div>至矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1145983_comment'></div>善庆孙谋，无得称已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1145983_comment'></div>尝试论之曰：神仙者，君子之所归也，故《真诰》云：至孝至贞之人，皆先受灵职，次为列仙，岁登降其幽明，如人间之考绩矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1145983_comment'></div>若乃尽忠于君，纯孝于亲，敷惠于民，归诚于仙，而不得与夫饵芝术、醮星斗者同隮真阶，吾不信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1145983_comment'></div>勖哉夫子，其惟有终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1145983_comment'></div>铉扈驾南巡，致礼名岳，假道过此，仰瞻久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1145983_comment'></div>博我以文，辄不逊让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1145983_comment'></div>其铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1145983'>我经池阳，池阳既康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1145983_comment'></div>化以至道，民知向方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1145983_comment'></div>乃新闲馆，以奉虚皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1145983_comment'></div>君子荐祉，则惟其臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1145983_comment'></div>我登新宫，新宫既崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1145983_comment'></div>深严耽耽，丹彩彤彤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1145983_comment'></div>九华散影，十绝盘空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1145983_comment'></div>若在宣岳，如游阆风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1145983_comment'></div>至道不烦，玄关甚迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1145983_comment'></div>孝享诚敬，奉时祖妣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1145983_comment'></div>善庆纯嘏，施于孙子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1145983_comment'></div>三茅二许，夫何远已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1145983_comment'></div>流芳金石，永永千祀<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1145983_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_1145983'>援：原脱，黄校本作「敌」，《全唐文》、李刊本作「援」，据补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_59_1145983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1145983'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_58_1145983_0'>⑴ 《徐公文集》卷一二。又见《全唐文》卷八八四。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1145983_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年7月</a>　七月，护李璟丧归金陵。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='08d9650622414958bcb951da54e07605_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("08d9650622414958bcb951da54e07605");'><span id='08d9650622414958bcb951da54e07605_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年</a>，46岁</div><div id='08d9650622414958bcb951da54e07605' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年11月</a>　十一月，出使南汉途中，过南昌，有诗送刘令言。作品：南都遇前嘉鱼刘令言游闵岭作此送之。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_42792' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42792' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42792?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南都遇前嘉鱼刘令言游闽岭作此与之</a><span class='authorDate'>（961年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span -----title
青阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='80221735f7fe4d2d8e2bbd55d80e0320_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("80221735f7fe4d2d8e2bbd55d80e0320");'><span id='80221735f7fe4d2d8e2bbd55d80e0320_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年</a>，46岁</div><div id='80221735f7fe4d2d8e2bbd55d80e0320' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年11月</a>　十一月，出使南汉途中，过九华山，有诗赠人。作品：奉使九华山途中遇青阳薛郎中。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_42771' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42771' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42771?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉使九华山中途遇青阳薛郎中</a><span class='authorDate'>（961年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42771")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_42771_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42771'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42771'>故人相别动相思，此地相逢岂素期。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42771'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_42771", 42771, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>九子</span>峰前闲未得，五溪桥上坐多时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42771'>甘泉从幸余知忝，宣室徵还子未迟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_42771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_42771'>且饮一杯消别恨，野花风起渐离披。<div id='poem_sentence_3_42771_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_42771'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_42771_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
彭泽
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e43093f404364c4d9f6a18f50f21fe64_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e43093f404364c4d9f6a18f50f21fe64");'><span id='e43093f404364c4d9f6a18f50f21fe64_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年</a>，46岁</div><div id='e43093f404364c4d9f6a18f50f21fe64' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年11月</a>　十一月，出使南汉途中，过彭泽，有诗。作品：奉命南使经彭泽。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_42597' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_42597' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/42597?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉命南使经彭泽<span class='inlineComment2'>（值王明府不在，留此。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（961年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_42597")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_42597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_42597'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_42597'>远使程途未一分，离心常要醉醺醺。<div id='poem_sentence_0_42597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_42597'>那堪彭泽门前立，黄菊萧疏不见君。<div id='poem_sentence_1_42597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_42597'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_42597_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
丰城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='24c65fd3b1954562ba2d94d3fabd3123_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("24c65fd3b1954562ba2d94d3fabd3123");'><span id='24c65fd3b1954562ba2d94d3fabd3123_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年</a>，46岁</div><div id='24c65fd3b1954562ba2d94d3fabd3123' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年11月</a>　十一月，出使南汉途中，过丰城，作《剑池颂》作品：剑池颂并序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_1145966' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145966' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145966?labeling=true' target='_blank'>剑池颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（961年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145966")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145966_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145966'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145966'>岁次辛酉，月躔仲冬，王人徐铉扬旌铜柱之乡，税驾剑池之庙，嘅叹灵迹，徘徊故墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145966_comment'></div>或曰：「龙泉、太阿，安得为宝？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145966_comment'></div>出也不为当世之用，佩之不免亡身之灾，天下固有虚名而无实效者欤」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145966_comment'></div>愚以为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145966_comment'></div>夫圣人之于天下，亦物耳，所禀受者异，故能与造物者并，而为天下王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145966_comment'></div>是以圣人之作也，天不爱其道，地不爱其宝，同声相应，同气相求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145966_comment'></div>人谋鬼谋，皆为圣人用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145966_comment'></div>无功无迹，岂寻常所能识乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145966_comment'></div>然则集阴阳之英，萃山泽之精，穷炉冶之妙，极锋铓之利，宜其冥合玄造，弼成圣功者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145966_comment'></div>昔黄帝法月满而铸镜，用能照烛怪魅，辟除不祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145966_comment'></div>大禹收贡金以铸鼎，使民知神奸，以远不若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145966_comment'></div>汉高祖佩斩蛇之剑，以拨乱除害，奄有天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145966_comment'></div>是以三者皆人力所为也，咸能辅佐兴运，与时隐见，其可诬乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145966_comment'></div>在昔三分叔世，咸有昏德，天命将改，寰宇将同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145966_comment'></div>斯剑知之，故灵发于下，气浮于上，应帝王之符命，瞩识者之观瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145966_comment'></div>亦犹伊尹负鼎于莘墟，仲尼动色于鲁相，千载一会，圣贤所以汲汲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145966_comment'></div>向使晋武能诞若天意，克明俊德，判忠邪之路，绌骄侈之心，则贤能尽其才，神灵效其用，淳耀之烈可续，七百之期不爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145966_comment'></div>而王猷既郁，乱本既成，百姓失望，群龙沮色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145966_comment'></div>于是斯剑也，委质张、雷之鉴，一泄其愤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145966_comment'></div>远迹刘、石之丑，复归于潜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145966_comment'></div>其出也，所以示神之不亡，其去也，所以示唯德是辅，则其为用也远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145966_comment'></div>昔者周过其数，秦不及期，是知天命之精微，可以人事而延促，前哲论之备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145966_comment'></div>若夫精真之诚修于内，感召之致应乎外，自然而然，有道存焉，不可以智求，不可以言达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145966_comment'></div>王者得之，则三五之功，其馀事耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145966_comment'></div>然则天下至宝，本非人臣所服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145966_comment'></div>变化无方，神物之事也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145966_comment'></div>忘身徇国，忠臣之节也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145966_comment'></div>两造其极，求仁得仁，复何怨乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145966_comment'></div>庙在丰城故县，俯瞰池岸，壮武侯雷府君之象祀焉，去今县四十里；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145966_comment'></div>而龙泉、太阿之庙别在中路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145966_comment'></div>栋宇绵久，皆将倾颓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1145966_comment'></div>邑人朱恽等，洽重熙之化，感百世之祀，奖率同志，唯新寿宫，千载光灵，焕然如在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1145966_comment'></div>县令孟宾于、尉孙举，皆以文行之懿，中贤良之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1145966_comment'></div>接武连事，惠此王畿，推诚于民，荐信于神，风雨不愆，耕凿咸若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1145966_comment'></div>先贤遗躅，其不泯也宜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1145966_comment'></div>是池广不终亩，深才数尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1145966_comment'></div>父老云：「近岁旦暮，往往有云雾蒙覆其中，惚恍之理，不可测已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1145966_comment'></div>今中兴三叶，圣政惟新，岂非灵命孔昭，玄贶将集？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1145966_comment'></div>天命不憯，弘之在人，使臣司言，敢告有位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1145966_comment'></div>乃为颂曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1145966'>周室既衰，仁兽来臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1145966_comment'></div>晋祚不融，龙剑效珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1145966_comment'></div>神化无方，天命无亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1145966_comment'></div>德之不建，与运俱沦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1145966_comment'></div>归潜厚载，以俟真人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1145966_comment'></div>惟剑之神，惟贤之识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1145966_comment'></div>湛湛灵沼，绵绵庙食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1145966_comment'></div>瑞气长在，玄符靡测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1145966_comment'></div>垂兹颂声，永永无极。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1145966_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
新干（新淦）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0f14e9e25f8842839f687519907ab106_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0f14e9e25f8842839f687519907ab106");'><span id='0f14e9e25f8842839f687519907ab106_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=961&endYear=961')">961年</a>，46岁</div><div id='0f14e9e25f8842839f687519907ab106' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; -----title
南康
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a725132b286d48f0800cc8ba0a539a3b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a725132b286d48f0800cc8ba0a539a3b");'><span id='a725132b286d48f0800cc8ba0a539a3b_link' id='poem_title_493651' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493651?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和陈处士在雍丘见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（976年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493651")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493651_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493651'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493651'>衰薄喜多幸，退公谁与闲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493651'>高人乘兴去，相望两程间。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493651'>卷箔有微雪，登楼无远山。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493651'>清谈胜题赠，何日杖藜还。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493651'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493651_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=976&endYear=976')">976年11月</a>　十一月，在开封府为太子率更令，与汤悦并直学士院，结识李昉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=976&endYear=976')">976年</a>　本年，在开封府为太子率更令，奉诏撰李汉超德政碑。作品：大宋推诚宣力翊戴功臣金紫光禄大夫检校司徒使持节齐州诸军事齐州刺史充本州岛防御使河堤等使关南兵马都监兼御史大夫上柱国陇西郡开国侯食邑一千九百户李公德政碑文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1146009' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146009' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146009?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋推诚宣力翊戴功臣金紫光禄大夫检校司徒使持节齐州诸军事齐州刺史充本州防御使河堤等使关南兵马都监兼御史大夫上柱国陇西郡开国侯食邑一千九百户李公德政碑文</a><span class='authorDate'>（976年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146009")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146009_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146009'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146009'>臣闻四岳畴咨，帝尧所以光宅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146009_comment'></div>三良共理，汉室于是隆兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146009_comment'></div>然则运历冥符，风云交感，必有则哲之后，乃有称职之臣，用能远肃迩安，刑清俗富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146009_comment'></div>其或久于其道，课最于时，行边按部籍其能，群吏万民浸其泽，流芳金石，旧典存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146009_comment'></div>公名汉超，其先陇西人，因官移籍，今为云中人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146009_comment'></div>柱下史之真源，克昌厥后；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146009_comment'></div>前将军之壮气，不陨其声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146009_comment'></div>世有哲人，多为名将，备诸前载，可以不书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146009_comment'></div>昔者同光之季，庄宗失驭，公烈考讳霸德，实典亲卫，力扈乘舆，奋不顾身，有死无二，忠显于国，庆钟于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146009_comment'></div>及公之贵，昭赠左监门卫将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146009_comment'></div>夫人石氏，追封本县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146009_comment'></div>道不虚行，没而可作，有后之报，斯焉岂诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146009_comment'></div>公方幼而孤，嶷然特立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146009_comment'></div>英果之气，出于天资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146009_comment'></div>远大之期，志为时用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146009_comment'></div>年未弱冠，自奋从军，始负羽于魏侯，复策名于郓帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146009_comment'></div>有周受命，选入禁军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146009_comment'></div>夫忘归之镞，非逢蒙无以宣其利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146009_comment'></div>绝影之骏，非造父无以骋其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146009_comment'></div>今上当历试之辰，受有征之任，妙选比校，公首预焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146009_comment'></div>上党之役，名书勋籍，奏发硎之刃，超渐陆之程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146009_comment'></div>及眷命有归，飞天在运，攀鳞之效，舍爵攸先，乃掌句陈，式严徼道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146009_comment'></div>恩威洽著而七萃知方，夙夜惟寅而九重甘寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146009_comment'></div>期岁考绩，较然可称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146009_comment'></div>皇上以文武之任，中外惟一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146009_comment'></div>有和众之略，必著抚俗之能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146009_comment'></div>有卫社之勤，必堪守土之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146009_comment'></div>越建隆二年，拜齐州刺史、本州防御使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146009_comment'></div>尔乃海岱封圻，虚危躔次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146009_comment'></div>历下屯兵之地，夙表要冲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146009_comment'></div>东陵聚众之乡，素称暴桀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1146009_comment'></div>公本以简易，济之强明，恕己以兼容，正身而可象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1146009_comment'></div>先之以孝悌，故其民和，则争讼息而囹圄虚矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1146009_comment'></div>示之以诚明，故其民信，则赋役充而储廪实矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1146009_comment'></div>农时不夺，故旷土辟而生殖滋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1146009_comment'></div>关市无征，故百货通而财用足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1146009_comment'></div>于是举废典，正国容，树门反坫以备制度，高闳厚垣以待客使，蒸肴折俎以宴嘉宾，椎牛酾酒以享军旅，出于私积，无以家为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1146009_comment'></div>近悦而远怀，家至而户到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1146009_comment'></div>一年而宿弊革，载稔而新政行，郡斋肃然，清啸而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1146009_comment'></div>由是知董戎之用，可移之于颁条；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1146009_comment'></div>露冕之风，可推之于护塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1146009_comment'></div>乾德二年，诏公以本官充关南兵马都监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1146009_comment'></div>幽都南际，河间北壤，守方之要，慎简为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1146009_comment'></div>至则远斥堠，审号令，养士如子，戢军无私，威声飙驰，亭障山立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1146009_comment'></div>绝窥边之虏，有狎野之农，而郡之大事，亦皆听命，千里之内，若指掌焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1146009_comment'></div>二职交修，七载如一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1146009_comment'></div>开宝二年，召赴京师，天言褒慰，复遣还郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1146009_comment'></div>而戍士思慕，氓俗繄凭，故其年冬，再为关南监护。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1146009_comment'></div>公负倜傥之气，蕴沈厚之谋，民已安而政益修，边既宁而备愈谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1146009_comment'></div>绩茂而不伐，宠至而若惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1146009_comment'></div>君子知福禄之攸归，郡人感惠泽而思报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1146009_comment'></div>于是僚吏之属，耆艾之徒，相与上言，愿旌不朽，且曰：「任贤使能，天子之明也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1146009_comment'></div>计功称伐，先王之典也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1146009_comment'></div>非有理世，孰扬颂声」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1146009_comment'></div>优诏嘉之，克遂其请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1146009_comment'></div>昔者考父「循墙」之颂，非曰君恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1146009_comment'></div>当阳「沉水」之文，真成自伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1146009_comment'></div>岂舆情欣洽，令誉升闻，播乐石于无穷，等高山而可仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1146009_comment'></div>永惟懿美，足焕文明，爰命下臣，勒铭纪实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1146009_comment'></div>其辞曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_1146009'>茫茫禹迹，画为万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1146009_comment'></div>建侯定守，立民之极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1146009_comment'></div>提封且千，属城以百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1146009_comment'></div>惟威惟怀，有典有则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1146009_comment'></div>威怀伊何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1146009_comment'></div>君子时中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1146009_comment'></div>典则伊何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1146009_comment'></div>二代同风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1146009_comment'></div>以使则悦，以令则从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1146009_comment'></div>率是古道，兹惟李公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1146009_comment'></div>济水之南，东陵之下，伏生荒耄，盗蹠狙诈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1146009_comment'></div>嗟我蒸黎，孰闻道化，至鲁犹远，尊周靡暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1146009_comment'></div>李公来思，富之教之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1146009_comment'></div>政先体要，物必由仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1146009_comment'></div>夜犬无挠，晨羊不欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1146009_comment'></div>归民影附，末俗风移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1146009_comment'></div>天下虽平，四方是守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1146009_comment'></div>桓桓虎旅，慑尔戎丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1146009_comment'></div>籍我兼资，是率是纠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1146009_comment'></div>道合舞干，威行戴斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1146009_comment'></div>郡政既成，边尘既清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1146009_comment'></div>俾比屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1146009_comment'></div>肃肃连营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1146009_comment'></div>夫怀其惠，人竭其诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1146009_comment'></div>欲报之恩，思垂颂声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1146009_comment'></div>明明大君，知臣善使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1146009_comment'></div>举必至公，义无虚美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1146009_comment'></div>用建隆碣，永昭信史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1146009_comment'></div>锡尔介福，施于孙子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1146009_comment'></div>晋称岘首，汉纪燕然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1146009_comment'></div>风流不续，寥落千年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1146009_comment'></div>猗欤良牧，无愧前贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1146009_comment'></div>高深自改，兰菊常传。</div><div id='poem_sentence_91_1146009_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=976&endYear=976')">976年</a>　约于本年秋，在开封府为太子率更令，有诗和李昉。作品：和翰长闻西枢副翰邻居夜宴。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493660' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493660' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493660?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和翰长闻西枢副翰邻居夜宴</a><span class='authorDate'>（976年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493660")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493660_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493660'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493660'>开筵别有邻居兴，卜夜应怜禁漏长。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493660'>旧友不期争命驾，新姬凭宠剩传觞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493660'>香烟结雾笼金鸭，烛焰成花照杏梁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493660'>京邑衣冠多胜赏，鲈鱼争敢道思乡。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493660'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493660_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=976&endYear=976')">976年</a>　约于本年冬，在开封府为太子率更令，有诗送汤悦之陈州。作品：送汤舍人之陈州。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493652' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493652' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493652?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送汤舍人之陈州</a><span class='authorDate'>（976年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493652")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493652_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493652'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493652'>尼父恓惶地，离情向此偏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493652'>家贫聊复尔，道在肯徒然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493652'>诗景明松雪，乡山隔水烟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493652'>三年须赴召，莫恋瓮头眠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493652'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493652_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=976&endYear=976')">976年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为太子率更令，为李承鼐庙作碑记。作品：洪州丰城县李司空庙碑文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1146023' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146023' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146023?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洪州丰城县李司空庙碑文</a><span class='authorDate'>（976年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146023")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146023_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146023'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146023'>先王之制，以劳定国，以死勤事，皆得祀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146023_comment'></div>然则非通幽洞灵之士，有惊愚显俗之迹，亦不能臻此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146023_comment'></div>李君讳承鼐，字大用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146023_comment'></div>其先陇西人，中叶因官，遂家上党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146023_comment'></div>先君讳神福，避乱择主，来适维扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146023_comment'></div>于时唐室崩离，诸侯角逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146023_comment'></div>吴武王奋桓、文之举，我先君效关、张之用，摧凶略地，所向无前，功加于时，庆钟于后，终淮南节度副使、鄂岳招讨使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146023_comment'></div>君即招讨长子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146023_comment'></div>幼而爽俊，长而雄勇，年始志学，即从义旗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146023_comment'></div>善抚士卒，生知韬略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146023_comment'></div>厉若鹰隼，疾如风电。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146023_comment'></div>时称虎子，敌畏马儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146023_comment'></div>以功累加检校左仆射，为横冲裨将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146023_comment'></div>天祐丙寅岁，从招讨使秦裴平豫章，叙功为最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146023_comment'></div>新附之地，属郡未宾，明年，命君领偏师平馀盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146023_comment'></div>戈船先进，群帅后期，山越雾集，汉矢且尽，同玄冥之没，若杜畿之沉，享年二十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146023_comment'></div>诸将嗣事，逋秽克清，迎君之丧，窆于洪州丰城县杨子洲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146023_comment'></div>惟君夙龄挺秀，尽忠死节，识与不识，杂然推奇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146023_comment'></div>而英灵肸蚃，若在左右，如郑人之惊伯有，类吴俗之畏子文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146023_comment'></div>于是耆艾相率，启求立祠于墓侧，公议佥允，因赠司空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146023_comment'></div>水旱祷祈，无不即应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146023_comment'></div>乡邑之际，频岁丰穰，湍濑无虞，疾疠不作，而君之家门亦康宁蕃衍焉，及今七十年矣，虽神道恍惚，不可备论，而忠诚报应，良足为劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146023_comment'></div>犹恐年世绵邈，流俗失传，或见猱于越巫，将受讥于淫祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146023_comment'></div>嫡孙仁昭，愿以事实，勒于贞珉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146023_comment'></div>铉素与君诸子游，复连姻戚，披文相质，所不获辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146023_comment'></div>初，君之长弟讳承鼎，为吴王之爱婿，故国人咸谓君为伯氏，而忘其官称焉，今用明白之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146023_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1146023'>呜呼李君，勇且有仁，生徇国难，没为明神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146023_comment'></div>南楚之郊，章江之滨，祠堂奕奕，像设侁侁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146023_comment'></div>荐信以时，降祐于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146023_comment'></div>龙泉太阿，校灵比珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146023_comment'></div>冲斗之气，终天不沦。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1146023_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=977&endYear=977')">977年</a>　春，在开封府为太子率更令，有诗和钱弘仪。作品：和金州钱太保春雨。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493665' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493665' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493665?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和金州钱太保春雨</a><span class='authorDate'>（977年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493665")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493665_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493665'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493665'>濛濛膏雨远空迷，点滴圆纹水绕堤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493665'>柳带喜如和醉舞，花房愁似宿妆啼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493665'>烟笼麦陇连天阔，云映渔舟掠岸低。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493665'>廉使解分天子念，一篇骚雅慰蒸黎。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493665'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493665_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=977&endYear=977')">977年3月17日</a>　三月十七日，在开封府为太子率更令，奉诏与修《太平御览》、《太平广记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=977&endYear=977')">977年</a>　本年，在开封府为太子率更令，与修《太平广记》时，将己作《稽神录》采入。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=977&endYear=977')">977年</a>　约于本年上元夜，在开封府为太子率更令，有诗和钱昱。作品：和白州钱使君上元夜侍宴。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493663' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493663' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493663?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和白州钱使君上元夜侍宴</a><span class='authorDate'>（977年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493663")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493663_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493663'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493663'>御宴宵陈敞百层，君恩芳景两难胜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493663'>风传天上九成乐，月映楼前万树灯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493663'>醉捧玉觞疑梦寐，静临丹槛似飞腾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493663'>因观谢守窗中咏，自愧瀛洲是滥登。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493663'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493663_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=977&endYear=977')">977年</a>　约于本年春，在开封府为太子率更令，有诗送人外任州官。作品：送容州程员外端州吴员外。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493654' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493654' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493654?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送容州程员外端州吴员外</a><span class='authorDate'>（977年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493654")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_493654_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493654'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493654'>士生秉道义，公论重才名。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493654'>美哉双白璧，高价等连城。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493654'>昔在南国时，折桂尝抗衡。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493654'>今为北朝客，通籍齐振缨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493654'>连镳适炎徼，并命典州兵。<div id='poem_sentence_4_493654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_493654'>地远乃寄重，无为惮遐征。<div id='poem_sentence_5_493654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_493654'>俗杂则财难，当在通其情。<div id='poem_sentence_6_493654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_493654'>投香与还珠，前哲有遗声。<div id='poem_sentence_7_493654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_493654'>君看奏谏者，接武趋承明。<div id='poem_sentence_8_493654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_493654'>掺袂赠斯言，斯言勿见轻。<div id='poem_sentence_9_493654_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_493654'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_493654_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=977&endYear=977')">977年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为太子率更令，有诗送人还宣州。作品：送宣州张员外。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493668' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493668' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493668?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送宣州张员外</a><span class='authorDate'>（977年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493668")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493668_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493668'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493668'>故国干戈后，怜君得意归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493668'>绮霞横郡阁，犀烛照渔矶。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493668'>天迥青山远，江平白鸟飞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493668'>此行同衣锦，况是老莱衣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493668'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493668_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=977&endYear=977')">977年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为太子率更令，有诗送周惟简。作品：送周郎中还司。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_493707' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493707' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493707?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送周郎中还司</a><span class='authorDate'>（977年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493707")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493707_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493707'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493707'>忆在庐山始识君，当时惟拟共眠云。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493707'>那知身计关前定，却向人间逐世纷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493707'>紫阁峰前欣独往，银台门里叹离群。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493707'>青囊旧有登真诀，莫遣閒人取次闻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493707_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493707'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493707_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年1月24日</a>　正月二十四日，在开封府为太子率更令，奉诏与汤悦、王克贞、张洎撰《江南录》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年3月</a>　三月，在开封府为太子率更令，诏赐天下无名佛寺寺额，为篆书“太平兴国之寺”六字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年7月</a>　七月，在开封府为太子率更令，奉旨探访李煜，启牵机药之祸。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年8月13日</a>　八月十三日，在开封府为太子率更令，与修之《太平广记》书成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年10月</a>　十月，在开封府为太子率更令，奉诏为李煜作墓志铭。作品：大宋左千牛卫上将军追封吴王陇西公墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1146025' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146025' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146025?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋左千牛卫上将军追封吴王陇西公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（978年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146025")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146025_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146025'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146025'>盛德百世，善继者所以主其祀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146025_comment'></div>圣人无外，善守者不能固其存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146025_comment'></div>盖运历之所推，亦古今之一贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146025_comment'></div>其有享蕃锡之宠，保克终之美，殊恩饰壤，懿范流光，传之金石，斯不诬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146025_comment'></div>王讳煜，字重光，陇西人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146025_comment'></div>昔庭坚赞九德，伯阳恢至道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146025_comment'></div>皇天眷祐，锡祚于唐，祖文宗武，世有显德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146025_comment'></div>载祀三百，龟玉沦胥，宗子维城，蕃衍万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146025_comment'></div>江淮之地，独奉长安，故我显祖，用膺推戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146025_comment'></div>淳耀之烈，载光旧吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146025_comment'></div>二世承基，克广其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146025_comment'></div>皇宋将启，玄贶冥符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146025_comment'></div>有周开先，太祖历试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146025_comment'></div>威德所及，寰宇将同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146025_comment'></div>故我旧邦，祗畏天命，贬大号以禀朔，献地图而请吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146025_comment'></div>故得义动元后，风行域中，恩礼有加，绥怀不世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146025_comment'></div>鲁用天王之礼，自越常钧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146025_comment'></div>酅存纪侯之国，曾何足贵？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146025_comment'></div>王以世嫡嗣服，以古道驭民，钦若彝伦，率循先志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146025_comment'></div>奉蒸尝、恭色养必以孝，宾大臣、事耇老必以礼，居处服御必以节，言动施舍必以时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146025_comment'></div>至于荷全济之恩，谨藩国之度，勤修九贡，府无虚月，祗奉百役，知无不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146025_comment'></div>十五年间，天眷弥渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146025_comment'></div>然而果于自信，怠于周防，西邻起衅，南箕构祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146025_comment'></div>投杼致慈亲之惑，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1146025", 1146025, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>乞火</span>无里妇之辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146025_comment'></div>始劳因垒之师，终后涂山之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146025_comment'></div>太祖至仁之举，大赉为怀，录勤王之前效，恢焚谤之广度，位以上将，爵为通侯，待遇如初，宠锡斯厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146025_comment'></div>今上宣猷大麓，敷惠万方，每侍论思，常存开释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146025_comment'></div>及飞天在运，丽泽推恩，擢进上公之封，仍加掌武之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146025_comment'></div>侍从亲礼，勉谕优容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146025_comment'></div>方将度越等彝，登崇名数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146025_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1146025_comment'></div>阅川无舍，景命不融，太平兴国三年秋七月八日遘疾，薨于京师里第，享年四十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1146025_comment'></div>皇上抚几兴悼，投瓜轸悲，痛生之不逮，俾殁而加饰，特诏辍朝三日，赠太师，追封吴王，命中使涖葬，凡丧祭所须，皆从官给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1146025_comment'></div>即其年冬十月日，葬于河南府某县某乡某里，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1146025_comment'></div>夫人郑国夫人周氏，勋旧之族，是生邦媛，肃雍之美，流咏国风，才实女师，言成阃则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1146025_comment'></div>子左千牛卫大将军某，襟神俊茂，识度淹通，孝悌自表于天资，才略靡由于师训，日出之学，未易可量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1146025_comment'></div>惟王天骨秀异，神气清粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1146025_comment'></div>言动有则，容止可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1146025_comment'></div>精究六经，旁综百氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1146025_comment'></div>常以为周、孔之道不可暂离，经国化民，发号施令，造次于是，终始不渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1146025_comment'></div>酷好文辞，多所述作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1146025_comment'></div>一游一豫，必颂宣尼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1146025_comment'></div>载笑载言，不忘经义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1146025_comment'></div>洞晓音律，精别雅郑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1146025_comment'></div>穷先王制作之意，审风俗淳薄之原，为文论之，以续《乐记》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1146025_comment'></div>所著文集三十卷，杂说百篇，味其文知其道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1146025_comment'></div>至于弧矢之善，笔札之工，天纵多能，必造精绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1146025_comment'></div>本以恻隐之性，仍好竺乾之教，草木不杀，禽鱼咸遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1146025_comment'></div>赏人之善，常若不及；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1146025_comment'></div>掩人之过，惟恐其闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1146025_comment'></div>以至法不胜奸，威不克爱，以厌兵之俗，当用武之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1146025_comment'></div>孔明罕应变之略，不成近功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1146025_comment'></div>偃王躬仁义之行，终于亡国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1146025_comment'></div>道有所在，复何愧欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1146025_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1146025_comment'></div>二室南峙，三川东注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1146025_comment'></div>瞻上阳之宫阙，望北邙之灵树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1146025_comment'></div>旁寂寂兮迥野，下冥冥兮长暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1146025_comment'></div>寄不朽于金石，庶有传于竹素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1146025_comment'></div>其铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_1146025'>天鉴九德，锡我唐祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1146025_comment'></div>绵绵瓜瓞，茫茫商土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1146025_comment'></div>裔孙有庆，旧物重睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1146025_comment'></div>开国承家，疆吴跨楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1146025_comment'></div>丧乱孔棘，我恤畴依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1146025_comment'></div>圣人既作，我知所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1146025_comment'></div>终日靡俟，先天不违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1146025_comment'></div>惟藩惟辅，永言固之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1146025_comment'></div>道或污隆，时有险易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1146025_comment'></div>蝇止于棘，虎游于市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1146025_comment'></div>明明大君，宽仁以济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1146025_comment'></div>嘉尔前哲，释兹后至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1146025_comment'></div>亦觏亦见，乃侯乃公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1146025_comment'></div>沐浴玄泽，徊翔景风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1146025_comment'></div>如松之茂，如山之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1146025_comment'></div>奈何不淑，运极化穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1146025_comment'></div>旧国疏封，新阡启室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1146025_comment'></div>人谂之谋，卜云其吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1146025_comment'></div>龙章骥德，兰言玉质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1146025_comment'></div>邈尔何往？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1146025_comment'></div>此焉终毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1146025_comment'></div>俨青盖兮裶裶，驱素虬兮迟迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1146025_comment'></div>即隧路兮徒返，望君门兮永辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1146025_comment'></div>庶九原之可作，与缑岭兮相期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1146025_comment'></div>垂斯文于亿载，将乐石兮无亏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_83_1146025_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年10月</a>　十月，在开封府为太子率更令，有诗挽李煜。作品：吴王挽词三首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《东轩笔录》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_493758' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493758' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493758?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴王挽词<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（978年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493758")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493758_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493758'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493758'>倏忽千龄尽，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_493758", 493758, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>冥茫</span>万事空。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493758'>青松洛阳陌，荒草建康宫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493758'>道德遗文在，兴衰自古同。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493758'>受恩无补报，反袂泣途穷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493758'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493758_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_493759' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493759' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493759?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（978年10月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493759_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493759'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493759'>土德承馀烈，江南广旧恩。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493759'>一朝人事变，千古信书存。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493759'>哀挽周原道，铭旌郑国门。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493759'>此生虽未死，寂寞已销魂<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493759'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_493759'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_493759_0'>⑴ 宋魏泰《东轩笔录》卷一〖按：原三首，魏泰仅录二首。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_493759_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年</a>　本年，在开封府为太子率更令，作江州彭泽县修山观碑记。作品：江州彭泽县修山观碑。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1146013' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146013' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146013?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江州彭泽县修山观碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（978年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146013")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146013_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146013'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146013'>混元资始，玄造权舆，道以久而化成，朴既散而为器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146013_comment'></div>圣人在位，修之于天下，则有明堂清庙，表训民事神之方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146013_comment'></div>贤者<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1146013", 1146013, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>贞遁</span>，修之于身，则有名山福地，为朝真降灵之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146013_comment'></div>小大则异，宗致惟均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146013_comment'></div>江州彭泽县有修山焉，瞰天险而高标，抗庐峰而特立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146013_comment'></div>气雄而势耸，翠积而光寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146013_comment'></div>峻屺深岩，风云蓄泄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146013_comment'></div>茂林穹谷，材用繁滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146013_comment'></div>游居之所走望，真隐之所栖息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146013_comment'></div>考诸图谍，昔静节先生游憩之地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146013_comment'></div>杉松交影，犹怀种柳之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146013_comment'></div>山水清音，尚想素琴之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146013_comment'></div>遗德所及，仙祠以兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146013_comment'></div>梁大同元年，有句曲道士尉文光，灵气夙成，阴功将满，遐择胜地，以恢妙门，聿来此山，益广基构，制度无阙，标题载光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146013_comment'></div>越二年，尉君白日登晨，举邑咸觌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146013_comment'></div>人民未改，飙歘载还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146013_comment'></div>霓衣则殊，鹤貌如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146013_comment'></div>税驾之地，甘棠永存，故今有尉驾池焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146013_comment'></div>而中山丹灶香炉，松坛石室，俨然奇迹，若奉宴居，历代严恭，有如旦暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146013_comment'></div>唐狄梁公履虎不咥，弦歌此邦，企仰仙游，重加崇饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146013_comment'></div>又塑高宗大帝圣像，以伸送往之诚，朔望朝拜，不失常礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146013_comment'></div>复以钱五十万，为致田园，厨廪所资，至今犹赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146013_comment'></div>季唐之世，临川宋震来为邑宰，掘地得药鼎、药合，因建尉真人之室于东序，设像以奉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146013_comment'></div>秩满还乡，遂入麻姑山为道士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146013_comment'></div>是知清心冥契，玄鉴孔昭，青天白日，孰云其远？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146013_comment'></div>道士谢又能早参真箓，夙负时名，闲馆灵场，备尝践历，空谈秘诀，悉诣精微，克享修龄，言归庐岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146013_comment'></div>郡侯敦请，付以修山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146013_comment'></div>阐教之心，勤行匪懈，栋宇之制，日以增严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146013_comment'></div>端闱屹其穹隆，周庑纷其回合，焕然藻绘，蔼尔重染。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146013_comment'></div>清澄之气攸充，汗漫之游斯在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146013_comment'></div>戊寅岁，谢君解化，弟子王省昂继之方行，才亦世出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1146013_comment'></div>金石之刻，佥曰其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1146013_comment'></div>铉也钦羡真猷，因为之颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1146013_comment'></div>其词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1146013'>大道混成，修之乃真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1146013_comment'></div>必有胜境，以居异人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1146013_comment'></div>南楚之域，玄风所臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1146013_comment'></div>邈哉修山，栖灵降神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1146013_comment'></div>陶令高名，尉师仙卿，狄公元臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1146013_comment'></div>矫矫三贤，千祀齐声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1146013_comment'></div>是相是宅，载经载营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1146013_comment'></div>疏此翠巘，列为殊庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1146013_comment'></div>想像玄圃，规模赤城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1146013_comment'></div>瞻之者肃，处之者宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1146013_comment'></div>心之所至，道岂虚行？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1146013_comment'></div>刊名翠琰，永告诸生。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1146013_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=978&endYear=978')">978年</a>　约于本年三月，在开封府为太子率更令，作序送刁衎出知桐庐。作品：送刁桐庐序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1145896' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145896' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145896?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送刁桐庐序</a><span class='authorDate'>（978年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145896")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145896_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145896'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145896'>陶彭泽，古之逸民也，犹曰「聊欲弦歌，以为三径之资」，是知清真之才，高尚其事，唯安民利物可以易其志仁之业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145896_comment'></div>元宾长官生钟鼎之族，处绮纨之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145896_comment'></div>懿文敏行，角立杰出；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145896_comment'></div>云心鹤态，萧然物外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145896_comment'></div>而世禄所及，初筮实从，策名兰台，寓直宫省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145896_comment'></div>挂冠解绂，至于再三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145896_comment'></div>终以地连肺腑，时属忧患，黾俛从事，出入十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145896_comment'></div>及时移世改，自以为获平昔之志矣，而物有万殊，命不我与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145896_comment'></div>昔之朱紫盈门，今则群从无所庇矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145896_comment'></div>昔之金玉满堂，今则箪瓢不常给矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145896_comment'></div>乃慨然曰：「洁其身而忘其宗，得为孝乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145896_comment'></div>于是濯缨清流，投迹名路，纡此茜绶，涖于桐庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145896_comment'></div>暮春三月，饮饯都邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145896_comment'></div>传曰：「人之所欲，天必从之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145896_comment'></div>尝闻桐庐，江浙之胜景也，朱、张、顾、陆，遗墟迩焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145896_comment'></div>王、谢、任、沈，旧迹存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145896_comment'></div>山水林壑，应接不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145896_comment'></div>夫以天下之广，而首获此邑，非天从子之欲乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145896_comment'></div>将惟新之化，抚思乂之俗，道在于己，事至乃应，诚接于物，令行莫违，弹琴咏诗，角巾蜡屐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145896_comment'></div>推是而往，所至必安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145896_comment'></div>朝市丘壑，复何有异？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145896_comment'></div>他日岂失为东方曼倩哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145896_comment'></div>离群之思，亦宜裁抑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145896_comment'></div>慎夏自爱，无假多谈。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1145896_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=979&endYear=979')">979年2月</a>　二月，在开封府为太子率更令，与人有诗歌唱和。作品：和旻道人见寄。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493674' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493674' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493674?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和旻道人见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（979年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493674")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493674_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493674'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493674'>戎服非吾事，华缨寄此身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493674'>谬为金马客，本是钓乡人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493674'>引领梁园雪，扬鞭辇路尘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493674'>知师亦多病，拥褐侍阳春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493674'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493674_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=979&endYear=979')">979年2月</a>　二月，在开封府为太子率更令，随宋太宗亲征。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='9f3740048bec43348169c436b3676aa0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9f3740048bec43348169c436b3676aa0");'><span id='9f3740048bec43348169c436b3676aa0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=979&endYear=991')">979-991年</a>，64-76岁</div><div id='9f3740048bec43348169c436b3676aa0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=979&endYear=979')">979年7月</a>　七月，随宋太宗回到开封府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=979&endYear=979')">979年9月</a>　九月，在开封府为太子率更令，以从征扈跸劳迁给事中，直学士院如故。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年1月20日</a>　正月二十日，在开封府为给事中，应单父县令毛应几之请，以小篆重书贾至《宓子贱碑颂》，并作碑阴记。作品：重建宓子贱碑阴记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1145957' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145957' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145957?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重建宓子贱碑阴记<span class='inlineComment2'>（太平兴国五年正月二十日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（980年1月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145957")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145957_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145957'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145957'>单父县宓子贱旧碑，贾至文，梁耿书，天宝十年四月四日柳载建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145957_comment'></div>始致于故县北隅琴堂之上，光化二年，以县为郡署，县令李知杰移理于今所，碑亦随徙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145957_comment'></div>措置不谨，风雨所摧，因折为数段，扶置垣墙之间，及今八十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145957_comment'></div>皇宋抚运，书轨大同，人文化成，清静为理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145957_comment'></div>县令毛君名庶几，越自江左，来抚斯民，见贤思齐，好古博雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145957_comment'></div>以为宓子之化，人犹不忘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145957_comment'></div>贾君之文，人共称赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145957_comment'></div>若弃之而不修，非所以训民事神也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145957_comment'></div>于是再建隆碣，重书旧词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145957_comment'></div>以铉尝学篆籀，见求运笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145957_comment'></div>梁氏之迹，本自非工，仍为倒薤之势，非八书之正也，而又字体<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1145957", 1145957, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>讹俗</span>，文词舛误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145957_comment'></div>今以贾氏集校而正之，远拟秦李斯，改为玉箸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145957_comment'></div>立于宓君之祠庭，事之宜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145957_comment'></div>以改作之意，附于碑阴云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145957_comment'></div>太平兴国五年正月二十日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1145957_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年3月16日</a>　三月十六日，在开封府为给事中，奉和宋太宗《御制击毬》七言诗。作品：奉和御制打毬。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493633' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493633' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493633?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制打毬</a><span class='authorDate'>（980年3月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493633")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493633_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493633'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493633'>雷传画鼓偏增气，星度飞毬欲映空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493633'>共道宸游因习武，凯歌犹似奏平戎。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493633_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493633'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493633_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年3月16日</a>　三月十六日，在开封府为给事中，奉和宋太宗《御制击毬》五言诗。作品：又五言。<span id='poem_sentence_1_493634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493634'>仙乐飘云外，祥风近<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作起）</span>日边。<div id='poem_sentence_4_493634'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493634_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年3月23日</a>　三月二十三日，在开封府为给事中，奉和宋太宗《喜春雨》诗。作品：奉和御制春雨。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493635' class='_poem'><div
