id='poem_title_493635_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493635'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493635'>祁祁甘雨正当春，草树精神一倍新。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493635'>匀洒农郊偏长麦，缓飘花槛不惊人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493635'>密随宫仗环青辂，普逐皇恩下紫宸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493635'>霁后楼台更堪望，满园桃李间松筠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493635_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493635'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493635_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年</a>　春，在开封府为给事中，有诗送梁周翰知苏州。作品：送苏州梁补阙。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493664' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493664' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493664?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送苏州梁补阙</a><span class='authorDate'>（980年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493664")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493664_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493664'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493664'>轧轧朱轮道路长，虎丘山下剩春光。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493664'>军城旧是吴王国，郡守曾为谏署郎。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493664'>祖席咏歌金玉振，下车条教蕙兰香。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493664'>青云旧是高飞处，三载徘徊亦未妨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493664'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493664_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为给事中，有诗送张谔出任西川转运副使。作品：送张学士赴西川。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_493745' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493745' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493745?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送张学士赴西川</a><span class='authorDate'>（980年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493745")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493745_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493745'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493745'>右蜀分忧辍近臣，翩翩旄节下青冥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493745'>单车唯载支机石，夙驾长先使者星。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493745'>已有清风驰栈道，犹酣别酒过长亭。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493745'>佗年报政徵黄入，留取文翁旧典刑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493745_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493745'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493745_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=980&endYear=980')">980年</a>　约于本年，载开封府为给事中，作易文赟神道碑。作品：大宋故天雄军节度行军司马易府君神道碑。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1146021' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146021' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146021?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋故天雄军节度行军司马易府君神道碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（980年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146021")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146021_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146021'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146021'>府君讳文赟，字广美，豫章高安人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146021_comment'></div>在昔有晋，舂陵令雄，位不充量，忠以亡身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146021_comment'></div>祚流子孙，繁衍荆楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146021_comment'></div>其世禄种德，则故老家牒详焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146021_comment'></div>曾祖暇、祖崇，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146021_comment'></div>妣邹氏，追封范阳县太君，从子贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146021_comment'></div>君符彩爽迈，质性深沉，少遭时乱，静守家法，刚而无犯，勇而有节，乡曲之誉，蔼然于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146021_comment'></div>有吴功臣刘公信，节制豫章，训兵选士，闻君名而召之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146021_comment'></div>君谓所亲曰：「大丈夫当立功立事，以大家门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146021_comment'></div>吾闻刘公刚毅倜傥，有英雄之量，必能申吾用也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146021_comment'></div>乃杖策从之，甚见器重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146021_comment'></div>委以御侮，授之亲兵，出为爪牙，入参侍直，外捍封略，中清寇攘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146021_comment'></div>十年之间，遂升右职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146021_comment'></div>刘公物故，唐室中兴，君于是策名周行，入典离卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146021_comment'></div>于时戎事俯定，国容载穆，君止于拊循士众，恭守官常，时其寒燠，均其劳逸，勤毖徼道，廉察何留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146021_comment'></div>不矜出位之思，甚得为将之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146021_comment'></div>自宣威军裨将，累迁至左右天威军都虞候，自检校右常侍，至检校太保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146021_comment'></div>及淮甸俶扰，都邑震惊，以君为雄州刺史，充建武军使，其理所即广陵之天长县也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146021_comment'></div>据冲要之地，有士民之众，绥怀训练，其俗用和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146021_comment'></div>会周世宗亲总六师，志平江右，于是濠、泗携叛，扬、楚摧陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146021_comment'></div>君城小援绝，坚守累旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146021_comment'></div>世宗使降将郭廷谓临城招谕，君曰：「弃命以茍生，不义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146021_comment'></div>剿民以全名，不仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146021_comment'></div>吾处中道而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146021_comment'></div>乃间道表于本朝，备陈形势，且谕远虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146021_comment'></div>还旨嘉纳，谕以割地之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146021_comment'></div>君即开城请罪，世宗慰劳数四，锡赉加等，即授衡州刺史，封太原县子，充天雄军节度行军司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146021_comment'></div>皇宋启运，优奖有加，改道州刺史，进爵为侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146021_comment'></div>君以俯绛老之年，有郤克之疾，表求致仕，优诏不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146021_comment'></div>勤恳固请，听归临淮郡私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146021_comment'></div>春秋七十有五，开宝元年秋七月考终命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1146021_comment'></div>三年九月，葬于盱眙县义和乡西嵩里北团山，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1146021_comment'></div>夫人会稽县君谢氏，亦江左之冠族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1146021_comment'></div>作合君子，克昭令仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1146021_comment'></div>箴管之勤，夙彰于妇德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1146021_comment'></div>汤沐之邑，晚从于夫贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1146021_comment'></div>训导诸子，备全义方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1146021_comment'></div>钟蓬首之痛，哀而知礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1146021_comment'></div>受高堂之养，严而有慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1146021_comment'></div>春秋七十有六，太平兴国二年秋七月，终于临淮私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1146021_comment'></div>某年月日合祔焉，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1146021_comment'></div>有子五人，曰延贵、延祚、延寿、延义，并克荷先业，勤修令名，或参藩郡，或干内职，皆先夫人而没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1146021_comment'></div>唯第四子延庆独禀粹和，服膺儒教，孝悌之至，称于州闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1146021_comment'></div>承颜先意，侔曾、闵之行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1146021_comment'></div>居丧过哀，有二连之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1146021_comment'></div>庐墓绝浆，义感生植，嘉木连理，玉芝成业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1146021_comment'></div>远近闻之，莫不惊叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1146021_comment'></div>由是自前临淮令拜大理丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1146021_comment'></div>及夫人卜葬，违制临赴，为有司所劾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1146021_comment'></div>有诏勿问，听解秩家居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1146021_comment'></div>惟府君之生也，临戎以恩信，理民以慈惠，事君全其节，处身由其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1146021_comment'></div>故垂此家法，推为庆门，是生孝子，以永世祀，美矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1146021_comment'></div>铉闻风而悦之，故勒铭于神道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1146021_comment'></div>其辞曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_1146021'>于惟易氏，忠义之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1146021_comment'></div>德厚流光，显于后昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1146021_comment'></div>后昆之贤，生我府君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1146021_comment'></div>体道自居，壮图不群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1146021_comment'></div>辍耕永叹，负羽从军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1146021_comment'></div>赳赳和门，勇爵斯设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1146021_comment'></div>静则严重，动则奋发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1146021_comment'></div>临难忘私，处危全节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1146021_comment'></div>名遂身泰，考终无阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1146021_comment'></div>芃芃泗川，永閟佳城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1146021_comment'></div>哀哀孝子，载感坤灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1146021_comment'></div>君恩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_64_1146021", 1146021, "Clauses/191/Comments/0")'>贲宠</span>，乐石刊铭，百代之下，常流淑声。</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1146021_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=981&endYear=981')">981年2月</a>　二月，在开封府为给事中，为江直木作墓志铭。作品：大宋故尚书兵部员外郎江君墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1146029' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146029' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146029?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋故尚书兵部员外郎江君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（981年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146029")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146029_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146029'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146029'>君讳直木，字子建，寻阳人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146029_comment'></div>庐九之地，时生俊才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146029_comment'></div>忠壮之族，世著南国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146029_comment'></div>末叶湮替，与时污隆，儒、墨退让，垂为家法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146029_comment'></div>曾祖晁、祖蠙、考骘，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146029_comment'></div>伯父梦孙，与先君同隐庐山，以经学大义自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146029_comment'></div>伯父后膺宰府之辟，自求弦歌之任，报政罢去，复隐旧山，孝友<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1146029", 1146029, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>贞清</span>，乡里推服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146029_comment'></div>先妣李氏方娠，梦神人授以直木一本，寤而生君，故取名焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146029_comment'></div>幼而颖悟，生知经义，七岁以神童擢第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146029_comment'></div>未几，丁先君忧，至性孺慕，宗族称叹，孜孜色养，无复宦情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146029_comment'></div>学古属文，惟日不足，爰及弱冠，遂以词艺知名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146029_comment'></div>其为文清淡简约，自为品格，尤长于古风诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146029_comment'></div>家居凡二十五年，亲友敦喻，乃从常调，释褐太常寺奉礼郎，转江都县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146029_comment'></div>直以事上，不失其恭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146029_comment'></div>勤以率下，毕举其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146029_comment'></div>民从其化，吏服其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146029_comment'></div>府尹陈玄藻、县令路仪，皆恃才傲物，独推重于君，以为不如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146029_comment'></div>改江夏令，其理如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146029_comment'></div>鄂帅何洙，武勋致位，性复暴桀，亦加优礼，异于馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146029_comment'></div>尝视君举止迂缓，车服朴野，辄怡然而笑，每责诸寮属曰：「君辈称为儒生，不学江令也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146029_comment'></div>秩满，改蕲州黄梅令，议者以为屈，君以乡曲俯接，欣然而往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146029_comment'></div>逾岁，迁歙州黟县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146029_comment'></div>会宗属封建，妙选府寮，授君记室之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146029_comment'></div>处平台复道之地，列玳簪珠履之间，清节素风，凛然不改，正词直道，动必尽规，府公甚重之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146029_comment'></div>十有馀年，累迁至水部员外郎，赐绯，而记室如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146029_comment'></div>庚午岁，府公奉使天朝，留镇兖海，授君泰宁节度判官、检校金部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146029_comment'></div>数年，迁司门员外郎，判刑部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146029_comment'></div>今上元年，加朝奉郎，先君赠大理司直，先妣追封陇西县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146029_comment'></div>视事三载，求外任以自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146029_comment'></div>上以君恭勤详慎，宜久其职，拜兵部员外郎，仍兼刑部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146029_comment'></div>享年六十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1146029_comment'></div>居常康宁，微病数日，奄从物故，时太平兴国五年冬十二月二十八日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1146029_comment'></div>即明年二月十日，葬于开封县汴阳乡丰台里，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1146029_comment'></div>前夫人封氏、今夫人太原县君王氏，皆有窈窕之质，幽闲之操，叶此贞节，蔚其门风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1146029_comment'></div>长子敞，京兆府醴泉县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1146029_comment'></div>次曰用成、用明、用澄、用康、用平、用文、用宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1146029_comment'></div>女二人，曰慕昭、用贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1146029_comment'></div>君生于季俗，世全素业，性纯貌古，行洁文高，守道安贫，非礼不动，未尝忤物，亦不随流，真所谓鞠躬君子者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1146029_comment'></div>夙惠之性，禀于天资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1146029_comment'></div>年十馀岁，侍伯父食，不过园疏而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1146029_comment'></div>伯父戏之曰：「啜白薤之羹，淡而无味」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1146029_comment'></div>君应声答曰：「齧紫茄之蒂，铿尔有声」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1146029_comment'></div>人知其当大成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1146029_comment'></div>余始闻其名，晚乃识面，察言观行，重其为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1146029_comment'></div>藩房见选，余所荐也，亦既称职，颇尝自多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1146029_comment'></div>丙寅岁与君俱年五十岁，日会饮酒，相与赋诗，君先就，曰：「学《易》宁无道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1146029_comment'></div>知非素有心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1146029_comment'></div>余遂不复作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1146029_comment'></div>君有文集二十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1146029_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1146029_comment'></div>契阔夷险，咨嗟年鬓，一生一死，孰克忘情！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1146029_comment'></div>聊存挂剑之期，故有刊铭之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1146029_comment'></div>其词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_1146029'>呜呼江君，世济其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1146029_comment'></div>生今之俗，为古之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1146029_comment'></div>闺门侃侃，乡里恂恂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1146029_comment'></div>其实如秋，其华如春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1146029_comment'></div>握兰有裕，伏阁惟勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1146029_comment'></div>考终归全，邈焉清尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1146029_comment'></div>葬于所没，古称达者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1146029_comment'></div>浚水长源，夷门迥野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1146029_comment'></div>徒挂宝剑，空驰白马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1146029_comment'></div>胜气如存，逝川不舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1146029_comment'></div>勒石垂芳，千载之下。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1146029_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=981&endYear=981')">981年10月</a>　十月，在开封府为给事中，编集张洎长子张冉遗稿，并作序。作品：张氏子集序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1145914' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145914' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145914?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张氏子集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（981年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145914")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145914_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145914'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145914'>观夫贤人君子，禀清真之气，应期运而出，故生而岐嶷，幼而敏惠，既成而负国士之器，既立而为天下之用，康宁寿考，繁衍流祚，此其常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145914_comment'></div>若乃秀而不实，仁而不遇，前圣所以兴叹，百代所以遗恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145914_comment'></div>斯则神道忽恍，万化茫昧，自古乃尔，吾将奈何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145914_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145914_comment'></div>张氏子，秀而不实者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145914_comment'></div>子名冉，本字叔相，今户部员外郎洎之长子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145914_comment'></div>年七岁，博览经史，日诵千言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145914_comment'></div>十岁能属文，诗赋议论，成于俄顷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145914_comment'></div>十二著《礼》上、下二篇，旧君吴王见之而叹曰：「此子天假之年，他日必为国器矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145914_comment'></div>乃至梁京，翰长李公昉、阁长李公穆，皆引之登门，特加礼遇，其道日以光矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145914_comment'></div>其风仪标格，萧然朗彻，观者谓之玉人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145914_comment'></div>余甚重之，以为四科之俊也，故改其字师德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145914_comment'></div>于时天子敦重文学，亲考英秀，海内士子，靡然向风，咸谓子必当振鳞附翼，一举凌迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145914_comment'></div>而介然特立，澹然贞退，求圣贤之微旨，以养亲修心为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145914_comment'></div>复探释老玄言，读华阳诸真经，飘然有脱落尘滓之志，而况于荣名乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145914_comment'></div>不幸羸瘵逾岁，遽从夭折，年十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145914_comment'></div>诸公闻之，无不悯恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145914_comment'></div>余以事旧之厚，钟情特深，故求其遗稿，集而为序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145914_comment'></div>又尝览前载，见古之人如子之人物敏俊、词藻趣尚，而促龄无禄者，皆密契真箓，蜕为列仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145914_comment'></div>此乃灵篇奇纪，非史笔所当言矣，但用遣慈父之追念尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145914_comment'></div>其草隶遗迹及佗著述，皆藏于家，此不备述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145914_comment'></div>辛巳岁冬十月序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1145914_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=982&endYear=982')">982年8月</a>　八月，在开封府为给事中，有诗挽王溥。作品：太师相公挽歌词二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_493708' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493708' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493708?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太师相公挽歌词二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（982年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493708")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493708_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493708'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493708'>岩廊旧德汉储师，富贵优游自古稀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493708'>四序不能违代谢，九原谁可与同归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493708'>精神恍惚骑龙尾，功业纷纶在虎闱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493708'>惆怅鸣珂洛阳道，素车丹旐奉灵衣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493708_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493708'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493708_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_493709' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493709' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_493709_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493709'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493709'>风流安石在东山，曾许从容妓乐间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493709'>倾盖算来能几日，逝川东去不知还。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493709'>北邙原上寒云结，郑国门前晓月弯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493709'>祖奠欲收宾御散，满衣零泪掩衰颜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493709_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493709'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493709_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=982&endYear=982')">982年9月</a>　九月，在开封府为给事中，奉诏与修《文苑英华》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=982&endYear=982')">982年12月17日</a>　十二月十七日，在开封府为给事中，受赐《御制雪诗》及酒，受命奉和。作品：奉和御制雪。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493632' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493632' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493632?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制雪</a><span class='authorDate'>（982年12月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493632")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493632_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493632'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493632'>丰登盈尺瑞，物象九门深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493632'>璧照环丹砌，梅花满上林。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493632'>茶香偏自得，酒力讵难禁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493632'>别有寒郊外，银河映玉岑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493632_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493632'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493632_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=983&endYear=983')">983年</a>　春，在开封府为给事中，有诗送郑文宝及第后西归。作品：送郑先辈及第西归。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_493713' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493713' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493713?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送郑先辈及第西<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>归</a><span "poem_title_493713")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493713_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_493713_0'>① 原作先，据四库本、备要本、徐本改</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493713'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493713'>春晚缑山路，华光满翠微。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493713'>怜君持郤桂，归去著莱衣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493713'>故国几人在，浮生万事非。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493713'>唯当拭病眼，看子九霄飞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493713_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493713'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493713_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=983&endYear=983')">983年</a>　春，在开封府为给事中，有诗送李寅辞官还乡。作品：送李秀才归建安。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_493722' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493722' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493722?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送李秀才归建安</a><span class='authorDate'>（983年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493722")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_493722_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493722'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493722'>昔闻武夷士，皆是帝曾孙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493722'>李君即其人，命舛道常存。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493722'>爱子已折桂，华组耀闺门。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493722'>吾身可拂衣，䌽服归丘园。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493722'>捧觞庆北堂，其乐不可言。<div id='poem_sentence_4_493722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_493722'>清溪环幽居，远岫横前轩。<div id='poem_sentence_5_493722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_493722'>弹琴咏招隐，芳意飘若兰。<div id='poem_sentence_6_493722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_493722'>老夫无此分，何必矜弹冠。<div id='poem_sentence_7_493722_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_493722'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_493722_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=983&endYear=983')">983年6月1日</a>　六月一日，在开封府为给事中，授右散骑常侍，判尚书都省，罢直学士院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=983&endYear=983')">983年6月</a>　六月，在开封府为右散骑常侍，建言都坐议事文案先送有关机构看详。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=983&endYear=983')">983年12月19日</a>　十二月十九日，在开封府为右散骑常侍，与修之《太平御览》书成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=983&endYear=983')">983年</a>　约于本年十二月二日，在开封府为右散骑常侍，作邢州紫极宫老君殿碑记。作品：邢州紫极宫老君殿记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1145949' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145949' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145949?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邢州紫极宫老君殿记</a><span class='authorDate'>（983年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145949")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145949_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145949'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145949'>昔者老君伯阳，悯大道之既隐，伤周室之既微，以为清净无为，道之本也，非建言不能尽其意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145949_comment'></div>安上治民，道之用也，非设教不能永其成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145949_comment'></div>乃著书于函关，以明清心之要；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145949_comment'></div>授礼于仲尼，以开垂世之统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145949_comment'></div>繇是教义之被于民，如造化之渐于物，贤者识其大，不贤者识其小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145949_comment'></div>出入战国，经历薄俗，君君、臣臣、父父、子子，民到于今受其赐，则二圣人是赖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145949_comment'></div>故并享明祀，格于宇县，虽百世不能易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145949_comment'></div>邢州紫极宫者，唐开元中所立，老君像则琢玉石以为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145949_comment'></div>真灵所凭，功用殊绝，睟容奇表，俨然若存，瞻仰之徒，莫不增肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145949_comment'></div>王室剥乱，郡国崩离，三晋之郊，戎马孔棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145949_comment'></div>崇堂隳落，乃移像于北极殿之西偏，数十年间，不绝如线。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145949_comment'></div>皇宋膺运，百度惟贞，道风载阳，真侣咸萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145949_comment'></div>女道士陈体元，江左右族，夙挺玄符，不从象服之华，自结凤罗之誓，勤行匪懈，真气日滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145949_comment'></div>乙亥岁，伯氏从宦，将之俱至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145949_comment'></div>㟪𡾊知化，汗漫与期，郡守贤之，授以宫任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145949_comment'></div>亦既涖止，慨然永怀，嗟崇构之倾颓，叹尊位之蹂杂，程工度费，即旧谋新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145949_comment'></div>知州事段公思恭，仙派分源，谏垣旧德，嘉其伟志，助以俸金，郡僚而下，欢然风靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145949_comment'></div>即宫之西序，建老君殿三间，材用必良，工艺必精，广袤中规，奢俭合度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145949_comment'></div>旭景升而丹彩焕，清风袭而爽气生，肃然仙都，复睹灵境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145949_comment'></div>粤某年月奉玉像而处焉，霓衣致虔，羽盖成列，几筵严肃，香烛苾芬，钟磬咸和，烟云改色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145949_comment'></div>非至诚感召，孰能臻此者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145949_comment'></div>练师之家，奕叶从公，清白垂训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145949_comment'></div>仲兄前鹿邑令省躬，秉直忤俗，退而居贞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145949_comment'></div>季兄邢州书记长参，学古入官，和以接物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145949_comment'></div>积善之家，宜生仙才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145949_comment'></div>铉知二君岁久，故美其事而纪于石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145949_comment'></div>某年十二月二日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1145949_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>　初春，在开封府为右散骑常侍，有诗送赞宁归钱塘。作品：送赞宁道人归浙中。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。此条事迹，原书系于太平兴国八年六月，此据李振中《徐铉入宋诗歌编年考》中对“凌澌”一词的解释而改。）</span><div id='poem_493710' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493710' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493710?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送赞宁道人归浙中</a><span class='authorDate'>（984年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493710")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493710_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493710'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493710'>故里夫差国，高名惠远师。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493710'>君恩从野逸，归棹逐凌澌。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493710'>旧访虽无念，牵怀亦有诗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493710'>因行过秦望，为致李斯碑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493710_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493710'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493710_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年4月16日</a>　四月十六日，在开封府为右散骑常侍，受诏参定封禅泰山礼仪。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年4月</a>　四月，在开封府为右散骑常侍，参与议定宋运膺火德。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年10月</a>　十月，在开封府为右散骑常侍，与滕中正、王祐等援引图史证岚州所献奇兽为祥麟。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>　本年，在开封府为右散骑常侍，为李至画像作赞。作品：参政李公至字言几年三十八真赞。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1145972' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145972' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145972?labeling=true' target='_blank'>参政李公至字言几年三十八真赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（984年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145972")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1145972_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145972'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145972'>金玉其相，君子之容。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1145972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1145972'>庙堂之器，多士攸宗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1145972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1145972'>谋先帷幄，道合云龙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1145972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1145972'>绝景横骛，干霄直上。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1145972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1145972'>黑头三公，风流宰相。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1145972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1145972'>人具尔瞻，惟肖之像。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1145972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1145972'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1145972_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>　本年，在开封府为右散骑常侍，应僧义韬之请，为作抚州永安禅院碑记。作品：抚州永安禅院记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1145955' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145955' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145955?labeling=true' target='_blank'>抚州永安禅院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（984年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145955")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145955_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145955'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145955'>教之大者其行远，利之博者其报丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145955_comment'></div>自三代已还，百家并骛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145955_comment'></div>炎灵之后，释氏特隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145955_comment'></div>经法之盛，参乎先圣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145955_comment'></div>祠宇之设，广于虞庠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145955_comment'></div>不知所以然而然，非言象所及已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145955_comment'></div>抚州郡署之左一里而近，有禅院焉，乾符中署曰宝国，天祐中改名永安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145955_comment'></div>方志失传，莫知肇兴之始；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145955_comment'></div>高人迭处，咸为宴坐之场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145955_comment'></div>夫经像之所居，苾馨之所荐，必将据郡国之形胜，袭川原之气象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145955_comment'></div>斯郡也，总楚、越之都会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145955_comment'></div>斯院也，浸章、汝之清流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145955_comment'></div>逸少、康乐，江左名士，而墨池经台介乎比闾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145955_comment'></div>麻姑、南真，丹台上列，而仙坛闲馆峙乎封域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145955_comment'></div>闬闳相望，钟磬交音，神灵之所依凭，烟霞之所韬映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145955_comment'></div>尔其栋宇之状也，则赫赫乎显敞，耽耽乎深严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145955_comment'></div>黼藻成文，磨砻尽妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145955_comment'></div>层楼对峙，脩廊四通，列讲肆于崇堂，安众士于奥室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145955_comment'></div>动有击蒙之益，静有宁体之娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145955_comment'></div>储峙必丰，器用必给，四方学者，至辄如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145955_comment'></div>考绩程功，则住持禅师义韬之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145955_comment'></div>韬公道学精诣，慧心朗悟，以济众为务，以兴教为怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145955_comment'></div>少游名都，历访先达；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145955_comment'></div>晚栖临汝，自辟师门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145955_comment'></div>甲申岁，来诣京华，褐衣请见，对扬玉扆，躬奉天言，论难所及，辞义响答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145955_comment'></div>圣恩嘉瞩，赠以紫衣，登门之徒，莫不增肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145955_comment'></div>韬公以斯院制度崇丽，修奉精严，金石阙如，何以示后，惠然见顾，求我以文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145955_comment'></div>辞让不获，因为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145955_comment'></div>年月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1145955_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1145955'><span class='label'>按：</span>《徐公文集》卷二八<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1145955_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=984&endYear=984')">984年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为右散骑常侍，为周本之女作墓志铭。作品：故汝南县太君周氏夫人墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_1146034' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146034' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146034?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故汝南县太君周氏夫人墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（984年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146034")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146034_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146034'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146034'>夫人讳某，字某，庐江舒人，三国时吴将公瑾之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146034_comment'></div>公瑾葬于舒之宿松，今裔孙奉祀者百馀家，虽降在畎亩，而时生间杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146034_comment'></div>烈考讳本，幼而遇乱，自奋从军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146034_comment'></div>吴王创基，功冠诸将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146034_comment'></div>季唐建业，位列宗臣，官至中书令，封西平王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146034_comment'></div>夫人即王之第某女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146034_comment'></div>天姿玉莹，淑性川渟，孝德内融，柔仪外映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146034_comment'></div>既笄，归于徐氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146034_comment'></div>府君讳某，即唐相司徒公玠之第某子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146034_comment'></div>于时江左方盛，二族齐荣，婚姻之贵，雄视王谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146034_comment'></div>而夫人雅性谦谨，率由礼经，至于蘋藻之严，佩环之节，浣濯之俭，织纴之勤，必以身先，罔弗由道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146034_comment'></div>宗族亲睦，人无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146034_comment'></div>府君仕为閤门副使、殿中少监，早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146034_comment'></div>四子皆幼，夫人提携教训，亲授经书，及其出就外傅，已通《孝经》、《论语》矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146034_comment'></div>性晓音律，而尚雅声，善丝竹而精琴瑟，习《孝经》而宗玄言，斋居讽诵，未尝懈怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146034_comment'></div>虽闺门之内，常以慈抚，而家人之节，有若严君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146034_comment'></div>故其门风肃然，先业不陨，岂非天和充己，而道气感物者欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146034_comment'></div>春秋四十八，开宝九年正月二十一日，终于建康瑞里官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146034_comment'></div>其年二月，葬于江宁县凤台乡娄侯里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146034_comment'></div>长子某，亦为诸司副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146034_comment'></div>及入朝，为京兆府醴泉令、陕州录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146034_comment'></div>公府交荐，遂升闺籍，太子右赞善大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146034_comment'></div>夫人始以子贵，授汝南县太君，至是朝命复追荣焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146034_comment'></div>次子继宏，举进士，次继宇，次继宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146034_comment'></div>初，夫人之亡，会宗国沦覆，窀穸之事，不暇如仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146034_comment'></div>至太平兴国某年月日，继宗等始改窆于某所，附大茔焉，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146034_comment'></div>铉与西平诸子，辱为交游，及相府宗党，复敦事旧，故得以门内之理，为隧道之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146034_comment'></div>传于无穷，斯为实录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146034_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1146034'>侯藩之子，相门之嫔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146034_comment'></div>道高莱妇，德邵陶亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146034_comment'></div>猗欤彤管，永世芳尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1146034_comment'></div>生荣没哀，何必眉寿？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1146034_comment'></div>粉田启邑，斯为不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1146034_comment'></div>令子承家，斯为有后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1146034_comment'></div>狐、郤降替，二族依然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1146034_comment'></div>陵谷迁贸，松楸附焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1146034_comment'></div>谓天盖高，福善胡愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1146034_comment'></div>勒铭泉户，兰菊绵绵。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1146034_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=985&endYear=985')">985年1月18日</a>　正月十八日，在开封府为右散骑常侍，受诏同知礼部贡举。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=985&endYear=985')">985年7月</a>　七月，在开封府为右散骑常侍，作泗州重修文宣王庙碑记。作品：泗州重修文宣王庙记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1145948' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145948' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145948?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泗州重修文宣王庙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（雍熙二年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145948")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145948_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145948'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145948'>昔我先圣，有周公之才，无文王之时，故宪章其道，以垂万世，精神冥契，夕则梦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145948_comment'></div>是知千载旦暮，盖其道同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145948_comment'></div>自时以降，鸿儒硕生，敷畅微言，佐佑大化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145948_comment'></div>专一之志，通于神明，咸梦宣尼，以著名实，斯文间作，来者不诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145948_comment'></div>国家彰灼神功，在宥天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145948_comment'></div>礼乐刑政，举百王之中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145948_comment'></div>典谟训诰，用三代之式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145948_comment'></div>文学之士，靡然向风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145948_comment'></div>临淮徐君名某，字某，弱而好学，壮而有立，行敦乎族党，名闻于州闾，修辞立诚，躬儒者之业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145948_comment'></div>博施济众，秉义士之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145948_comment'></div>随计春官，再不中选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145948_comment'></div>会长子宗孟，郡亦举秀才，君以为名不可多取，即欲退而求志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145948_comment'></div>无何，梦游淮上，倏有沦胥之厄，众君子拯之而置于宣圣之堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145948_comment'></div>俨然逢掖之容，若奉缁帷之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145948_comment'></div>寤而神耸，益用兢怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145948_comment'></div>闻者奇之，勉以西上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145948_comment'></div>明年春，冕旒临御，亲较群才，崇朝之间，父子俱捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145948_comment'></div>盖古今未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145948_comment'></div>君叹曰：「天子广孤平之路，杜请谒之门，先圣知之，是有敦勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145948_comment'></div>斯实至德感兆，鄙何有焉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145948_comment'></div>思欲昭答灵心，丕显玄贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145948_comment'></div>惟兹泗上，雄视百城，学校之制，我不在后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145948_comment'></div>王业伊始，天下初平，舟车辐凑之都，邮传旁午之地，邦君丞掾，日不暇给，弦诵之所，窥户阒然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145948_comment'></div>君白于公府，愿补阙政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145948_comment'></div>于是出家积，鸠国工，即旧谋新，瞻星揆日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145948_comment'></div>乃建路寝，乃立应门，辟讲论之堂，设东西之序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145948_comment'></div>广袤合度，奢俭中规，像设增严，绘素加焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145948_comment'></div>凡祭器制度，皆图于垣墉，俾夫观艺之徒、横经之侣，居今识古，虚往实归，三代之风，由斯而致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145948_comment'></div>录事参军张君浚纲纪之任，夙夜惟寅，尝与同僚及斯而叹曰：「振举废阙，公力未遑，当属于好事君子，非徐君不能也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145948_comment'></div>及兹缔构，如宿契焉，是知善人之言，罔弗响答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145948_comment'></div>夫圣人之教也，与天地常在，将阴阳并运，恍惚玄应，昧者不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1145948_comment'></div>今徐君服之而成大名，感之而臻介福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1145948_comment'></div>咨尔后学，可不勉欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1145948_comment'></div>金石之铭，其无愧已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1145948_comment'></div>于时岁次乙酉，雍熙二年秋七月记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1145948_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=985&endYear=985')">985年</a>　约于本年秋，在开封府为右散骑常侍，与钱昱有诗歌唱和。作品：和钱秘监边谏议南宫同直赠答。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_493706' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493706' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493706?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和钱秘监与边谏议南宫同直赠答</a><span class='authorDate'>（985年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493706")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493706_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493706'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493706'>筵上<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_493706", 493706, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>诗题</span>共笔床，樽前酒兴话高阳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493706'>心清自觉官曹简，院静先知节候凉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493706'>南国少年推贵重，东堂前辈让贤良。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493706'>好看双凤追飞处，胡<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作垩）</span>粉新涂紫界墙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493706_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493706'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493706_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=985&endYear=985')">985年</a>　约于本年秋，在开封府为右散骑常侍，有诗和钱昱。作品：钱秘监旅居秋怀二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_493719' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493719' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493719?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和钱秘监旅居秋怀二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（985年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493719")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493719_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493719'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493719'>秘监疏朝谒，门前长绿苔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493719'>未愁玄鬓改，且喜素秋来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493719'>独坐翻棋势，闲行绕药栽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493719'>凉风入书幌，时动水沉灰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493719_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493719'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493719_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_493720' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493720' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493720?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（985年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493720_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493720'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493720'>閒静无凡客，开樽共醉醒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493720'>琴弹<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>碧玉调，书展太玄经。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493720'>酒熟看黄菊，诗成写素屏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493720'>晚来萧洒甚，山鸟下中庭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493720'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493720_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_493720'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_493720_0'>⑴ 原作调，据四库本、备要本、徐本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_493720_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=985&endYear=985')">985年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为右散骑常侍，与人有诗歌唱和。作品：和徐秘书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493658' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493658' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493658?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和徐秘书</a><span class='authorDate'>（985年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493658")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493658_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493658'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493658'>年少支离奈命何，悲秋怀旧苦吟多。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493658_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493658'>龙泉有气终难掩，荆玉无瑕岂惮磨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493658_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493658'>会偶良工收杞梓，莫将閒梦挂烟萝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493658_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493658'>他年得路抟风去，肯念今朝煦沫么。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493658_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493658'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493658_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=985&endYear=985')">985年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为右散骑常侍，有诗送钱熙出任虔州观察推官。作品：送钱先辈之虔州。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_493731' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493731' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493731?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送钱先辈之虔州</a><span class='authorDate'>（985年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493731")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493731_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493731'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493731'>子实东南美，来参第一流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493731'>从容持片玉，谈笑运前筹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493731'>赣石连云秀，廉泉带月秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493731'>可怜行乐地，况从板舆游。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493731'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493731_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=985&endYear=985')">985年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为右散骑常侍，作洪州新建白公祠堂碑记。作品：洪州新建尚书白公祠堂之记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1145952' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145952' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145952?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洪州新建尚书白公祠堂之记</a><span class='authorDate'>（985年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145952")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145952_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145952'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145952'>大丈夫处厚居实，据德依仁，岂徒洁身，将以济世，故著于事业，发于文词，而后功绩宣焉，声名立焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145952_comment'></div>盖有其实者，必有其名，是以君子耻没世而名不闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145952_comment'></div>若乃格于穹壤，渐于蛮夷，大则藏于金匮石室之书，细则诵于妇女稚孺之口，则古今已来，彰灼悠久，未有如白乐天者，不其异乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145952_comment'></div>故神明相之，攸居不倾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145952_comment'></div>黎氓怀之，馀风不泯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145952_comment'></div>士大夫神交道亲，若旦暮焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145952_comment'></div>寻阳古郡，昔公谪宦之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145952_comment'></div>绵祀二百，市朝屡变，而司马听事之室，岿然独存，斯益异矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145952_comment'></div>圣运光启，崇古尚文，三代之风，传远万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145952_comment'></div>礼部郎中、江南转运使张去华，述职按部，聿来是邦，弭节城闉，摄齐堂奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145952_comment'></div>以为先贤所舍，邑里具瞻，与夫元规之楼、惠远之社，崇饰祗荐，我何后焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145952_comment'></div>太子中允、知州事梁君翊，赞善大夫、通判州事罗君彧，叶规同心，相视莫逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145952_comment'></div>政有馀裕，府多羡财，即旧谋新，创为祠宇，传写庐山之遗像，寘于北墉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145952_comment'></div>栋宇深严，门序奥秘，肃然庙貌，想见其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145952_comment'></div>凡游居之徒，仰高山，聆遗韵，荐诚观艺，结辙于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145952_comment'></div>《礼》不云乎：祷祠古之卿士有益于人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145952_comment'></div>观乐天之文，主讽刺，垂教化，穷理本，达物情，后之学者服膺研精，则去圣何远？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145952_comment'></div>其为益也，不亦多乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145952_comment'></div>尸而祝之，固其宜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145952_comment'></div>某昔游庐岳，获拜仪形；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145952_comment'></div>今尘骑省，遥闻缔构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145952_comment'></div>喜儒宗之不坠，嘉使者之得人，故作斯文，勒于贞石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145952_comment'></div>年月某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1145952_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年2月17日</a>　二一十七日，在开封府为右散骑常侍，奉和宋太宗《御制寒食十韵》作品：奉和御制寒食十韵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493637' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493637' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493637?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制寒食十韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年2月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493637")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_493637_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493637'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493637'>朝阳散宿烟，登望思悠然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493637'>檐影晴偏暖，云容晚更鲜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493637'>共欢时景好，不惜岁华迁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493637'>旋试娇骢步，新调宝瑟弦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493637'>宫花红照耀，御水碧潺湲。<div id='poem_sentence_4_493637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_493637'>歌吹清连夜，辎軿丽满川。<div id='poem_sentence_5_493637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_493637'>依林张幄幕，夹道建鞦韆。<div id='poem_sentence_6_493637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_493637'>仙乐来天上，祥光起日边。<div id='poem_sentence_7_493637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_493637'>游丝轻冉冉，芳草绿芊芊。<div id='poem_sentence_8_493637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_493637'>圣制如春色，周流遍八埏。<div id='poem_sentence_9_493637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_493637'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_493637_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>　春，在开封府为右散骑常侍，受诏与句中正、葛湍、王惟恭等校定许慎《说文解字》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年4月</a>　四月，在开封府为右散骑常侍，为表甥女婿曾文照作墓志铭。作品：大宋故亳州蒙城县令曾君墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_1146035' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146035' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146035?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋故亳州蒙城县令赐绯鱼袋曾君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146035")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146035_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146035'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146035'>君讳文照，字知章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146035_comment'></div>其先鲁人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146035_comment'></div>百行之先，垂为家法，子孙蕃衍，不陨其声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146035_comment'></div>末叶因官，徙居南楚，今为庐陵新淦人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146035_comment'></div>祖朴、考福，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146035_comment'></div>君生禀异气，卓然老成，六经之旨，有若夙习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146035_comment'></div>于时江表之地，唐室犹兴，宪章文物，不失旧典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146035_comment'></div>君年七岁，应州里之举，以神童擢第，选满补江州东流尉，迁靖安、句容二尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146035_comment'></div>皆以清白敏惠，承上率下，和而有正，能不自矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146035_comment'></div>连考殊尤，擢为吉州太和令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146035_comment'></div>桑梓之地，瓜李多嫌，君闺门之行素修，童艾之情已信，而复临事能断，尽公无私，由是期年政成，就赐朱绂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146035_comment'></div>会宗国沦覆，举族入朝，授亳州永城令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146035_comment'></div>舟车辐凑之地，邮传旁午之涂，盘根错节，发硎靡滞，事无愆素，民不告劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146035_comment'></div>上疏论以一邑之众，供列郡之赋，指引利害，较然可分，诏特许免其县挽船夫，岁省万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146035_comment'></div>改蒙城令，其理益精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146035_comment'></div>顷之，河南大蝗，独不入蒙城之境，于是吏民相率诣阙借留，优诏褒美，许留三载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146035_comment'></div>会王师北讨，君督本县运输，深入虏庭，危而后济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146035_comment'></div>既还遇疾，以雍熙三年四月日终于永城传舍，享年若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146035_comment'></div>初，君之赴选也，余遇之于建康，察言观行，知为良士，因以表甥女姜氏妻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146035_comment'></div>有子六人，女八人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146035_comment'></div>君之从仕，世涂多故，王事靡盬，不遑顾私，雅志未申，中路早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146035_comment'></div>唯第三子乾度，再举进士，名闻场中，有后之庆，当在于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146035_comment'></div>即以某年月，号奉灵柩，归葬于某乡里，祔大茔焉，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146035_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146035_comment'></div>姻旧之故，岂无他人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146035_comment'></div>援毫濡涕，识彼陵谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146035_comment'></div>其铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1146035'>有惠于民，死事以勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146035_comment'></div>呜呼曾君，永世清芬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146035_comment'></div>仙山之阴，章江之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146035_comment'></div>考终归全，下从先人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146035_comment'></div>刻兹琬琰，垂示后昆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1146035_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年9月</a>　九月，在开封府为右散骑常侍，为乡贡进士刘鹗作墓志铭。作品：故乡贡进士刘君墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_1146037' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146037' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146037?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故乡贡进士刘君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146037")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146037_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146037'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146037'>君讳鹗，字仲翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146037_comment'></div>其先彭城人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146037_comment'></div>炎灵之裔，繁衍万邦，占籍庐陵，盖重世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146037_comment'></div>高祖滉、祖珍，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146037_comment'></div>父雄，尝从九江辟司兵掾，自免去职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146037_comment'></div>闺门之教，不肃而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146037_comment'></div>有三子，君其仲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146037_comment'></div>质性纯素，智识聪敏，年十有五则知属文，未及弱冠驰名矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146037_comment'></div>至于事亲孝，事长悌，与朋友信，接乡党让，动不违礼，居常慎独，故州里耆耋与时之名辈推重焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146037_comment'></div>郡举茂才，擢升上第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146037_comment'></div>明年而宗国沦覆，君慨然知时之不利也，于是闭门却扫，为学益勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146037_comment'></div>以为今之文人，率以词赋取高，先王之教化盖蔑如也，乃摭天下之务，论古今之变，著《法语》八十一篇，大抵宗尚周、孔，以质百氏之惑，视其书知其人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146037_comment'></div>皇宋二圣，崇古尚文，郡国孝秀，亲临考覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146037_comment'></div>君以词场旧望，复为本郡升闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146037_comment'></div>余与翰林学士贾公，承诏先考第于南宫，贾公重君之文，以为古人之俊也，乃第为高等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146037_comment'></div>而君徇难进易退之节，禀内敏外愚之容，及其扬庭，复不中选，退还乡里，笃行如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146037_comment'></div>雍熙三年九月卒于家，享年四十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146037_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146037_comment'></div>有才有时，命不我与，自古同叹，可胜道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146037_comment'></div>遗文累裒，不朽之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146037_comment'></div>即某年月葬于本县化龙乡折桂里之原，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146037_comment'></div>君娶郭氏，先十日而亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146037_comment'></div>子师望、文绮，皆得父风，其有后矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146037_comment'></div>二女：长适太原郭方，次适陇西李某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146037_comment'></div>师望以余为父之知己也，故千里号诉，求志其墓云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146037_comment'></div>词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1146037'>呜呼刘生，江楚之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146037_comment'></div>才识兼茂，时命难并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146037_comment'></div>没于白屋，閟此泉扃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146037_comment'></div>立言可法，何必浮荣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146037_comment'></div>刻兹贞石，永尔高名<span class='inlineComment2'>（《徐公文集》卷三○。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146037_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1146037'>之：原脱，据徐校、黄校本、李刊本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1146037_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年10月</a>　十月，在开封府为右散骑常侍，作重修《说文解字》序。作品：重修说文序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1145909' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145909' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145909?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重修说文序</a><span class='authorDate'>（雍熙三年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145909")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145909_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145909'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145909'>银青光禄大夫、守右散骑常侍、上柱国、东海县开国子、食邑五百户臣徐铉，奉直郎、守秘书省著作郎、直史馆臣句中正，翰林书学臣葛湍、臣王惟恭等，奉诏校定许慎《说文》十四篇，并《序目》一篇，凡万六百馀字，圣人之旨盖云备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145909_comment'></div>稽夫八卦既画，万象既分，则文字为之大辂，载籍为之六辔，先王教化所以行于百代，及物之功，与造化均，不可忽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145909_comment'></div>虽复五帝之后，改易殊体，六国之世，文字异形，然犹存篆籀之迹，不失<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1145909", 1145909, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>形类</span>之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145909_comment'></div>及暴秦苛政，散隶聿兴，便于末俗，人竞师法，古文既绝，讹伪日滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145909_comment'></div>至汉宣帝时，始命诸儒修仓颉之法，亦不能复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145909_comment'></div>故光武时马援上疏，论文字之讹谬，其言详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145909_comment'></div>及和帝时，申命贾逵修理旧文，于是许慎采史籀、李斯、扬雄之书，博访通人，考之于贾逵，作《说文解字》，至安帝十五年始奏上之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145909_comment'></div>而隶书行之已久，习之益工，加以行草、八分，纷然间出，返以篆籀为奇怪之迹，不复经心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145909_comment'></div>至于六籍旧文，相承传写，多求便俗，渐失本原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145909_comment'></div>《尔雅》所载草木鱼鸟之名，肆意增益，不可观矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145909_comment'></div>诸儒传释，亦非精究；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145909_comment'></div>小学之徒，莫能矫正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145909_comment'></div>唐大历中，李阳冰篆迹殊绝，独冠古今，自云「斯翁之后，直至小生」，此言为不妄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145909_comment'></div>于是刊定《说文》，修正笔法，学者师慕，篆籀中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145909_comment'></div>然颇排斥许氏，自为臆说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145909_comment'></div>夫以师心之见，破先儒之祖述，岂圣人之意乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145909_comment'></div>今之为字学者，亦多从阳冰之新义，所谓贵耳贱目也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145909_comment'></div>自唐末丧乱，经籍道息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145909_comment'></div>皇宋膺运，二圣继明，人文国典，粲然光被，兴崇学校，登进群才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145909_comment'></div>以为文字者六艺之本，固当率由古法，乃诏取许慎《说文解字》，精加详校，垂宪百代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145909_comment'></div>臣等愚陋，敢竭所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145909_comment'></div>盖篆书堙替，为日已久，凡传写《说文》者皆非其人，故错乱遗脱不可尽究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145909_comment'></div>今以集书正副本及群臣家藏者，备加详考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145909_comment'></div>有许慎注义、序例中所载而诸部不见者，审知漏落，悉从补录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145909_comment'></div>复有经典相承传写及时俗要用而《说文》不载者，承诏皆附益之，以广篆籀之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145909_comment'></div>亦皆形声相从，不违六书之义者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145909_comment'></div>其间《说文》具有正体而时俗讹变者，则具于注中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145909_comment'></div>其有义理乖舛，违戾六书者，并序列于后，俾夫学者无或致疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145909_comment'></div>大抵此书务援古以正今，不徇今而违古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145909_comment'></div>若乃高文大册，则宜以篆籀著之金石；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145909_comment'></div>至于常行简牍，则草隶足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1145909_comment'></div>又许慎注解，词简义奥，不可周知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1145909_comment'></div>阳冰之后，诸儒笺述，有可取者，亦从附益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1145909_comment'></div>犹有未尽，则臣等粗为训释，以成一家之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1145909_comment'></div>《说文》之时，未有反切，后人附益，互有异同，孙愐《唐韵》，行之已久，今并以孙愐音切为定，庶夫学者有所适从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1145909_comment'></div>食时而成，既异淮南之敏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1145909_comment'></div>县金于市，曾非吕氏之精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1145909_comment'></div>尘渎圣明，若临冰谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1145909_comment'></div>谨上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1145909_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年11月1日</a>　十一月一日，在开封府为右散骑常侍，奉表上新定《说文解字》三十卷，获赐银币，并受命点检国子监书写雕造。作品：上说文解字表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《说文解字》卷一五下。）</span><div id='poem_1145879' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145879' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145879?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上说文解字表</a><span class='authorDate'>（雍熙三年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145879")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145879_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145879'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145879'>银青光禄大夫、守右散骑常侍、上柱国、东海县开国子、食邑五百户臣徐铉等，伏奉圣旨，校定许慎《说文解字》一部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145879_comment'></div>伏以振发人文，兴崇古道，考遗编于鲁壁，缉蠹简于羽陵，载穆皇风，允符昌运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145879_comment'></div>伏惟应运统天睿文英武大圣至明广孝皇帝陛下，凝神系表，降鉴机先，圣靡不通，思无不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145879_comment'></div>以为经籍既正，宪章具明，非文字无以见圣人之心，非篆籀无以究文字之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145879_comment'></div>眷兹讹俗，深恻皇慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145879_comment'></div>爰命讨论，以垂程式，将惩宿弊，宜属通儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145879_comment'></div>臣等寔愧謏闻，猥承乏使，徒穷懵学，岂副宸谟！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145879_comment'></div>尘渎冕旒，冰炭交集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145879_comment'></div>其书十五卷，以编袟繁重，每卷各分上下，共三十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145879_comment'></div>谨诣东上閤门进上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145879_comment'></div>谨进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145879_comment'></div>雍熙三年十一月日翰林书学臣王惟恭、臣葛湍等状进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145879_comment'></div>奉直郎、守秘书省著作郎、直史馆臣句中正，银青光禄大夫、守右散骑常侍、上柱国、东海县开国子、食邑五百户臣徐铉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1145879_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1145879'><span class='label'>按：</span>《说文解字》卷一五下，中华书局一九六三年影印陈昌治同治刻本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1145879_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年12月3日</a>　十二月三日，在开封府为右散骑常侍，与修之《文苑英华》书成上奏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>　本年，在开封府为右散骑常侍，借校定《说文解字》之机，对弟徐锴所编《说文解字韵谱》加以增补更定。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>　本年，在开封府为右散骑常侍，为胡仲尧作洪州奉新县重建闿业观碑记。作品：洪州奉新县重建闿业观碑铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二六。）</span><div id='poem_1146015' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146015' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146015?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洪州奉新县重建闿业观碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146015")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146015_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146015'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146015'>道之为体也大，大则众无不容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146015_comment'></div>道之为用也柔，柔则物莫与校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146015_comment'></div>南方之强也，故冲气之所萃，异人之所生，坛馆之所宅，景福之所兴，相乎域中，南楚为盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146015_comment'></div>先圣之论，岂诬也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146015_comment'></div>洪州奉新县闿业观者，案方志，西晋邑人刘真君之故居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146015_comment'></div>真君名道诚，以经明行修，仕至刺史郡守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146015_comment'></div>金行不竞，仁兽非时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146015_comment'></div>知几之贤、有道之士，卷怀而退，修之于乡，玄德阴功，昭受灵贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146015_comment'></div>故真君辞张、邴之禄，追茅、许之风，单车还家，勤行不息，以永嘉二年八月十五日举族上升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146015_comment'></div>蔼尔福乡，依然旧址，锦帷乍降，玉舄长留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146015_comment'></div>后学瞻望，若仲尼之阙里；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146015_comment'></div>遗民思慕，如召伯之甘棠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146015_comment'></div>梁大同元年，乃建为观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146015_comment'></div>尔其豫章垂荫，洪井储灵，华林苍翠当其阳，冯水清泠环其域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146015_comment'></div>烟霞韬映，竹树青葱，居然人境之间，自是仙游之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146015_comment'></div>载祀四百，朝市三移，封域之间，英灵不泯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146015_comment'></div>鹿巾霞帔之士，往往冥升；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146015_comment'></div>缙绅逢掖之流，时时杰出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146015_comment'></div>存诸旧史，是号名区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146015_comment'></div>土德既微，群方构难，城有复隍之患，室多桡栋之凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146015_comment'></div>乃眷殊庭，俄悲阒户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146015_comment'></div>而琼蕴之所秘，霜钟之所悬，屹尔丽谯，俨然对峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146015_comment'></div>有道门都监余守徵者，剪除宿莽，草创精庐，苦节忘形，五十馀载，修心以化俗，传法以度人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146015_comment'></div>入室弟子龚绍元、吴绍甄，皆能肃奉真科，祇禀遗训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146015_comment'></div>惟乡人之善者，知岁计之有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146015_comment'></div>高士胡君名仲尧，延庆簪缨，息机丘壑，师黄、老之术以虚方寸，躬曾、闵之行以睦闺门，博施济众，斯谓<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>仁智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146015_comment'></div>以为集灵之馆，祈福之场，陋而不度，民将安仰？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146015_comment'></div>于是揆时属役，即旧谋新，询谋佥同，𧵥信咸萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146015_comment'></div>增湫下为爽垲，易卑室为崇构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146015_comment'></div>栋宇之设，则因夫故基；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146015_comment'></div>制度之中，则考于经法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1146015_comment'></div>凡殿堂门阙，居室厨廪，延袤周遍，殆且百区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1146015_comment'></div>三尊众真，羽仪侍卫，精严肃穆，不可为状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1146015_comment'></div>履端闱，造广庭，恍然如从汗漫之游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1146015_comment'></div>即瑶阶，瞻玉座，竦然若奉武夷之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1146015_comment'></div>既而息徒已事，日吉辰良，明祀以告成功，精意以答真祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1146015_comment'></div>举紫旄之节，摇太霄之佩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1146015_comment'></div>燃九华之烛，奏空洞之章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1146015_comment'></div>星斗回光，烟云改色，青天白日，夫岂远哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1146015_comment'></div>于时胡君以姻睦之行，慈惠之泽，里闾称举，郡国拜闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1146015_comment'></div>诏书褒美，特加旌表，揭以双阙，蠲其追胥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1146015_comment'></div>江楚之间，以为盛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1146015_comment'></div>是知玄风之被俗，圣政之化人，变鲁至道，见于今矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1146015_comment'></div>夫如是，则可以传芳金石，垂裕昆云，俾乎好道之徒，益励齐贤之志云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1146015_comment'></div>其铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1146015'>大道无名，得之为真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1146015_comment'></div>矫矫刘君，知几其神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1146015_comment'></div>逊尔侯社，上为帝宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1146015_comment'></div>维梓之地，甘棠之人，峙此仙祠，章江之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1146015_comment'></div>华表未归，桑田已改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1146015_comment'></div>旧井谁渫？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1146015_comment'></div>高台尚在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1146015_comment'></div>不见芝英，犹芳兰茝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1146015_comment'></div>佳气郁葱，如将有待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1146015_comment'></div>彼美胡君，州闾之英，世味道腴，家传义声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1146015_comment'></div>归诚玉阙，奉贽金籯，易此颓构，化为殊庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1146015_comment'></div>乃眷福乡，实惟南楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1146015_comment'></div>闲馆相望，飙轮交午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1146015_comment'></div>真图秘箓，唯仁是与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1146015_comment'></div>刻颂贞珉，永归终古<span class='inlineComment2'>（《徐公文集》卷二六。）</span>。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_1146015'></div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1146015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1146015'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_25_1146015_0'>⑴ 徐校、李校云：「『斯谓』下有脱字」。四库本有「仁」字，据补。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1146015_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>　本年，在开封府为右散骑常侍，为胡仲尧作胡氏书堂记。作品：洪州华山胡氏书堂记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二六。）</span><div id='poem_1145950' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145950' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145950?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洪州华山胡氏书堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145950")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145950_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145950'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145950'>士君子承积善之庆，服圣人之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145950_comment'></div>治身修心，义之本也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145950_comment'></div>风行于家，德之充也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145950_comment'></div>教被于俗，仁之周也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145950_comment'></div>畴克具举，吾其与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145950_comment'></div>豫章属邑，世云旧里，山水特秀，英灵所躔，安定胡君籍于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145950_comment'></div>君名仲尧，字光辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145950_comment'></div>奕叶儒学，蝉联簪绂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145950_comment'></div>曾门标举，焕列宿之华；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145950_comment'></div>祖德韬映，戢少微之耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145950_comment'></div>至于我先人，少好《左氏春秋》之学，研几索隐，儒者宗焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145950_comment'></div>及君之长，克扬其业，言斯出矣，身则践之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145950_comment'></div>揖让周旋之仪，孝友姻睦之行，修乎闺门之内，形于群从之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145950_comment'></div>少长有礼，丝麻同爨，乡党率义，人无间然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145950_comment'></div>君以为上古之风，可以驯致，由六经之旨，可以化成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145950_comment'></div>乃即别墅华林山阳玄秀峰下，构书堂焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145950_comment'></div>筑室百区，聚书五千卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145950_comment'></div>子弟及远方之士肄学者常数十人，岁时讨论，讲席无绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145950_comment'></div>又以为学者当存神閒旷之地，游目清虚之境，然后粹和内充，道德来应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145950_comment'></div>于是列植松竹，间以葩华，涌泉清池环流于其间，虚亭菌阁鼎峙于其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145950_comment'></div>处者无斁，游者忘归，兰亭石室，不能加也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145950_comment'></div>又案图牒云，昔陶丘公、李八百皆修道于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145950_comment'></div>是知人境相得，其道乃光，勤而行之，古犹今也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145950_comment'></div>铉钦羡其事，道阻且跻，故述斯文，以垂不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145950_comment'></div>年月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1145950_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>　约于本年春，在开封府为右散骑常侍，有诗和李仲㝢，并寄潘慎修。作品：和清源太保寄湖州潘郎中。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493661' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493661' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493661?labeling=true' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493661'>老大离群一倍愁，溪山风物且淹留。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493661'>酝成春酒谁斟酌，抄得新书自校雠。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>　约于本年秋，在开封府为右散骑常侍，有诗送人还乡。作品：送曾秀才。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_493717' class='_poem'><div
