原作涂，据四库本、备要本、徐本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_493717_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=986&endYear=986')">986年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为右散骑常侍，有诗和李从谦。作品：和复州李太保酬笔。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493675' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493675' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493675?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和复州李太保酬笔</a><span class='authorDate'>（986年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493675")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493675_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493675'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493675'>处处良工事笔锋，宣毫自昔最称雄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493675'>因思南国巾箱学，愿入兰台掌握中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493675'>委质幸归彫玉匣，操词曾侍兔园公<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本、备要本、徐本作宫）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493675'>一篇丽藻真閒暇，共仰才多道不穷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493675'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493675_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年1月2日</a>　正月二日，在开封府为右散骑常侍，奉和宋太宗《岁日诗》作品：奉和御制岁日诗二首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493638' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493638' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493638?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制岁日二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（987年1月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493638")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493638_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493638'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493638'>运历三元正，升平太古同。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493638'>五侯皆辑瑞，四海尽占风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493638'>圣政乾行内，群生寿域中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493638'>撞钟元会罢，晃<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>朗日升东。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493638'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493638_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_493638'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_493638_0'>⑴ 原作见，据四库本、备要本、徐本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_493638_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_493639' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493639' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493639?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（987年1月2日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493639_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493639'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493639'>正仗临轩万国来，汉仪周礼尽堪咍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493639'>光浮云盖青龙转，香透椒花白兽开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493639'>庆赐应时均亿兆，卜年从此数京垓。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493639'>群臣共感文明运，况是天言诫懋哉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493639'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493639_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年1月</a>　正月，在开封府为右散骑常侍，为陈文颢所刊徐锴《说文解字韵谱》作后序。作品：韵谱后序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1145911' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145911' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145911?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韵谱后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（987年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145911")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145911_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145911'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145911'>初，《韵谱》既成，广求馀本，孜孜雠校，颇有刊正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145911_comment'></div>今复承诏，校定《说文》，更与诸儒，精加研核，又得李舟所著《切韵》，殊有补益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145911_comment'></div>其间有《说文》不载，而见于序例、注义者，知必脱漏，并从编录；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145911_comment'></div>疑者，则以李氏《切韵》为正，殆无遗矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145911_comment'></div>前序犹谓学者殊寡，而今之学者益多，家蓄数本，不足以供其求借。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145911_comment'></div>颍川陈君文颢，任当守土，宠列侍祠，习武好文，怜才乐善，见人为学，如己之诲子弟焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145911_comment'></div>因取此书，刊于尺牍，使摸印流行，比之缮写，省功百倍矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145911_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145911_comment'></div>仁人之用心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145911_comment'></div>因躬自篆籀，庶祗来命，序之于后，以记其由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145911_comment'></div>雍熙四年正月序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1145911_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年8月14日</a>　八月十四日，在开封府为右散骑常侍，奉和宋太宗《殿前松》诗。作品：奉和御制殿前松兼以书事。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493645' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493645' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493645?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制殿前松兼以书事</a><span class='authorDate'>（987年8月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493645")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493645_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493645'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493645'>长松修干列承明，虎盼龙盘气貌灵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493645'>风度乍闻琴曲调，巢高初见鹤仪形。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493645'>枝笼陛戟寒生槛，叶带炉烟翠满庭。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493645'>涧底山头各生殖，托根争似在青冥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493645_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493645'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493645_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年8月14日</a>　八月十四日，在开封府为右散骑常侍，奉和宋太宗《烟》诗。作品：奉和御制烟。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493641' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493641' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493641?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和御制烟</a><span class='authorDate'>（987年8月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493641")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493641_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493641'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493641'>春晴纤霭映斜阳，羃羃偏能覆水乡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493641'>浓似庆云同馥郁，薄如轻素自飞扬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493641'>堤横新柳真成画，楼对遥山正好望。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493641'>谁见朝元香案上，龙旂交影共腾骧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493641'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493641_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年10月</a>　十月，在开封府为右散骑常侍，为李从善作墓志铭。作品：大宋右千牛卫上将军陇西郡公李公墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1146026' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146026' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146026?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋右千牛卫上将军陇西郡公李公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（987年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146026")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146026_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146026'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146026'>公讳从善，字子师，陇西成纪人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146026_comment'></div>唐室之诸孙，元和之近属，谱谍详悉，此不具陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146026_comment'></div>若夫天祚之德，大运有时而极；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146026_comment'></div>积庆之祀，百世无得而逾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146026_comment'></div>必生克肖之贤，以承有后之应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146026_comment'></div>保姓受氏，公实宜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146026_comment'></div>昔者土德既微，群雄角立，维我显祖，奄宅旧吴，延祚四纪，传国三世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146026_comment'></div>公以天属之爱，膺宝玉之封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146026_comment'></div>始在胶庠，已有名望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146026_comment'></div>姿仪秀出，文学生知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146026_comment'></div>仁孝极于事君，谦揖形于下士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146026_comment'></div>中外之论，翕然称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146026_comment'></div>由是受任六官，交修庶职，弥纶旧典，咨访老成，恪居无违，所至皆理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146026_comment'></div>于时圣人出于中土，正朔及于四方，维我先君，祗畏天命，受盟请吏，息民弭兵，玉帛交驰，冠盖相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146026_comment'></div>公亲则介弟，位则中台，独奉丝纶，留参槐棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146026_comment'></div>元戎驷牡，分建节之权；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146026_comment'></div>玄冕九章，奉侍祠之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146026_comment'></div>朝奖既厚，臣诚益恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146026_comment'></div>后凋之叶无渝，万顷之陂自若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146026_comment'></div>故得全名节于危疑之际，保恩顾于终始之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146026_comment'></div>环卫迭迁，寄任增重，盘根必解，师律以真，十有馀年，其志如一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146026_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146026_comment'></div>修涂方骋，景命不融，春秋四十有八，雍熙四年秋九月，薨于通许护军之廨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146026_comment'></div>诏辍朝一日，赙绢百匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146026_comment'></div>即其年冬十月十三日葬于开封府开封县吹台乡苏里，祔太夫人凌氏之茔，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146026_comment'></div>前夫人徐氏，继室周氏，并早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146026_comment'></div>皆有肃雍之德，窈窕之华，宜家治内尽其规，鱼轩象服昭其盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146026_comment'></div>子十四人：仲顗、仲翊、仲衍、仲华、仲雅、仲颖、仲宁、仲简、仲彬、仲文、仲猷、仲玄、仲义、仲端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146026_comment'></div>女十四人：慕英、懿卿、奉蘋、蕴兰、正容、茂节、稚仙、惠昭、如宾、道崇、凤兆、幼贞、闺秀、秀真，或嫔于盛族，或待礼未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146026_comment'></div>惟公生于深宫，特禀异气，谦而得礼，和而执中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146026_comment'></div>容纳直言，宾延素士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1146026_comment'></div>经历夷险，雅度不渝，大年未登，终古同叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1146026_comment'></div>铉登门斯久，辱顾殊深，永惟知己之恩，愿表为陵之谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1146026_comment'></div>其铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1146026'>真源引派，仙李垂芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1146026_comment'></div>实生我公，金玉其相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1146026_comment'></div>非礼勿动，出言有章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1146026_comment'></div>忠信以济，终然允臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1146026_comment'></div>三代之姓，倏焉为庶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1146026_comment'></div>九万之程，溘然中路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1146026_comment'></div>吹台北峙，浚川东注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1146026_comment'></div>不植刺草，长瞻宰树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1146026_comment'></div>大雅君子，陇西公之墓。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1146026_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年</a>　约于本年三月十七日，在开封府为右散骑常侍，奉和宋太宗《赏花》诗。作品：应制赏花。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493650' "poem_title_493650")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493650_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493650'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493650'>上林春暮紫英开，组绣成帷荫玉阶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493650'>艳逐晨光随步武，香和轻翠<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>透襟怀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493650'>生成泽广时芳茂，鱼水情通乐韵<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作咏）</span>谐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493650'>禁篽年年陪睿赏，何时梁甫奉燔柴。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493650_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
