四库本、备要本、徐本作吹</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_493650_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年</a>　约于本年冬，在开封府为右散骑常侍，有诗送郑文宝出任梓州录事参军。作品：送修武郑主簿纠郡梓潼兼寄王舍人八韵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_493727' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493727' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493727?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送修武郑主簿纠郡梓潼兼寄王舍人八韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（987年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493727")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_493727_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493727'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493727'>杖策辞清浴<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作洛）</span>，驱车向梓潼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493727'>栖鸾才乍展，叱驭气方雄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493727'>暂割趋庭恋，将伸纠郡功。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493727'>诗清冲密雪，别酒愬寒风。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493727'>山水秦关外，烟花锦里东。<div id='poem_sentence_4_493727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_493727'>府公名素重，语掾道仍同。<div id='poem_sentence_5_493727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_493727'>坐啸新知洽，随行旧分通。<div id='poem_sentence_6_493727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_493727'>当令从此去，不复数文翁。<div id='poem_sentence_7_493727_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_493727'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_493727_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为右散骑常侍，称誉夏侯嘉贞所作《洞庭赋》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=987&endYear=987')">987年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为右散骑常侍，有诗送慎知礼解官侍亲。作品：送慎大卿解官侍亲。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_493701' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493701' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493701?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送慎大卿解官侍亲</a><span class='authorDate'>（987年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493701")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493701_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493701'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493701'>圣朝无事九卿閒，蔼蔼东门䌽服还。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493701'>旧日高名齐汲郑，今朝至行似曾颜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493701'>更怜霜<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>鬓垂玄发，犹恨深居远旧山。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493701'>老鹤乘轩真自愧，徘徊空在稻粱间。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493701'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_493701'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_493701_0'>⑴ 备要本、徐本作双</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_493701_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年1月</a>　正月，在开封府为右散骑常侍，为李巨源之父作墓志。作品：大宋故陈留县主簿赠太子中允李府君墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1146030' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146030' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146030?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋故陈留县主簿赠太子中允李府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146030")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146030_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146030'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146030'>府君讳某，字广途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146030_comment'></div>其先陇西狄道人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146030_comment'></div>仙源帝系，蕃衍万邦，陇西一族，独为鼎甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146030_comment'></div>中叶从官，因家雍丘，今为县人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146030_comment'></div>曾祖巢、祖礼，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146030_comment'></div>考洪，蔡州长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146030_comment'></div>府君清明禀气，才智夙成，幼而属文，已洽时誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146030_comment'></div>既志学，通《左氏春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146030_comment'></div>未冠，即为讲说，横经请益，虚往实归，微言奥义，别为编录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146030_comment'></div>年二十三，举进士再不中第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146030_comment'></div>后唐天成初，宗人璩为大宗正，见而器之，曰：「王室多故，吾道未光，得禄而已，何必是也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146030_comment'></div>乃表为属吏，委以笺奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146030_comment'></div>丞相郑公珏，奇君之能，特除蔡州汝阳主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146030_comment'></div>奏课连最，改冀州南宫主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146030_comment'></div>于时期运告谢，河朔多虞，君内抚疲羸，外给军旅，民安事集，郡国称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146030_comment'></div>泽潞节度、侍中马公存节闻其名，辟为管记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146030_comment'></div>荐章连上，制命弗临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146030_comment'></div>君知命之不遭，乃谢病而退，闭门却扫，以名教自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146030_comment'></div>汉氏初基，群心改属，亲友敦喻，复诣京师，直道而行，焉往无吝，又为兴平、河东二主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146030_comment'></div>秩满，以常调当迁望令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146030_comment'></div>时皇运肇启，多士徇名，君之次子巨源已从乡荐，获知于尚书陶公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146030_comment'></div>公时典选事，谓曰：「丈人才高运否，邅回下位，区区一宰，未足为光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146030_comment'></div>孰若复佐近畿，以便吾子之举事，不亦可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146030_comment'></div>乃除陈留主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146030_comment'></div>乾德六年春三月四日，终于县署，享年六十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146030_comment'></div>夫人追封琅耶郡太君王氏，缑山仙派，河洲懿德，妇道以顺，家人用严，睦族惟和，训子由义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146030_comment'></div>以乾德三年月日先逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146030_comment'></div>俱权殡于县之乾明寺，至雍熙五年二月日，合葬于开封府开封县吹台乡苏村，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146030_comment'></div>子五人：长巨舟，早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146030_comment'></div>次巨源，擢进士第，今为都官郎中、盐铁副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146030_comment'></div>次巨载，以疾家居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1146030_comment'></div>次巨川、巨卿及二女皆早夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1146030_comment'></div>惟君怀恬淡之性，秉贞介之规，孝于奉亲，仁以睦俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1146030_comment'></div>雅志宗道，馀力攻文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1146030_comment'></div>有孔、墨之志，无管、乐之遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1146030_comment'></div>淹翔末路，从容自若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1146030_comment'></div>所至之处，辄构茅斋，延高士，谈宴终日，曾无倦容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1146030_comment'></div>尝谓诸子曰：「吾志在大名，非欲夸世，欲行吾道尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1146030_comment'></div>时命不偶，古则皆然，汝辈宜勉成吾志也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1146030_comment'></div>而巨源果能奋奇藻，捷高科，际会圣明，骞翔台阁，长才利刃，应用忘疲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1146030_comment'></div>追远之泽漏于泉，卜宅之仪由乎礼，积善之家斯在，大名之应何惭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1146030_comment'></div>仁人孝子，正当如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1146030_comment'></div>铉向风斯久，倾盖甚欢，不朽之文，惠然见托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1146030_comment'></div>贤贤善善，翰墨之任也，故采家牒，勒于贞珉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1146030_comment'></div>其词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1146030'>才高位下，古实有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1146030_comment'></div>积善馀庆，神宁舍旃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1146030_comment'></div>邈哉李君，一时之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1146030_comment'></div>其身则屈，其道斯全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1146030_comment'></div>馀庆伊何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1146030_comment'></div>实有令子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1146030_comment'></div>奉之以孝，葬之以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1146030_comment'></div>蜃辂同载，佳城双启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1146030_comment'></div>九原与归，三庙而祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1146030_comment'></div>遗爱被俗，没而不亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1146030_comment'></div>贞珉颂美，久而弥芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1146030_comment'></div>阡如京兆，地即桐乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1146030_comment'></div>绵绵瓜瓞，永永流光。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1146030_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年2月26日</a>　二月二十六日，在开封府为右散骑常侍，改官左散骑常侍。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年4月5日</a>　四月五日，在开封府为左散骑常侍，为人作文集序。作品：进士廖生集序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1145916' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145916' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145916?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进士廖生集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年4月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145916")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145916_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145916'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145916'>端拱改元岁，春官庀职，俊造毕集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145916_comment'></div>有廖生者，惠然及门，以文十五轴为贽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145916_comment'></div>观之则博赡渊奥，清新相接，其名理则师荀、孟之流，其文词则得四杰之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145916_comment'></div>问其年，则既冠矣，覆篑之功，往而未止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145916_comment'></div>询其爵里，则闽方茂族，组绶奕叶，善庆之所及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145916_comment'></div>他日与之语，则风骨清粹，识度淹雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145916_comment'></div>咸以为远大之程，可企而致，不幸遇暴疾，数日，夭于逆旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145916_comment'></div>士君子知与不知，莫不为之悲叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145916_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145916_comment'></div>以生之词藻俊秀，盖天假之也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145916_comment'></div>而促龄早世，又天夺之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145916_comment'></div>然则神理玄邈，圣人犹复不论，余当何言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145916_comment'></div>会其友生采其遗文，著于编简，因为之序，以示方来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145916_comment'></div>夏四月辛卯，左散骑常侍徐铉述。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1145916_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年9月</a>　九月，在开封府为左散骑常侍，为人作诗集序。作品：邓生诗序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1145915' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145915' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145915?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邓生诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145915")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145915_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145915'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145915'>古人云：诗者，志之所之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145915_comment'></div>故君子有志于道，无位于时，不得伸于事业，乃发而为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1145915", 1145915, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>诗咏</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145915_comment'></div>南阳邓君，少而从吏，服勤靡盬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145915_comment'></div>时命不偶，淹翔末涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145915_comment'></div>养心浩然，不以为慊，遇事造景，辄以吟咏自怡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145915_comment'></div>悔吝不及，终始无累，至于皓首，未见愠容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145915_comment'></div>家贫晏然，惟诗稿盈箧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145915_comment'></div>太原王君、武陵龚君，好文乐善，皆序而伸之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145915_comment'></div>愚亦与君有姻，故复为之述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145915_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145915_comment'></div>士君子乐道自娱，贞节没齿，斯可矣，悠悠世利，曾何足云！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145915_comment'></div>子其勖之，无易尔守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145915_comment'></div>丙子岁秋九月，左散骑常侍徐铉述。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1145915_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年12月</a>　十二月，在开封府为左散骑常侍，为李至之父作墓志铭。作品：大宋故处士赠太子少师李公墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1146027' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146027' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146027?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋故处士赠太子少师李公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146027")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146027_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146027'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146027'>道之泰也，贤人振衣而济物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146027_comment'></div>时之否也，君子括囊以独善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146027_comment'></div>其有修之家而孚教于俗，无其位而博施于人，角立杰出，盖亦难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146027_comment'></div>公讳某，字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146027_comment'></div>庭坚迈德，百世流光，源长派远，蕃衍郡国，今为常山真定人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146027_comment'></div>祖某，赠太子少保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146027_comment'></div>考某，赠太子少傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146027_comment'></div>公即少傅第三子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146027_comment'></div>幼而岐嶷，长而纯孝，承颜先意，实禀生知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146027_comment'></div>七岁丁太夫人忧，泣血绝浆，殆于毁灭，宗族惊异，谓之神童。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146027_comment'></div>事兄弟，人莫能间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146027_comment'></div>先是，唐之叔世，燕、赵多虞，故我先人，累世贞遁，公亦奉家法，咸乐丘园，躬耕敦本，俭以足用，百年之业，是享素封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146027_comment'></div>既而天下兵兴，生民益否，公尽出私积，以均有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146027_comment'></div>为食以救饥歉，微嗟来之诮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146027_comment'></div>焚券以赒乏绝，非市义之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146027_comment'></div>远迩之人，全济甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146027_comment'></div>怀仁向义者，抚之既无矜色；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146027_comment'></div>背惠弃信者，接之亦无愠容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146027_comment'></div>襟怀旷然，莫窥其际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146027_comment'></div>慈爱恻隐，视人如伤，昆虫草木，无所夭阏，故闾里率化，风俗以和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146027_comment'></div>崇儒尊道，坟籍未尝释手；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146027_comment'></div>喜酒好客，醒醉必与之同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146027_comment'></div>常以为芳华易凋，光阴不驻，发于吟咏，以寄其情，黎杖角巾，所至皆适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146027_comment'></div>是非扰扰，若蚊虻之过前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146027_comment'></div>愚智憧憧，若蜾裸之在侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146027_comment'></div>至矣哉，古之达者也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146027_comment'></div>开运末，有晋失御，猃狁孔棘，公挈家南度，居于胙城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146027_comment'></div>伯氏飞龙，府君时在荥阳，召公同处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146027_comment'></div>广顺三年夏六月日，终于郑州私第，享年四十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146027_comment'></div>夫人清和郡太夫人张氏，以谢女之淑德，徇莱妻之高节，宜家理内，令问蔼然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146027_comment'></div>威姑性严，诸妇皆耸，夫人顺而得礼，勤而无怨，晨夕参侍，独被深慈，凡饮食药饵，须经夫人之手，然后即御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1146027_comment'></div>长姒亦颇严厉，夫人事之如姑，或被诮责，怡声致拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1146027_comment'></div>由是闺门之内，不肃而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1146027_comment'></div>及罹恭姜之哀，更全孟母之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1146027_comment'></div>诸孤稍长，教以学文，为之择师友，为之致经籍，凡学舍宾馆之所须者，辍衣食、捐簪珥以奉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1146027_comment'></div>躬截发之惠，俾其亲仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1146027_comment'></div>引断织之言，诫其中废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1146027_comment'></div>故诸子皆立，门户如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1146027_comment'></div>越建隆二年秋七月十日，终于郑州私第，享年四十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1146027_comment'></div>长子格，大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1146027_comment'></div>次子至，吏部侍郎兼秘书监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1146027_comment'></div>吏部以文学冠时，擢高第于圣鉴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1146027_comment'></div>以才业膺世，参大政于中枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1146027_comment'></div>以疾告罢，复为少宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1146027_comment'></div>天子秘御书于中禁，命我专掌，式恢文教，时人荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1146027_comment'></div>先是，少师之葬也，世犹多故，礼或有阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1146027_comment'></div>及夫人祔也，茔地逼隘，介于群冢之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1146027_comment'></div>君子曰：非安神之宅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1146027_comment'></div>即以端拱元年冬十二月十三日，改卜于郑州管城县某乡里原，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1146027_comment'></div>铉乡里辽夐，声尘致睽，朅来京师，获与吏部游处，睹于公高门之盛，知臧孙有后之由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1146027_comment'></div>公之行实，皆闻于舆论，或得于家老，梗概而已，不能备举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1146027_comment'></div>金石之纪，宜在鸿儒，惠然见顾，辞不获命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1146027_comment'></div>谨为铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_1146027'>天生贤人，以佑生民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1146027_comment'></div>生民数奇，贤人隐沦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1146027_comment'></div>修之于家，富以其邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1146027_comment'></div>里闾率化，宗族归仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1146027_comment'></div>乐天知命，全和保真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1146027_comment'></div>凤皇于飞，以况嘉耦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1146027_comment'></div>伯鸾之妻，士行之母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1146027_comment'></div>婉淑宜家，严慈启后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1146027_comment'></div>金钩鹊印，鱼轩紫绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1146027_comment'></div>令问无已，流光不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1146027_comment'></div>刻此贞珉，高深共久。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1146027_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在开封府为左散骑常侍，因议安崇绪讼继母案不当，被罚俸一月。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　本年，在开封府为左散骑常侍，有诗送陈文颢出知同州。作品：送陈使君之同州。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_493752' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493752' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493752?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送陈使君之同州</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493752")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493752_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493752'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493752'>太守驱征旆，翩翩西过关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493752_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493752'>冰容先腊至，膏雨逐春还。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493752_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493752'>绿树游沙苑，高楼看华山。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493752_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493752'>从来京辅地，出入尽崇班。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493752_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493752'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493752_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=988&endYear=988')">988年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为左散骑常侍，为樊知古之父作神道碑。作品：故唐大理司直鄂州汉阳令赠卫尉少卿樊公神道碑。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1146022' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146022' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146022?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故唐大理司直鄂州汉阳令赠卫尉少卿樊公神道碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（988年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146022")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146022_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146022'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146022'>公讳潜，字仲明，京兆万年人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146022_comment'></div>昔者虞仲垂孙谋之庆，肇启我封；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146022_comment'></div>山甫昭补职之勤，实大吾族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146022_comment'></div>或则游圣门而称达者，或则冠仙籍而号真人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146022_comment'></div>丰沛功臣，经营于大业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146022_comment'></div>南阳外戚，佐佑于中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146022_comment'></div>传祀百世，流光万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146022_comment'></div>而我之占籍，世茂西京，樊川之居，抗衡韦、杜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146022_comment'></div>曾祖澄，以七世同爨，孝德升闻，大中制恩，特加旌表，峨峨石阙，至今存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146022_comment'></div>祖称，濮州司户参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146022_comment'></div>考谕，光化中补池州至德令，时天下已乱，因家池阳，终润州金坛令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146022_comment'></div>公中和禀粹，形器夙成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146022_comment'></div>好学之勤，本由天赋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146022_comment'></div>至孝之性，不坠家声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146022_comment'></div>始及弱冠，并违怙恃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146022_comment'></div>绝浆泣血，哀感州闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146022_comment'></div>负土成坟，终丧庐墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146022_comment'></div>言子道者，以为美谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146022_comment'></div>于时唐祚沦胥，宗室称制，江淮之地，不失旧章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146022_comment'></div>公以射策高等，补润州丹阳尉，试吏之课，书考为优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146022_comment'></div>庐陵之民，古称多讼，加以亩籍违制，乱狱滋丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146022_comment'></div>守臣上言，求拯其弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146022_comment'></div>有命择堪其事者，闻公之能，因而命之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146022_comment'></div>公既至，乃相五土之沃瘠，察夫家之众寡，采古之制，酌今之宜，创为新规，众皆悦服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146022_comment'></div>而复出械系之者，穷两造之辞，雪当死者数十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146022_comment'></div>使还议赏，增秩进等，迁寿州寿春县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146022_comment'></div>既而庐陵之政日理，南楚之人耸观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146022_comment'></div>久之，以公为光州光山县令，加大理评事，犹以前效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146022_comment'></div>于时南北分裂，县临敌境，有争桑之女，多探丸之吏，比闾之众，罕尝宁居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146022_comment'></div>公于是纠集义勇，分守要害，推以恩信，济之强明，三载之中，一邑用乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146022_comment'></div>迁池州石埭令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1146022_comment'></div>县有大姓，侵挠细民，岁比不登，俗乃重困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1146022_comment'></div>公绳之以法，董之以威，豪右震悚，相与逃匿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1146022_comment'></div>于是启请出官粟以赈乏，绝省力役，以济农功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1146022_comment'></div>慈抚仁薰，视之如子，岁丰俗阜，政用大成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1146022_comment'></div>就加大理司直，旌能政也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1146022_comment'></div>秩满，迁鄂州汉阳令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1146022_comment'></div>未几遇疾，壬子岁某月日，终于县之正寝，享年五十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1146022_comment'></div>以丙辰岁某月日葬于池州贵池县永泰乡保静里之原，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1146022_comment'></div>夫人王氏，鸿胪卿滔之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1146022_comment'></div>轩冕之族，闺房之秀，室家垂训，惠问风行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1146022_comment'></div>长子若讷，不事王侯，自全高尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1146022_comment'></div>次子知古，才艺毕给，际会昌朝，践历台省，交修繁剧，今为右谏议大夫、河北转运使，扬名之业方茂，显亲之数遂优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1146022_comment'></div>公累赠秘书丞、户部员外郎、卫尉少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1146022_comment'></div>夫人封琅耶县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1146022_comment'></div>惟公生而岐嶷，长而学问，穷九经之奥旨，综百氏之微言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1146022_comment'></div>率是古道，施于为政，行之以直，守之以廉，事亲以孝，饰躬以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1146022_comment'></div>士元之器，命屈于生前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1146022_comment'></div>臧孙之忠，庆贻于身后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1146022_comment'></div>君恩饰壤，世禄传家，咸京之旧表未堙，秋浦之丰碑复立，俗有遗爱，吾无愧辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1146022_comment'></div>其铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_1146022'>南山崇崇，樊川溶溶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1146022_comment'></div>剪商之烈，补衮之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1146022_comment'></div>百代之后，流光不穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1146022_comment'></div>爰有孝德，克生我公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1146022_comment'></div>猗欤我公，显允君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1146022_comment'></div>投此利刃，行于百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1146022_comment'></div>有惠于民，何必贵仕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1146022_comment'></div>垂庆于后，何必在己！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1146022_comment'></div>庆霄之泽，自叶流根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1146022_comment'></div>殁垂中佃，生驾鱼轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1146022_comment'></div>二子殊志，俱大吾门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1146022_comment'></div>僾僾愚谷，英英谏垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1146022_comment'></div>九峰之下，贵池之口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1146022_comment'></div>覆斧马鬣，金鸡玉狗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1146022_comment'></div>民即桐乡，碑如岘首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1146022_comment'></div>江水长流，令名同久。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_1146022'></div><div id='poem_sentence_65_1146022_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年2月1日</a>　二月一日，在开封府为左散骑常侍，为僧闰真作润州甘露寺新建舍利塔碑记。作品：润州甘露寺新建舍利塔记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1145956' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145956' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145956?labeling=true' target='_blank'>润州甘露寺新建舍利塔记</a><span class='authorDate'>（端拱二年二月一日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145956")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145956_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145956'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145956'>维皇宋二叶，改元五祀，润州丹徒县令王纪改筑县墙，掘地得石函，验其刻文，梁大同五年道人法序瘗真身舍利于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145956_comment'></div>函中铜龛一，龛中银合一，合中银瓶二，舍利七粒存焉，而铜龛复有刻文，则唐贞观十二年再加营奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145956_comment'></div>掌役者张遇获之以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145956_comment'></div>遇也感贞应之在己，念妙道之可修，因投郡之慈云寺，削发为沙门，易名闰真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145956_comment'></div>精心苦行，誓复前迹，广募众施，畴咨协心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145956_comment'></div>数年之间，克果其愿，即以端拱元年夏四月八日，迁致于郡之甘露寺东隅，建浮屠焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145956_comment'></div>献状而来，求志其绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145956_comment'></div>粤圣人在上，钦若灵心，政无不修，神靡不举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145956_comment'></div>玄贶交感，坤元效珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145956_comment'></div>用能使幽瘗之质，焕然景彰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145956_comment'></div>骞崩之迹，蔚然云构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145956_comment'></div>然则泽及微隐，福被含生，其可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145956_comment'></div>是郡也，扬州之都会，京口之重镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145956_comment'></div>六代之风流人物，综萃于斯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145956_comment'></div>三吴之山川林泉，肇发于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145956_comment'></div>高深自改，气象常存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145956_comment'></div>是寺也，北固山之阴崖、赞皇公之遗迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145956_comment'></div>峥嵘飞阁，回阚沧江；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145956_comment'></div>逦迤岩房，周行数里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145956_comment'></div>植□之作，远迩云臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145956_comment'></div>故真师因人之心，相地之胜，获此空隙，建兹崇封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145956_comment'></div>材用工役，必求善良；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145956_comment'></div>规模制度，必据经法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145956_comment'></div>其高七十尺，其周二十步，八隅莹玉，五盏凌霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145956_comment'></div>冠星珠于觚棱，海日先照；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145956_comment'></div>图云气于棼橑，宿雾常栖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145956_comment'></div>中严睟容，肃然月满；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145956_comment'></div>旁绩灵变，焕若霞舒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145956_comment'></div>游居之徒，莫不称叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145956_comment'></div>愚尝见释氏子为此役者多矣，如真师者，其涉道也浅，其居处也卑，上无许、史之托，下无猗、陶之助，苦节以感物，绩微而著功，不慁民，不愆素，而能事以立，亦可尚也，故嘉而志之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145956_comment'></div>端拱二年二月一日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1145956_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年4月</a>　四月，在开封府为左散骑常侍，作序送叶元辅还乡。作品：送叶元辅秀才序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1145899' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145899' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145899?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送叶元辅秀才序</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145899")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145899_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145899'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145899'>君子依仁据德，读书为文，孜孜于求己，汲汲于待问，盖将以行道济物，勤身存教，然而有不偶者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145899_comment'></div>人君侧席求贤，悬科取士，昧旦丕显，日旰忘食，盖将以尽一国之才，成天下之务，然而有所遗者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145899_comment'></div>此古人所谓离合之由运命之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145899_comment'></div>君子审其若此，故退而无闷，进而不矜，岂以无可奈之命，而挠不可夺之志？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145899_comment'></div>间者，愚及诸贤品第贡士于南宫，其间高等者，数年之中，登第略尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145899_comment'></div>今所遗者，唯叶生而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145899_comment'></div>「苟有良田，何忧晚岁」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145899_comment'></div>先后之间，其与几何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145899_comment'></div>行矣叶君，蘋洲若下，清风朗月，一时胜赏，矧复故乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145899_comment'></div>唯恐子青云之志，不得啸傲于其间尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145899_comment'></div>慎夏自爱，无假多谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145899_comment'></div>己丑岁孟夏序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1145899_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年6月</a>　六月，在开封府为左散骑常侍，为王祐文集作序。作品：故兵部侍郎王公集序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1145912' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145912' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145912?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故兵部侍郎王公集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145912")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145912_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145912'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145912'>君子之道，发于身而被于物，由于中而极于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145912_comment'></div>其所以行之者言也，行之所以远者文也，然则文之贵于世也尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145912_comment'></div>虽复古今异体，南北殊风，其要在乎敷王泽，达下情，不悖圣人之道，以成天下之务，如斯而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145912_comment'></div>至于格高气逸，词约义微，音韵调畅，华采繁缛，皆其馀力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145912_comment'></div>琅邪王公，负英俊之才，禀耿介之气，世济其美，为时而生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145912_comment'></div>遒文丽句，冠缙绅而杰出；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145912_comment'></div>纯诚直道，历夷险而安贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145912_comment'></div>故能奋厉羽仪，抑扬声实，振清芬于台阁，浃仁政于藩垣，润饰典谟，铨衡人物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145912_comment'></div>主恩时望，终始不渝，载籍所高，何以过此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145912_comment'></div>铉顷岁来自江左，会公西适三峰，客有以拙文示公者，大相知赏，击节而喜，曰：「此人必能知我」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145912_comment'></div>及召还京辇，惠然见寻，亦以旧文为贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145912_comment'></div>观其丽而有气，富而体要，学深而不僻，调律而不浮，寻既返覆，如四子复生矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145912_comment'></div>由是倾盖甚欢，恨相知之晚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145912_comment'></div>是时天子方阐文明之化，辟俊造之场，网罗群才，待以不次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145912_comment'></div>公则首冠纶阁，摽表朝伦，前达后进，莫不推仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145912_comment'></div>犹以为古道未尽复，己用未尽伸，每在谈宴，屡形词色，由是论者颇以躁竞为讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145912_comment'></div>愚以为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145912_comment'></div>夫古之君子，莫不汲汲于逢时，孜孜于救世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145912_comment'></div>汲长孺，汉之贤卿也，而有积薪之叹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145912_comment'></div>李令伯，晋之名臣也，而有中人之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145912_comment'></div>其有仰惮贵势，旁畏流议，缄词含意，从容自全者，不得已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145912_comment'></div>如公则内无隐情，外无饰貌，遇事辄发，胸中豁然，此真赵、魏意气之士，岂为儿女之态哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145912_comment'></div>上方注怀，而公寝疾，十旬既满，即卧内拜兵部侍郎，其恩礼如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145912_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145912_comment'></div>流运不停，仪表长谢，伯牙之弦已绝，延陵之剑徒悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145912_comment'></div>公平生所为文未尝编录，至是诸子缉缀断简，得二十卷，泣授故人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145912_comment'></div>铉也不才，无足延誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145912_comment'></div>善善恶恶，敢言褒贬之能！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145912_comment'></div>一死一生，粗达交朋之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145912_comment'></div>后之知我者，庶斯言之不诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145912_comment'></div>端拱二年夏六月序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1145912_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　本年，在开封府为左散骑常侍，为王克贞作墓志铭。作品：大宋故尚书户部郎中王君墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1146028' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146028' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146028?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋故尚书户部郎中王君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146028")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146028_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146028'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146028'>君讳克贞，字守节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146028_comment'></div>其先太原人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146028_comment'></div>缑山之胄，本固源长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146028_comment'></div>淮水既微，枝分派别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146028_comment'></div>所居占籍，吴楚为多，今为庐陵人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146028_comment'></div>曾祖某，不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146028_comment'></div>祖某，赠吉州别驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146028_comment'></div>考某，屯田郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146028_comment'></div>君弱不好弄，幼善属文，风骨峻整，器度闲雅，年未及冠，名闻于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146028_comment'></div>自唐室之季，词场道丧，江左延祚，复睹旧章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146028_comment'></div>翰林学士江君文蔚典司春官，详求艺实，取人至寡，较文尤精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146028_comment'></div>君一举擢第，首冠诸子，时人以为追踪元和之际矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146028_comment'></div>明年，以秘书省正字释褐，寓直枢近，专掌文翰之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146028_comment'></div>措词典雅，叙事详审，守位以慎，当官以勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146028_comment'></div>由是二十馀年，累迁至中书舍人、枢密副使，未尝他任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146028_comment'></div>求之前载，亦为异矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146028_comment'></div>及末叶多故，时政浸衰，唯吾守道中立，不涉浮议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146028_comment'></div>及宗国沦丧，策名天朝，自太子中允，历户部、兵部二员外郎，礼部、户部二郎中，典汉、滑、襄、梓四州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146028_comment'></div>皆以宽简为务，仁爱推诚，当时之不名臣仆，长孺之择任丞史，是故民以之睦，政以之修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146028_comment'></div>端拱二年秋，自梓潼还至京，九月十八日，遘疾终于兴州之传舍，享年六十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146028_comment'></div>明年某月日，葬于扬州某县乡里，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146028_comment'></div>夫人陇西县君李氏，早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146028_comment'></div>无子，女一人，许适盐铁使谏议陈某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146028_comment'></div>惟君有文雅之用，有周慎之诚，言行相顾，光尘不异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146028_comment'></div>奉职无废举，在私无惰容，历夷险而不回，保始终而无吝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146028_comment'></div>初，君始从乡荐，余已典纶诰，谬为先达，屡辱请益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146028_comment'></div>及余消长在运，而君金石不渝，古人之风，于是在矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146028_comment'></div>已悲深谷，更阅逝川，发为哀词，识彼泉户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146028_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1146028'>猗嗟夫君，心冥气纯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146028_comment'></div>英英达士，亹亹词臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146028_comment'></div>不愆于位，有惠于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1146028_comment'></div>无悔无咎，不缁不磷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1146028_comment'></div>吉往凶归，道悠运促。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1146028_comment'></div>旋自九折，复于左毂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1146028_comment'></div>驷马悲鸣，市人行哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1146028_comment'></div>邈矣彼苍，云何不淑！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1146028_comment'></div>悠悠邗水，隐隐昆冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1146028_comment'></div>慈亲临奠，令季持丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1146028_comment'></div>旁罗宰树，下閟玄堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1146028_comment'></div>郊原掩霭，云日冥茫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1146028_comment'></div>痛光尘兮永已，念兰菊兮徒芳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1146028_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　本年，在开封府为左散骑常侍，奉诏撰重修峨眉山普贤寺碑记。作品：大宋重修蛾眉山普贤寺碑铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1146011' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146011' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146011?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大宋重修蛾眉山普贤寺碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146011")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146011_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146011'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146011'>臣闻贤人阐化，必有胥附之资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146011_comment'></div>贤士膺期，必垂不朽之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146011_comment'></div>是以颜回默识，冠师门于洙泗之滨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146011_comment'></div>尹喜受经，应真气于崤函之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146011_comment'></div>故得千载之下，好学之徒，入其国而知其教，思其人而爱其树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146011_comment'></div>圣贤相遇，有如此焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146011_comment'></div>在昔像教权舆，能仁命世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146011_comment'></div>综百灵而贯群动，归向如流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146011_comment'></div>穷绝国而亘诸天，感通若响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146011_comment'></div>爰有法王之子，来从普胜之方，凭翼真乘，导扬宗极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146011_comment'></div>具大悲之愿行，综十智之因缘，从我立名，斯为上首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146011_comment'></div>及乎慈航既济，慧炬分华，乃暨众真，俱承佛敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146011_comment'></div>乘六牙之瑞兽，降右蜀之灵峰，将以协井络之会昌，镇金方之劲气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146011_comment'></div>犹且潜而勿用，明而未融，闇持摩顶之仁，阴骘含生之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146011_comment'></div>故使神婴青缕，肇建国都；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146011_comment'></div>路辟金牛，始通华夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146011_comment'></div>沉犀息沴，李太守之玄功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146011_comment'></div>噀酒救灾，栾尚书之妙用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146011_comment'></div>郡开学校，文翁广洽于儒风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146011_comment'></div>乐播《中和》，四子诞扬于帝德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146011_comment'></div>蔼尔褒斜之域，穆然周、汉之民，非法力之攸凭，岂人谋之独得？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146011_comment'></div>其后金人既应，白马斯来，神开显俗之徵，家识致诚之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146011_comment'></div>于是祥符焕烂，灵变纷纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146011_comment'></div>或则银色浮空，与朝阳而共丽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146011_comment'></div>或则灯光并列，将夜魄以俱明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146011_comment'></div>圣众盘旋，真容隐见，奇踪万状，不可胜图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146011_comment'></div>瞻之者耳目咸新，闻之者身心共肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146011_comment'></div>一方欣赖，历代修崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146011_comment'></div>遂于白水之源，特建普贤之寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146011_comment'></div>金土交运，开闭不常，白毫之相长存，法鼓之音靡绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146011_comment'></div>夫以导江遗迹，天汉名区，必有道之见归，岂三分之能久？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1146011_comment'></div>太祖神德皇帝，文修内禅，武定中区，正卿扬九伐之威，远俗致七旬之格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1146011_comment'></div>纳蜀王之土贡，受刘禅之骡车，重钮坤维，还铭剑阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1146011_comment'></div>于时王风初被，污俗尚繁，游魂篁竹之间，假息雈蒲之际，匪轻刑之可禁，顾先甲以徒勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1146011_comment'></div>金地宝坊，浸成薮泽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1146011_comment'></div>田衣毳褐，渐致流离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1146011_comment'></div>妖禽既就于焚巢，绀宇终悲于阒户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1146011_comment'></div>虽复葺其挠栋，缮彼垝垣，而陛序犹卑，基扃未广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1146011_comment'></div>尊号皇帝长君嗣统，二圣重熙，覆万物以如天，廓重昏而比日，聿修成业，钦若灵心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1146011_comment'></div>尺书徵怀德之君，折箠定畏威之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1146011_comment'></div>尽炎洲而极玄朔，尉候徒存；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1146011_comment'></div>亘日域而浃流沙，车书莫二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1146011_comment'></div>然后胜残去杀，反朴斲雕，包干戈以虎皮，铸剑戟为农器，定《大护》、《云门》之乐，举淹中、稷下之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1146011_comment'></div>慈卫仁薰，时和俗阜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1146011_comment'></div>天地应而庆云甘醴，律吕调而玉烛景风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1146011_comment'></div>犹复成而不居，勤则有继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1146011_comment'></div>一游一豫，表王度之惟常；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1146011_comment'></div>必躬必亲，示庶民之光圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1146011_comment'></div>虑极冰霜之诫，皇纲毕举，睿思弥精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1146011_comment'></div>以为象外微言，无生妙理，修于心则圆通无滞，被于物则福应来臻，足以助王道之和平，致苍生于仁寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1146011_comment'></div>乃申明诏，历选精庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1146011_comment'></div>唯此蛾<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作峨）</span>眉，独标殊胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1146011_comment'></div>天真人皇谕道之地，楚狂接舆隐景之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1146011_comment'></div>封域之间，气象盘薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1146011_comment'></div>洪源奔注，二江双流，沱潜之川；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1146011_comment'></div>峻岊回环，玉垒铜梁，岷嶓之阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1146011_comment'></div>况禅枝擢秀，来自祗园；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1146011_comment'></div>法海馀波，别疏定水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1146011_comment'></div>慈氏所相，畴能废之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1146011_comment'></div>烝哉圣谟，符此玄贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1146011_comment'></div>五年春，申命中使，率将杼人，伐贞石于它山，下瑰材于邃谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1146011_comment'></div>或子来而肆力，或神运以标奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1146011_comment'></div>模制度于鹫峰，极庄严于花界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1146011_comment'></div>耽耽正殿，䡾䡾飞甍，玉甃丹楹，金铺琐闼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1146011_comment'></div>洞户顺阴阳之候，中宸变寒暑之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1146011_comment'></div>揭以端闱，绕之周庑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1146011_comment'></div>铸鸿钟之万石，贯猛簴之千钧，桀孽凌空，铿訇震野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1146011_comment'></div>其后则层楼入汉，飞陛连云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1146011_comment'></div>彩槛离娄，冠馀霞而上出；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1146011_comment'></div>璇题玓瓅，缀列宿以旁回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1146011_comment'></div>神明之台不足以语其高，天梁之宫不足以矜其丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1146011_comment'></div>铄金为字，写大藏之经秘于上，逾五百函；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1146011_comment'></div>范铜为像，拟普贤之容设于下，高二十尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1146011_comment'></div>味其文，则如来之宗旨可得而观；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1146011_comment'></div>礼其相，则菩萨之威神于是乎在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1146011_comment'></div>将使三蜀之地，一切有情，皆冲气以含和，尽革凡而成圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1146011_comment'></div>则知大雄之教，渐于世也深焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1146011_comment'></div>元后之仁，利于民也至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1146011_comment'></div>昔者轩皇访道，历襄野以犹迷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1146011_comment'></div>汉帝祈年，拜竹宫而无得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1146011_comment'></div>恭惟盛美，允属皇猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1146011_comment'></div>若夫事以颂宣，言以文远，作而不记，后嗣何观？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1146011_comment'></div>爰命下臣，式旌不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1146011_comment'></div>其铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_83_1146011'>允矣象教，洪惟法王，如河不竭，比日同光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1146011_comment'></div>有情斯应，无远弗彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1146011_comment'></div>化自八国，声驰万方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1146011_comment'></div>爰有大贤，是称达者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1146011_comment'></div>异境齐致，同声协雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1146011_comment'></div>闻道莫逆，瞻颜不舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1146011_comment'></div>乃演真乘，来仪东夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1146011_comment'></div>蛾眉之阻，群帝之庭，作固作镇，栖真宅灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1146011_comment'></div>普贤至止，潜耀千龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1146011_comment'></div>尔未我觌，我畴尔形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1146011_comment'></div>经教既孚，神明乃作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1146011_comment'></div>瑞相显晦，圆光歘霍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1146011_comment'></div>万变凌峰，百灵溢壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1146011_comment'></div>信士归依，舆人骇愕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1146011_comment'></div>崇崇梵宇，于此宏开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1146011_comment'></div>时迁末运，数偶三灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1146011_comment'></div>焚如鲁庙，倾若齐台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1146011_comment'></div>淳风必复，圣日斯回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1146011_comment'></div>赫矣皇图，烝哉二圣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1146011_comment'></div>混一区宇，受天明命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1146011_comment'></div>与物皆春，得人为盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1146011_comment'></div>式叙九畴，迭修三正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1146011_comment'></div>皇帝曰咨，咨尔西人，助我神化，其惟正真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1146011_comment'></div>为尔祈福，转兹法轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1146011_comment'></div>禅林则旧，宝刹惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1146011_comment'></div>秘殿耽耽，高门奕奕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1146011_comment'></div>修廊四注，层楼百尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1146011_comment'></div>尊经圣像，金文宝质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1146011_comment'></div>妙善周园，福釐繁锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1146011_comment'></div>乾光俯烛，慧炬朝焞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1146011_comment'></div>同开寿域，共辟重昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1146011_comment'></div>䝙氓之伍，杜宇之魂，乘是妙果，俱登法门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1146011_comment'></div>明明大君，照临下土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1146011_comment'></div>坠典咸修，靡神不举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1146011_comment'></div>彼都人士，式歌且舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1146011_comment'></div>揭此丰碑，永传终古<span class='inlineComment2'>（《徐公文集》卷二五。）</span>。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_118_1146011'></div><div id='poem_sentence_118_1146011_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为左散骑常侍，有诗送曾会归宁。作品：送曾直馆归宁泉州。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_493699' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493699' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493699?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送曾直馆归宁泉州</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493699")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493699_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493699'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493699'>常怜客子倦征岐，谁似曾郎得意归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493699'>厅琐石渠封简册，手持仙<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作丹）</span>桂拜庭闱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493699'>舟横剑浦凌清濑，马过猿岩点翠微。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493699'>却笑辽东千岁鹤，下来空叹昔人非。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493699_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493699'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493699_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为左散骑常侍，有诗送乐史出知舒州。作品：送乐学士知舒州。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_493700' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493700' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493700?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送乐学<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>士知舒州</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493700")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_493700_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_493700_0'>① 原缺，据四库本、备要本、徐本补</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493700'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493700'>忆在同安郡，谁知是胜游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493700'>仙山常独往，骚客自忘忧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493700'>暂别经多难，劳生已白头。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493700'>羡君驱茜旆，兼得漱清流。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493700'>民俗常如古，风光最称秋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_493700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_493700'>短歌聊抒意，为我谢沙鸥。<div id='poem_sentence_5_493700_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_493700'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_493700_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为左散骑常侍，有诗寄乐史。作品：寄舒州乐学士。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_493703' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493703' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493703?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄舒州乐学士</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493703")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_493703_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493703'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493703'>皖伯台前绿树春，吴塘初下碧溪分。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493703'>旧游风景长牵梦，遥羡高斋望白云。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493703_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493703'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_493703_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为左散骑常侍，有诗送冯伉使蜀。作品：送冯中允使蜀。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_493748' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493748' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493748?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送冯中允使蜀</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493748")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493748_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493748'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493748'>莫笑皤然一病翁，百年交分两家同。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493748'>今朝倒屣迎王粲，旧日清谈赏阿戎。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493748'>玉垒无辞轺传送，金闺初喜姓名通。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493748'>青城山下逢仙客，为说心丹<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作丹心）</span>未辍功。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493748'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493748_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=989&endYear=989')">989年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为左散骑常侍，应僧鉴琮之请，为其师澄源禅师作碑铭。作品：洪州西山翠岩广化院故澄源禅师碑铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1146019' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146019' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146019?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洪州西山翠岩广化院故澄源禅师碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（989年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146019")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146019_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146019'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146019'>圣人设教，贤者学之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146019_comment'></div>有能极深研几，剖疑析滞，不背本以矫激，不沿波而流宕，世人宗仰，时君褒异，斯可以为君子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146019_comment'></div>禅师名无殷，姓吴氏，连江人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146019_comment'></div>昔泰伯获让，肇启南蕃，至德所及，流光百代，子孙蕃衍，吴越为多，至今为著姓焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146019_comment'></div>累世隐德，乡曲推重，道气钟粹，而生禅师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146019_comment'></div>幼异常童，不染俗态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146019_comment'></div>年七岁，从晋安雪峰真觉禅师出家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146019_comment'></div>二十，诣开元寺受度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146019_comment'></div>真觉之道，见重于时，禅师默识微言，尽得要旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146019_comment'></div>而复博考往行，幽寻胜迹，江浙诸郡，靡不经游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146019_comment'></div>先达推称，后生请益，结辙连袂，虚往实归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146019_comment'></div>禅师以道贵冲用，性复虚静，所止之处，学徒俯千人，辄复舍去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146019_comment'></div>晚岁止庐陵之禾山，其名益彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146019_comment'></div>季唐先主召见之，特加礼遇，俾居广陵之祥光院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146019_comment'></div>嗣君践祚，优礼有加，赐号澄源禅师，命移处豫章之上蓝，西山之翠岩院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146019_comment'></div>是皆都邑之胜概，高人之游集，自非密行淳德，不能镇服群情，我迭居之，绰有馀裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146019_comment'></div>虽身在岩谷，而恩注帷扆，存省问遗，使者相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146019_comment'></div>享寿七十有七，建隆元年春二月五日终于翠岩院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146019_comment'></div>甘露被树，数日不晞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146019_comment'></div>皓鹤盘空，三周而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146019_comment'></div>门弟子用西域之礼，葬于院之巽隅，封于其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146019_comment'></div>恩旨褒饰，名其丘曰大医。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146019_comment'></div>道俗孺慕，会其葬者万数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146019_comment'></div>铉也趋舍异术，声尘致睽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146019_comment'></div>于时释氏方盛，师门互启，尝侍嗣君宴语，从容上言曰：「古称千里一贤犹比肩也，今号长老者十数，无乃多乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146019_comment'></div>嗣君深以为善，因曰：「惟澄源禅师其殆庶矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146019_comment'></div>无几何，以家门情礼，请告至山，会师已没，瞻仰遗像，参迹行事，乃信名不虚得，亦表君之知臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146019_comment'></div>今来京都，复与师弟子鉴琮相遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146019_comment'></div>琮师志性端悫，修习精勤，肃奉成规，博总众艺，慈惠救物，时人称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146019_comment'></div>明诏赐号慧觉大师，锡以紫服，朝恩浃于累世，实教门之荣观也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146019_comment'></div>于时禅师委顺三十年矣，琮也思广铭颂，庶永遗风，以铉尝学旧史，见求直笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1146019_comment'></div>若夫褒善称伐，翰墨攸先，载瞻西山，实寄松槚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1146019_comment'></div>敢抽秘思，以告九原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1146019_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1146019'>芁芁东越，武夷之区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1146019_comment'></div>时生异人，与古为徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1146019_comment'></div>禅师出焉，俊迈且都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1146019_comment'></div>显显南楚，西山作镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1146019_comment'></div>真灵所宅，教法斯振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1146019_comment'></div>禅师居之，允矣令问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1146019_comment'></div>道无不在，法非可名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1146019_comment'></div>理超言象，俗仰风声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1146019_comment'></div>丰碑载勒，胜气长生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1146019_comment'></div>猗嗟来者，用此为程。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1146019_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年6月</a>　六月，在开封府为左散骑常侍，为道士聂紫庭作洪州始丰山兴玄观碑记。作品：洪州始丰山兴玄观记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1145953' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145953' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145953?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洪州始丰山兴玄观记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳化元年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145953")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145953_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145953'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145953'>圣人之言，道无不在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145953_comment'></div>若乃域中归其大，万物恃之生，鸿化玄造，无德而称已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145953_comment'></div>至于显神道之教，挺方外之朝，反之于身，以固其本，清心鍊气，保精啬神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145953_comment'></div>餐霞茹芝，修用者殊规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145953_comment'></div>御风乘景，游集者无方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145953_comment'></div>盖真阶仙品之有差，故洞天福地而区别，奇篇所纪，灵境可寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145953_comment'></div>豫章始丰山者，案图牒，第三十七之福地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145953_comment'></div>尔其穹窿蹇产，干霄蔽日，凌空瞰野之势；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145953_comment'></div>嵚崟窈窕，蒸云泄雨，储神宅怪之奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145953_comment'></div>阴林脩干，材用之所生也周；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145953_comment'></div>飞湍激流，利泽之所及者远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145953_comment'></div>紫烟白雾，隐映而纷霏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145953_comment'></div>灵风爽气，萧寥而披靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145953_comment'></div>醮享之数，历代相因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145953_comment'></div>爰有兴玄之观，是为荐诚之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145953_comment'></div>土德云季，三灾迭兴，市朝贸迁，堂构隳顿，几叹辽城之鹤，常栖楚幕之乌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145953_comment'></div>若夫真气所凭，神灵攸相，物无终否，道不远人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145953_comment'></div>道士聂紫庭，袭玉笥之地英，追九仙之夙契，以勤行为志业，以访古为师资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145953_comment'></div>岁在玄枵，来游此观，顾瞻祠宇，慷慨伤怀，徒侣敦请，遂膺其任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145953_comment'></div>积行所应，至诚易通，游居之人，莫不信奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145953_comment'></div>以为兴作者古人之所慎，因循者前哲之所宗，足备制度，何必侈大？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145953_comment'></div>于是补其阙而葺其坏，窒其隙而扶其倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145953_comment'></div>集瓴甋塼埴之工，加圬镘丹雘之饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145953_comment'></div>琐窗镂槛，朱户金铺，深沈靡迤，虚明藻丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145953_comment'></div>百年旧制，一旦维新；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145953_comment'></div>日就厥功，十稔而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145953_comment'></div>己不病于费，人不知其劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145953_comment'></div>用此修真，真其焉往？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145953_comment'></div>又以方志漏略，碑颂堙沉，使夫来者，何所宗仰？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145953_comment'></div>谓余为好道者，故求我以文，是用直书，以观成绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145953_comment'></div>淳化元年夏六月记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1145953_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年8月1日</a>　八月一日，在开封府为左散骑常侍，受李至之请，就秘阁观书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年</a>　本年，在开封府为左散骑常侍，奉诏与王禹偁、孔承恭校定《道藏经》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为左散骑常侍，有诗寄钱昱。作品：代书寄泗州钱侍郎。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_493702' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493702' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493702?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代书寄泗州钱侍郎</a><span class='authorDate'>（990年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493702")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_493702_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493702'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493702'>起部纡两绶，恢恢刃有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493702'>既为侍中郎，又复专城居。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493702'>无久恋铃阁，早应还直庐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493702'>浚川春水满，珍重寄双鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493702_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493702'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493702_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=990&endYear=990')">990年</a>　约于本年，在开封府为左散骑常侍，有诗送朱昂出知复州。作品：送秘阁朱员外知复州。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493682' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493682' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493682?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送秘阁朱员外知复州</a><span class='authorDate'>（990年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493682")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493682_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493682'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493682'>景陵山水旧知名，珍重诗人建隼行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493682'>未免簿书劳利刃，省贪烟月纵高情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493682'>扬雄阁下诸生送，陆羽门前百吏迎。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493682'>圣代群贤皆得路，三年倾首望鹏程。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493682_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493682'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493682_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=991&endYear=991')">991年1月</a>　正月，在开封府为左散骑常侍，为道士倪少通作墓碣。作品：洪州道正倪君碣。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1146024' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1146024' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1146024?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洪州道正倪君碣</a><span class='authorDate'>（991年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1146024")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1146024_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1146024'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1146024'>君讳少通，字子明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1146024_comment'></div>其先千乘人也，末叶避地，徙居巴陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1146024_comment'></div>濯洞庭之馀波，袭九嶷之秀气，儒风继世，贞节自持，垂庆炳灵，仙才是出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1146024_comment'></div>君风骨秀整，襟怀坦夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1146024_comment'></div>幼挺高情，即依道楗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1146024_comment'></div>弱冠遐举，来游九江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1146024_comment'></div>悦庐阜之名区，得董君之故静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1146024_comment'></div>种杏之地，榛莽森如，慨然永怀，誓复灵构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1146024_comment'></div>诛茅筑室，练行修身，闇然而彰，千里斯应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1146024_comment'></div>于时唐运告谢，宗室代兴，江左被玄元之风，二叶恢清净之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1146024_comment'></div>君以清心苦节，升闻于朝，癸丑岁赐钱三百万，即所居建太一之观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1146024_comment'></div>于是疏凿旧址，草创新规，悦以子来，成之勿亟，十有馀岁，清宫焕然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1146024_comment'></div>凡建四殿五堂，重门两序，内外栋宇，总百三十区，像设仪卫，莫不称是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1146024_comment'></div>力辟污莱为良田者五百亩，而饭贤之费有馀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1146024_comment'></div>手植杉松成茂林者千馀根，而甘露之祥再降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1146024_comment'></div>由是牧守嘉尚，道俗依凭，为本州道正，乃知太一观事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1146024_comment'></div>享寿九十有一，体力康壮，淳化元年秋八月八日子时，怡然而化，容貌如生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1146024_comment'></div>初，君自择葬地于莲花峰下，即以二年春正月窆焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1146024_comment'></div>君性质冲淡，不耀其光，表率教门，正身而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1146024_comment'></div>喜赋咏，善鼓琴，龙凤之形皆由手制，山水之操自洽天和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1146024_comment'></div>所居之观，俯迩城郭，登山之客，必先造焉，君将迎接待，高卑如一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1146024_comment'></div>绝迹朝市，咸乐林泉，六十馀年，慎终如始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1146024_comment'></div>门人弟子，先以慈孝为训，有若李延照、蒋守龙等，近四十馀人，皆以孝行为时所称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1146024_comment'></div>亲弟德规、同学弟谢又能等，叶力同心，共复灵迹，并先早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1146024_comment'></div>今谢君弟子王省昂嗣膺道任，师孙钱知素继知太一观事，师门之盛，论者美之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1146024_comment'></div>铉顷岁扈从南巡，与师款接旬日，倾盖之分，有如素交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1146024_comment'></div>钱君以论撰见求，不当为让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1146024_comment'></div>其铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1146024'>太一董君，上帝之宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1146024_comment'></div>遗方眇邈，旧迹荆榛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1146024_comment'></div>倪师慷慨，复来清尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1146024_comment'></div>种杏之地，林光再新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1146024_comment'></div>异世神交，岂其后身？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1146024_comment'></div>冥升自远，代剑非沦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1146024_comment'></div>瞻言华表，谁见千春？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1146024_comment'></div>刊铭翠琰，道契攸亲。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1146024_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=991&endYear=991')">991年</a>　春，在开封府为左散骑常侍，有诗和苏易简。作品：奉和武功学士舍人纪赠文懿大师净公。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493689' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493689' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493689?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和武功学士舍人纪赠文懿大师净公<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（991年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493689")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_493689_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493689'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493689'>旧国荒凉成黍稷，故交危脆似琉璃。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493689'>高人独喜汤师在，手把新文数道碑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493689_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493689'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_493689_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_493690' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493690' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493690?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（991年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_493690_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493690'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493690'>满卷文章为世重，出尘心迹少人同。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493690_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493690'>腾腾自得修真理，不管浮生觉梦中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493690_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493690'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_493690_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_493691' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493691' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493691?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（991年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_493691_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493691'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493691'>文似春华铺晓陌，思如泉涌注长江。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493691'>诗情<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_493691", 493691, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>道性</span>知无梦，频见残灯照曙窗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493691_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493691'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_493691_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_493692' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493692' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493692?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（991年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_493692_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493692'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493692'>已洁心源超<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>世表，却缘诗句有时名。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493692'>初闻行业如耆宿<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作旧）</span>，及见容颜是后生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493692'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_493692_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_493692'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_493692_0'>⑴ 原作起，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_493692_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_493693' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493693' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493693?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（991年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_493693_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493693'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493693'>只有閒情搜景物，不将客<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>鬓惜流光。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493693'>京华才子多文会，众许清词每擅场。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493693'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_493693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_493693'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_493693_0'>⑴ 四库本、备要本、徐本作容</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_493693_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_493694' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493694' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493694?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（991年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_493694_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493694'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493694'>惠远禅师名素重，维摩居士室皆空。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493694'>群公竞有诗相赠，组绣珠玑满袖中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493694_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493694'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_493694_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_493695' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493695' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493695?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（991年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_493695_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493695'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493695'>南朝人物古犹今，只恐前身是道林。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493695_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493695'>处处经行常自适，不妨谭笑不妨吟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493695_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493695'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_493695_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_493696' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493696' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493696?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（991年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_493696_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493696'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493696'>往往冥搜宵不寐，时时任性昼仍眠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493696'>高情丽句谁偏重，圣代词臣李谪仙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493696'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_493696_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_493697' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493697' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493697?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（991年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_493697_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493697'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493697'>霜髯病叟掩闲<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作柴）</span>扃，禅客相寻有故情。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493697'>每忆江南初识面，至今犹得爱才名。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493697_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493697'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_493697_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=991&endYear=991')">991年</a>　春，在开封府为左散骑常侍，有诗送人。作品：送文懿大师净公西游。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493688' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493688' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493688?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送文懿大师净公西游</a><span class='authorDate'>（991年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493688")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493688_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493688'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493688'>乘兴西游谁与同，一囊诗藁一枝筇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493688'>厌栖庐岳莲花社，却访南山紫阁峰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493688'>怀古有时应怅望，寻幽何处不从容。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493688'>关中风物常牵梦，老卧闲曹转放慵。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493688_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493688'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493688_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=991&endYear=991')">991年9月2日</a>　九月二日，在开封府为左散骑常侍，坐庐州尼道安之讼，免官，削一任，以检校工部尚书，出为静难军节度行军司马。<br /></div>
-----end
