-----title
临漳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d492ce37ca41453e9e801a7e36e9720b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d492ce37ca41453e9e801a7e36e9720b");'><span id='d492ce37ca41453e9e801a7e36e9720b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=979&endYear=979')">979年</a>，64岁</div><div id='d492ce37ca41453e9e801a7e36e9720b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=979&endYear=979')">979年7月</a>　七月，于邺都行在，有诗和刁衎。作品：邺都行在和刁秘书见寄。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《徐公文集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_493673' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_493673' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/493673?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邺都行在和刁秘书见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（979年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_493673")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_493673_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_493673'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_493673'>征袍结束从宸游，边上尘清见戍楼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_493673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_493673'>柏殿赋诗知是幸，茂陵多病自堪愁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_493673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_493673'>清漳幽咽长流恨，铜雀荒凉几换秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_493673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_493673'>深羡高眠全道气，姓名应已在丹丘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_493673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_493673'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_493673_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
彬县（新平）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='79ae4d80f6a44d8e87b8d196b8e2df83_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("79ae4d80f6a44d8e87b8d196b8e2df83");'><span id='79ae4d80f6a44d8e87b8d196b8e2df83_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=992&endYear=992')">992年</a>，77岁</div><div id='79ae4d80f6a44d8e87b8d196b8e2df83' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=992&endYear=992')">992年3月</a>　三月，在静难军节度行军司马任，作邠州定平县传灯禅院碑记。作品：邠州定平县传灯禅院记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《徐公文集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1145958' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1145958' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1145958?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邠州定平县传灯禅院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳化三年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 五代至宋初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(15869, "五代至宋初", "徐铉", "poem_title_1145958")'>徐铉</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1145958_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1145958'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1145958'>乾维巨屏，寔曰邠郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1145958_comment'></div>其地险固，其气刚劲，被宗周信厚之泽，咏王业艰难之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1145958_comment'></div>是故人知徼福之方，俗严慈氏之教，精庐静宇，隐辚相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1145958_comment'></div>定平县传灯禅院者，带位署之左方，据郭邑之胜势，四面环其趾，湮水荡其胸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1145958_comment'></div>却倚崇冈，爰标龙尾之号；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1145958_comment'></div>上写寒涧，仍有天河之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1145958_comment'></div>蔼尔鲜原，郁然佳气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1145958_comment'></div>昔居唐室之季，四海崩离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1145958_comment'></div>中和四年，有禅师从一者，挺秀宗门，从师临海，避难高举，择地遐征，万里而来，税驾于此，相其爽垲，有志盘桓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1145958_comment'></div>群心翕然，助成其事，买地筑室者咸集，横经跪履者亦臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1145958_comment'></div>十年之间，百堵斯建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1145958_comment'></div>守官嘉尚，请命于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1145958_comment'></div>景福二年，诏赐题署，天光所及，道誉弥高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1145958_comment'></div>一公化去，弟子佐范克嗣其业，范之弟子知信复继其任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1145958_comment'></div>守之以恪，加之以勤，感召益多，法事增广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1145958_comment'></div>殿堂像设，靡不庄严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1145958_comment'></div>储峙器用，无乏供亿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1145958_comment'></div>而经典犹阙，讲诵弗闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1145958_comment'></div>以为居今识古者存乎书，观象得意者存乎言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1145958_comment'></div>金匮石室之宏规，名山京师之故事，此而不务，何以为能？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1145958_comment'></div>乾德四年秋，肇启精诚，指期缮写。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1145958_comment'></div>邑人石迁等，闻风而悦，叶比其谋，日就月将，惟力是视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1145958_comment'></div>卷以缃帙，贮之琅函。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1145958_comment'></div>邑人高玘，奉其家山，以备构室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1145958_comment'></div>采伐未备，夫役未充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1145958_comment'></div>俄而暴雨猥至，山溜奔激，屹然巨石，自至院前，取以给用，宛契心匠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1145958_comment'></div>虽庐岳神运之殿，石头后渚之梁，感通冥符，无以过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1145958_comment'></div>既而信公复没，以属弟子令熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1145958_comment'></div>熙也遵行，弗敢失坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1145958_comment'></div>而民非兆万，俗空猗、陶，渐以化之，静以俟之，二十许年，犹未讫事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1145958_comment'></div>会中使王君名素，分榷筦之职，督关梁之征，归馀于终，率吁众力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1145958_comment'></div>于是简牍几阁，即日僝工，俾下帷凿壁者得肆其勤，研精索隐者不愆其义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1145958_comment'></div>真风无泯，介福来臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1145958_comment'></div>繄高士四世之勤，垂本宗百代之宪，宜其篆刻金石，永示方来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1145958_comment'></div>知余有好善之心，专旧史之学，求我以文，是用直书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1145958_comment'></div>于时岁次壬辰淳化三年春三月记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1145958_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=992&endYear=992')">992年</a>　本年，在静难军节度行军司马任，以隶书写《说文解字》，过数万言。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=992&endYear=992')">992年8月26日</a>　八月二十六日，在静难军节度行军司马任，卒于贬所。<br /></div>
-----end
